23215562|Revision of the genus Trichocline (Compositae). The genus Trichocline belongs to the family of the Compositae, tribe Mutisieae, and it includes 22 species, most of them from South America, and only one from Australia. In South America the genus is distributed in two geographical areas, both with the same number of species: the Andean area extending through Bolivia, Chile and W of Argentina and the south brazilian area extending through the south of Brazil, Paraguay, Uruguay and NE of Argentina. Three species grow in the northern or central part of Argentina. The genus is divided into three sections: Nervifolium, with one species, Amblysperma, with two species and Trichocline, with 19 species. The author considers that the most primitive section is Nervifolium, and in the section Trichocline which includes most of the species, the most primitive species are those which grow in the south brazilian area. The pollen of this genus has been studied and the chromosome number of three species has been determined. All the species are described and illustrated. The following new taxa or combinations are proposed: Trichocline spathulata (Phil.) nov. comb., Trichocline auriculata var. breviscapa nov. var., Chaptalia denticulata (Bak.) nov. comb., and Chaptalia martii (Bak.) nov. comb. A number of synonyms is proposed, all of them based on the study of the respective nomenclatural types.
23222536|A new species of Caesalpinia (Leguminosae) from Peru. Caesalpinia ancashiana nov. sp. is described and illustrated. It is related to C. bangii Rusby, but with different numbers of pinnae and size of the flowers.
23215730|A detailed biometrical study of Vicia in Tierra del Fuego demonstrates that two species can be recognized, differing in pollen size and structure, leaflet size, peduncle length and leaf-tendril form and size. The Andean Patagonian diploid V. bijuga Gillies ex Hook. & Arn. is restricted to northern and eastern Tierra del Fuego, while the tetraploid V. magellanica Hook. f. extends further south and west, reaching the south side of the Beagle Channel. In cultivation both species are shown to be self-compatible and capable of self- pollination. Rarely, naturally occurring triploids (2n = 21) have been found. El estudio biomtrico detallado de Vicia en Tierra del Fuego revela que se pueden reconocer dos especies, que se diferencian en el tamao y estructura del polen, el tamao de los foliolos, la longitud de los pednculos y la forma y tamao de los zarcillos. El diploide patagnico-andino V. bijuga Gillies ex Hook. & Arn. est limitado en su distribucin al Norte y Este de la Tierra del Fuego, mientras que el tetraploide V. magellanica Hook. f. se extiende ms al Sur y al Oeste, alcanzando la parte Sur del Canal Beagle. Bajo cultivo, ambas especies muestran ser autocompatibles y capaces de autopolinizacin. Raramente se pueden encontrar hbridos naturales triploides (2 n = 21).

23223905|This paper deals with the interpretation, description and typological characterization of the inflorescences of the following genera of the tribe Petreeae Briq.: Petrea L., Xolocotzia Miranda and Recordia Moldenke. All of them have a polytelic type of synflorescence. Florescences of all genera are racemes with decussate bracts. The heterothetic diplobotryum is present in Recordia and also in several species of Petrea. Truncation of the main florescence has been found in P. maynensis J. Huber, P. volubilis L. and P. pubescens Turcz. giving rise to an homothetic diplobotryum. Suppression of the enriching zone occurs in Xolocotzia, Recordia and some species of Petrea. Xolocotzia has monobotrya and reduction of flower number within the florescences. In the monobotrya the pair of leaves preceding the basal internode is bracteose and bears axillary resting buds. In the heterothetic diplobotryum this node represents an intercalar inhibition zone. Some Petrea species show aborted accesory paraclades. These arise from the accesory axillary buds of the enrichment zone. According to this study, the heterothetic pleiobotryum has been considered as a primitive or central form, from which monobotrya derived through processes of suppression of the enrichment zone, and homothetic pleiobotrya, by suppression of the main florescence (truncation). The use of inflorescence characters for a cladistic analysis accomplished by Rueda (1994) for the genus Petrea, are discussed. Se interpretan, describen y caracterizan tipolgicamente las inflorescencias de los generos pertenecientes a la tribu Petreeae Briq.: Petrea L., Xolocotzia Miranda y Recordia Moldenke. En todos los casos las inflorescencias son del tipo politlico; las florescencias son racimos con brcteas decusadas. Se han encontrado diplobotrios hetroteticos en Recordia, y en algunas especies de Petrea, diplobotrios homotticos en P. maynensis J. Huber, P. volubilis L. y P. pubescens Turcz. y monobotrios en Xolocotzia, Recordia y algunas especies de Petrea. En los monobotrios el par de hojas que precede al entrenudo basal es bracteoso y porta yemas axilares en reposo, en los diplobotrios hetroteticos este nudo, con iguales caractersticas, representa una zona de inhibicon intercalar. Algunas especies de Petrea muestran paracladios accesorios abortados que tienen su origen en yemas axilares accesorias de la zona de enriquecimiento. En este estudio el pleiobotrio heterottico se considera una forma primitiva o central de la que derivan los monobotrios por supresin de la zona de enriquecimiento, y los pleiobotrios homotticos por supresin de la florescencia principal (truncamiento). Se discute la interpretacon y utilizacin de los caracteres de la inflorescencia, aplicados a un anlisis cladstico del gnera Petrea, realizado por Rueda (1994).

23223011|With the purpose of identifying the most important honey plants of the Paran River Delta, field observations were made in order to assess honey bee (Apis mellifera L.) activity. The Asteraceae family is the best represented in number of species and the most visited by bees. The Leguminosae family was placed second. Species with massive blooms were used whenever they were present. Many species were used by bees only during a short period in the blooming season in spite of being available. The floral resource, estimated as the number of flowering species by week was hich at the beginning of spring and at the end of summer, showing a decrease at the beginning of the summer season. The species used with greater intensity during all their blooming period are considered to be a good resource.

El cariotipo es simtrico y est compuesto por 8 pares m, 3 pares sm y 1 par st. Los cromosomas son de pequeo tamao. El tamao promedio es 0,87-1,31 m para el tipo m, 1,17-1,51 m para el tipo sm y 0,90 m para el tipo st.

23228365|The ornamentation pattern of the upper anthecium in species of Paniceae belonging to the PCK group, in particular of the genus Urochloa, was analyzed. Nineteen different ornamentation patterns were recognized, of which 11 are reported for the first time. Several epidermal elements are described, including simple papillae, compound papillae and ridges in the anticlinal or periclinal cell walls. The ornamentation patterns were useful for infrageneric delimitation in the genus Urochloa but not to delimit the genus from related ones; on the contrary, this character provided more evidence to sustain the paraphyly of the genus. Systematic and phylogenetic value of this character in Urochloa and other related genera are also discussed. Como resultado se hallaron 19 patrones de ornamentacin diferentes, de los cuales 11 se describen aqu por primera vez. Varios elementos epidrmicos son descritos, incluyendo papilas simples, papilas compuestas y engrosamientos, tanto en las paredes celulares anticlinales como periclinales. Los patrones de ornamentacin resultaron de valor para la delimitacin infragenrica de Urochloa, pero no para delimitar este gnero de otros relacionados; por el contrario, este carcter provee ms evidencia que sustenta la parafilia del gnero. Se discute tambin el valor sistemtico y filogentico del patrn de ornamentacin del antecio superior en Urochloa y gneros vecinos.

Pollen grains of Cyclanthera have a mean polar diameter of 51.40 m, and an equatorial mean diameter of 49.10 m, a prolate spheroidal shape (P/E = 1.11), 4-7 zonocolporate, with circular endoapertures, and punctitegilate exine. Pollen grains of Sicyos have a mean polar diameter of 50.60 m and a mean equatorial diameter of 61.30 m, an oblate spheroidal shape (P/E = 0.88), 8-12 colpate, supra and microreticulate echinate exine. Los granos de Sicyos poseen el dimetro polar medio de 50,60 m y un dimetro ecuatorial medio de 61,30 m, formato oblato esferoidal (P/E = 0,88), 8-12 colpados, y la exina supra y microreticulada equinada. 23215056|Root cuttings taken from vertical and horizontal roots of Solanum eleagnifolium Cav. were found to have a high capacity for regeneration. The potencial of this species to form new roots and shoots is a rhithmie physiological process. Those cuttings obtained in the winter exhibited the maximum regeneration activity, while those collected during the summer, at the time of maximum flowering, had the minimum amount of regeneration. The number of roots initiated exceeded that of shoots on all root cuttings collected during all months of the year. Also more roots and shoots were differentiated on vertical root cuttings than on horizontal ones. The relative position of the new roots and shoots on both horizontal and vertical root segments clearly indicate the existence of the phenomenon of polarity. Those samples arising from vertical roots showed a high potential for regeneration regardless of the depth from which they were extracted. Some cuttings were still alive after being kept for fifteen months with the only requirement of a moist environment. They still exhibited a capacity for differentiation after this length of time.
23227995|Canna ascendens sp. nov. is described from several populations found in moist coastal and central locations of Buenos Aires Province, Argentina, often growing together with another colonial, urban species, C. variegatifolia, having larger plants with variegated leaves. Plants of C. ascendens are tall and large, yet smaller and more delicate than plants of C. variegatifolia; the leaves are concolorous, green, ovate to ovate-lanceolate in outline, usually conduplicate along their midrib with epicuticular wax over a striated or folded epidermis. More or less abundant intercellular pectic protuberances (warts) were found on the cell walls of both adaxial and abaxial hypodermis. The inflorescences are polytelic, reduced, with 1-2 paraclades or, eventually, no paraclades at all. Paraclade flowers are few, often only one, with a dull, rosy orange color. Plants were investigated anatomically, and a detailed description with diagnostic characters is included. The new species is compared with other species of Canna that grow in the area and also with other argentine species. Canna ascendens sp. nov. se describe a partir de poblaciones situadas en localidades hmedas, costeras y centrales de la provincia de Buenos Aires, a menudo coexistiendo con C. variegatifolia, otra especie colonial y urbana representada por plantas ms grandes, con hojas variegadas. Las plantas de C. ascendens son altas y grandes, aunque ms delicadas y de tamao algo menor que las de C. variegatifolia. Las hojas son concolores, verdes, ovadas a ovado lanceoladas, con frecuencia se doblan lo largo de la vena media, en forma conduplicada; en estado natural presentan una cubierta de cera epicuticular sobre la epidermis plegada y estriada y abundantes protuberancias intercelulares pcticas (verrugas) distribuidas sobre las paredes de las clulas de las hipodermis abaxial y adaxial. Las inflorescencias son politlicas reducidas, con 1-2 paracladios o con stos ausentes. Las flores son pocas, a menudo una sola, de color anaranjado rosado apagado. Se efectuaron anlisis de la anatoma, se da una descripcin completa de la nueva especie que incluye nuevos caracteres y se la compar con otras que crecen en la misma rea y con otras especies de Argentina.
23225161|Evidence from recent molecular studies suggested a reappraisal of genome relationships between Larrea ameghinoi and the other South American species of the genus. As a consequence, new attemps to study the meiotic pairing of the L. ameghinoi x L. cuneifolia hybrids were undertaken (2n = 3x = 39). Mean number of bivalents and univalents were 9.8 and 19.4, respectively. Since the basic number x is 13, the interpretation that is favored is that L. ameghinoi (2n = 2x = 26) (AA) and L. cuneifolia (2n = 4x = 52) (DDCC) share partially homeologous genomes (A and C) that are involved in most bivalent pairing and this would explain the partial seed fertility of these triploid hybrids (15-19.4 %). L. ameghinoi genome (A) could have retained several parts of an ancestral genome which makes possible at least some pairing with those of the other species and enable it to function as a pivotal genome producing some fertility (from partial to complete) in all the possible hybrid combinations with its three South American congeners. An appendix is included with the captions of the figures of chapter 2 from the book edited by Mabry et al. (1977) which were erroneously omitted in the editorial and printing process. Estudios moleculares recientes nos han inducido a realizar una reinterpretacin de las relaciones genmicas entre Larrea ameghinoi y las otras especies sudamericanas del gnero. Se hicieron nuevos intentos para estudiar el apareamiento de los cromosomas del hbrido L. ameghinoi x L. cuneifolia (2n = 3x = 39). El promedio de bivalentes y univalentes fue de 9.8 y 19.4, respectivamente. Dado que el nmero bsico x es 13 la interpretacin ms razonable es que L. ameghinoi (2n = 2x = 26) (AA) y L. cuneifolia (2n = 4x = 52) (DDCC) comparten genomas parcialmente homelogos (A y C) que forman la mayora de los bivalentes y eso explicara la produccin de semillas (15-19.4 %) de estos hbridos triploides. El genoma de L. ameghinoi (A) podra haber retenido varias partes de un genoma ancestral que hace posible algn apareamiento con aquellos de las otras especies y que lo capacitara para funcionar como un genoma pivote que permite alguna fertilidad (desde parcial a completa) en todas las posibles combinaciones hbridas con sus tres congneres sudamericanos. Se incluye un apndice con las leyendas completas del captulo 2 del libro de Mabry et al. (1977) que fueran omitidas por error en el proceso editorial y de impresin.
23222564|Fifty-one plants of Paspalum distichum L., each from a different place of the Buenos Aires province were studied in order to: a) establish their chromosome numbers; b) assess the phenotypic variability that presents this species; c) determine which percentage of that variability is due to genetic causes; d) evaluate the morphological similarities among plants and to rank them based on those similarities. The existence of hexaploid (2n = 60) and tetraploid (2n = 40) plants was confirmed and, for the first time, the presence of pentaploids (2n = 50) and hiperpentaploids (2n = 52, 54, 57 and 58) was reported in this species. Hexaploids are the most frequent cytotype under the ecological conditions of Buenos Aires province. The analized plants showed a great morphological variability. This variability is due both to the heteroploidy shown by this species and to the existence of genetic differences among individuals of the same cytotype. Applying multivariate analysis to the data obtained, two well differentiated groups of individuals were distinguished, one composed by tetraploid plants and, the other, constituted by pentaploids, hiperpentaploids and hexaploids.

The affinities between R. brittonii and R. microcarpa Baldw. ex Asa Gray and R. confinis and R. filiformis Vahl have been considered and their special characteristics have been pointed out in two keys. Thirty five species of marine Cyanophyceae from Puerto Deseado and Cabo Blanco (Prov. Santa Cruz, Argentina) are described. They are distributed among fifteen genera belonging to the following families: Chroococcaceae, Dermocarpaceae, Oscillatoriaceae, Nostocaceae and Rivulariaceae. Most of the thirty five species are cosmopolitan (68,5%) or sub-cosmopolitan (20%) and only 11,5% are more restricted in their geographical distribution. From the ecological point of view and according to the kind of substratum, seven communities were observed: muddy soil-, Salicornia- blue green algae-, lithophytic-, planktonic-, epiphytic- and a very conspicuous one on rocks integrated by Brachidontes purpuratus-Rhodophyceae- Cyanophyceae; each of these is described and the predominant species are given. This paper also includes a list of marine blue green algae recorded until up to date from Argentine coasts (16 species from which only 9 are marine).

23230246|Tillandsia bryoides was sunken into the synonmy of T. tricholepis because all the elements of the lectotype (P. Lorentz 128, BM) belong to the latter species. 23222568|Argentinean members of five Solanaceae tribes, 2 of the subfam. Solanoideae (Solaneae and Jaboroseae) and 3 of the subfam. Cestroideae (Cestreae, Nicotianeae and Salpiglossideae) are studied in their meiotic chromosomes. A total of 166 accessions from 65 species and 14 genera are examined. Among them, the chromosome numbers of 27 species are reported for the first time. A statistical analysis of the chromosome behavior at diakinesis-metaphase I is made on 11 species from 8 sections and 4 subgenera of Solanum L. Some meiotic irregularities are detected in 29 specimens from 19 species and 7 genera. Furthermore, polyploids were observed in several Solanum sect. Lathyrocarpum (G. Don) Walp. species. Leptostemonum (Dun.) Bitt. A great difference in chromosome size is found between the members of Solanum sect. Cyphomandropsis Bitt. and the ones of the other sections of this genus. The results are discussed in respect to the unclear delimitation between Solanum and Cyphomandra Sendt.

23222998|Nectar chemical composition and nectary anatomy are studied in two Argentine species of Mutisieae: Hyaloseris rubicunda Griseb. and Barnadesia odorata Griseb. The capitulum of H. rubicunda has reddish bracts and it is composed of 5-6 perfect, red-orange, nectariferous flowers. On the other hand, B. odorata capitulum has greenish bracts and white, perfect, dimorphic flowers; only the 3-central flowers are nectariferous while the several peripheral ones do not have nectaries. Nectar sugar composition is rich in hexose in B. odorata and rich in sucrose in H. rubicunda. Alkaloids, phenols, reducing acids, lipids and amino acids were not detected in any sample. In both species, the nectary is related to the upper portion of the ovary. Its base is supplied with the ovarian vascular bundles. The upper nectary portion surrounds the style base and shows many stomata and has no special vascular bundles. Hummingbirds Sappho sparganura (Lesson) and Chlorostilbon aureoventris (D' Orbigny et Lafresnaye) were seen visiting the capitula of H. rubicunda in the studied population. The white flowers of B. odorata produce a weak, pleasant scent during evening hours and would be pollinated by sphingids. The data are compared and discussed considering the flower biotypes of the studied species.
23223859|Variation of the plant diversity of five remnants of secondary wet forest was studied at different successional stages in the Cordillera Central of the Colombian Andes, at 750-1100 m. Several transects were used (50 m  2 m) for the analysis, and the total area analyzed was 2000 m. Only individuals with a dbh  2.54 cm were considered. Structural analysis revealed 837 individuals belonging to 145 species distributed among 60 families. The richest families were Leguminosae (14 species), Melastomataceae (12), Rubiaceae (10), and Arecaceae, Clusiaceae and Lauraceae (7 species each). Species-rich genera were Miconia (7 species) and Inga (6 species). About 74% of the species were represented by less than three individuals, showing a very homogenous distribution. Pielou's Evenness Index J' showed values close to 1. Simpson's Index D' revealed low dominance, contrary to what is expected for secondary forests. Floristic similarity was estimated based on Czekanowski's Index, which showed values lower than 16% between remnants. This demostrates great variation in the floristic composition of the study area. Linear regression analysis showed no relationships between age of the remnants and diversity, species number, evenness, and dominance. This suggests that the most advanced successional stages are not necessarily more diverse than the younger ones. A balance of the number of species is reached early in the successional process in the area investigated. However, the remnants are in a taxonomically unstable condition, as was demonstrated by the strong variation in the floristic composition among remnants. This study demonstrates that there is a balance between local inmigration and extinction. Se estudi la variacin de la diversidad florstica en cinco remanentes de diferentes estadios sucesionales en un bosque hmedo secundario de la cordillera Central de los Andes colombianos, localizado a una altura de 750-1100 m s.m. Se emplearon transectas de 50 m  2 m, siendo el rea total analizada de 2000 m. Slo fueron considerados los individuos con un DAP  2,54 cm. Los anlisis estructurales revelaron la existencia de 837 individuos pertenecientes a 145 especies, distribuidas en 60 familias. Las familias ms diversas fueron Leguminosae (14 especies), Melastomataceae (12), Rubiaceae (10) y Arecaceae, Clusiaceae y Lauraceae con 7 especies cada una. Los gneros ms ricos fueron Miconia (7 especies) e Inga (6 especies). Cerca del 74% de las especies estuvieron representadas por menos de tres individuos, mostrando una distribucin muy homognea. El ndice de equidad de Pielou mostr valores cercanos a uno, mientras que el ndice de Simpson revel baja dominancia, contrario a lo que se espera para bosques secundarios. La similitud florstica se estim a partir del ndice de Czekanowski, el cual arroj valores inferiores al 16% entre remanentes. Esto demuestra la gran variacin en la composicin florstica del rea estudiada. Los anlisis de regresin lineal mostraron que no haba relacin entre la edad de los remanentes y la diversidad, el nmero de especies, la equidad y la dominancia de las especies. Esto sugiere que los estadios sucesionales ms avanzados no son necesariamente ms diversos que los estadios ms jvenes. En el rea de estudio, el equilibrio del nmero de especies es alcanzado tempranamente en el proceso sucesional. Sin embargo, los remanentes se encuentran en desequilibrio taxonmico, lo que fue demostrado con la fuerte variacin en la composicin florstica entre remanentes. Este estudio demuestra que hay un equilibrio entre extincin e inmigracin locales.

23213878|The author describes two new monotypic genera of Malvaceae, tribe Malveae: Dirhamphis and Hochreutinera. 23218072|This paper deals with the palynological study of the Argentine representatives of the genus Cathormion (Benth.) Hassk, C. polyanthum (A. Spreng.) Burk. and C. polycephalum (Gris.) Burk., which were placed in the Secc. Cryptarthra by A. Burkart in 1964. As it is common in Mimosoideae, the dispersal unit is the poliade. The authoress has found in both species poliades formed by 16 or 28-32 monades, either in the same or different specimens. The sculpture of the exine at the distal face of the central monades is areolate or fosulate; at the distal face of lateral monades is fosulate to smooth, sometimes areolate. The palynological characters added to some morphological features do not furnish enough differences to distinguish both entities as different species.
23222537|A new species of Cyperus (Cyperaceae) from Misiones, Argentina. Cyperus burkartii nov. sp. is described and illustrated; an anatomical description is also given. It is a very distinct species because of its cancellate achenes, longitudinally striate with transverse rectangular epidermal cells. This is a rare character among the species of Cyperus, shared with C. mirus C. B. Clarke, an Australian species of the section Graciles. C. burkartii belongs to section Diffusi and is related to C. friburgensis Bck., a South American species with smooth achenes and pedicellate spikelets.
23215047|Pollen grains of Argentine Leguminosae. III. Mimosoideae, Tribe Piptadenieae and Mimozygantheae. The pollen grains of the Argentine species of the tribe Piptadenieae occur in apparently similar poliads. Nevertheless it is possible to differenciate them in the whole of characters for each species. The comparative table and a key to recognise the species, corroborate the distinctive characters. The pollen grains of the tribe Mimozygantheae, represented by one species, have similar characters with the pollen grains of the Argentine representatives of tribe Adenanthereae.
23218943|The occurrence of crystals in the hairs of several species of Nassauvia (Compositae). Calcium oxalate crystals frequently prismatic, but also as rhomboedral and lenticular types, were observed in the lumen of the leaf hairs of 8 Argentine species of Nassauvia: N. fuegiana, N. axillaris, N. aculeata, N. uniflora, N. darwinii, N. chubutensis, N. glomerulosa and N. ulicina. These crystalliferous hairs, described here for the first time for the genus, are non glandular, 3-10 cells long, with 2-3 short basal cells, intermediate ones longer and a terminal pointed cell. The transverse walls, sometimes very oblique, possess conspicuous pit pairs, looking like articulations, being therefore denominated here oblique-septate articulated hairs. The crystals, isolated or in groups, are mainly located near the transverse-oblique walls. As these crystals are particularly abundant in the xerophilous species of Nassauvia, a relationship between their occurrence and the habit of the plant was suggested. A brief discussion on the existence, mentioned by other authors, of this uncommon character in the Compositae is also given, as well as a short reference on the probable function accomplished by the crystals in the plant metabolism.
23218078|Se describe el cariotipo volumen nuclear y contenido de ADN en 7 especies afines de Oxalis con 2n = 10 cromosomas y se relacionan estos datos con las distintas formas biolgicas observadas en las mismas. O. refracta St. Hil. y O. niederleinii Knuth tienen un cariotipo casi totalmente asimtrico con 2n = 10 (2m + 8t) y son anuales. O. hepatica Norlind con 2n = 10 (2m + 2sm + 4st + 2t) y O. sarmentosa Zucc. con 2n = 10 (2m + 4sm + 4t) tienen el cariotipo ms simtrico y son perennes con tallo areo estolonfero. O. eriocarpa D.C. con 2n = 10 (4m + 2smm + 2sm + 2st), O. praetexta Prog. 2n = 10 (4m + 4sm + 2st) y Oxalis sp. 2n = 10 (4m + 4sm + 2st) tienen cariotipos ms simtricos que las cuatro especies descriptas ms arriba, las tres son perennes y tienen un tallo subterraneo leoso. El contenido de ADN se incrementa con la simetra del cariotipo. Se considera que aquellas especies anuales con menos contenido de ADN y cariotipo ms asimtrico (O. refracta y O. niederleinii) son probablemente ms avanzadas que el resto de las especies perennes. Se discute tambin la correlacin encontrada entre el contenido de ADN y el volumen nuclear. The karyotype, nuclear volume and DNA content of 7 allied species of Oxalis were analyzed. In spite of having 2n = 10 large chromosomes they were classified, according to their variation of the vegetative morphology, in different sections of the genus. However, the cytological data and the morphology of the inflorescence and fruit suggest that the 7 entities are probably taxonomically related. On the other hand, a probable relationship between the vegetative characteristics and the variation of karyotype symmetry in these species was found. O. refracta St. Hil. and O. niederleinii Knuth possess an asymmetrical karyotype with 2n = 10 (2m + 8t); they are both annuals. O. hepatica Norlind with 2n = 10 (2m + 2sm + 4st + 2t) and O. sarmentosa Zucc, with 2n = 10 (2m + 4sm + 4t) are perennials. O. eriocarpa D.C. 2n = 0 (4m + 2smm + 2sm + 2st) O. praetexta Prog. 2n = 10 (4m + 4sm + 2st) and O. sp. 2n = 10 (4m + 4sm + 2st) have the most symmetrical karyotypes of the 7 species studied, because they have only one pair of subtelocentrics. The 3 entities are parennials. The variation in the symmetry of the karyotype is probably related to the variation found in DNA content. The latter ranged from 9.25 pg in O. refracta to 15.99 pg in O. eriocarpa and the differences in DNA amount between species are significant. Moreover the correlation between DNA content and the mean of the centromeric index, as a relative value of the karyotype symmetry, is positive and highly significant. This shows that the increase in DNA amount is probably related to the symmetry of the karyotypes. The relationships between the cytological data and the life cycle in these species suggests that the two annual species with less DNA content and asymmetrical karyotypes (O. refracta and O. niederleinii) are probably more advanced than the other 5 perennial species. Also the positive and significant correlation found between the DNA content and nuclear volume is discussed.
23612317|The biosiliceous microfossil record has a high preservation degree in different natural and cultural contexts. For that reason, the study of phytoliths and other siliceous microremains may contribute both to infer environmental conditions of local plant communities that surrounded an archaeological site, and to identify plant species with anthropic use. We analized phytoliths and other siliceous microremains from a profile of Tres Cerros 1 archaeological site (LTC1, Las Moras Island, Victoria Department, Entre Ros, Argentina) and other collected samples from particular features observed during excavation of the site. The bio-siliceous microfossil analysis revealed elements related to both wild plant resources from the present phytogeographic unit, and cultural plant management of species related to Arecaceae, Cucurbitaceae, and Poaceae (subfamilies Maideae and Oryzoideae). The bio-siliceous microfossil record of the LTC1 profile has a clear change between baseline and the top of the anthropic depositional unit, which can be correlated with different activities during the construction process of the mound, which took place between ca. 1000 - 500 years 14C BP. El registro de microfsiles biosilceos posee un alto grado de preservacin en distintos contextos naturales y culturales. Por esta razn, el estudio de los fitolitos y otros microrrestos biosilceos puede contribuir a determinar las condiciones ambientales de las communidades vegetales que rodearon un sitio arqueolgico, as como tambin identificar especies vegetales domesticadas. En esta contribucin se realiz el anlisis de fitolitos en el marco de otros bioindicadores de los depsitos superiores de la secuencia sedimentaria antrpica del sitio Los Tres Cerros 1 (LTC1, isla Las Moras, Departamento Victoria, Entre Ros, Argentina). Los anlisis desarrollados permitieron identificar morfotipos silceos relacionados con la presencia de vegetales silvestres que caracterizan a la unidad fitogeogrfica actual del rea de emplazamiento, y morfotipos silceos asignables a recursos vegetales de inters cultural, pertenecientes a las familias Arecaceae, Cucurbitaceae, y Poaceae (subfamilias Maideae y Oryzoideae). El registro de microfsiles biosilceos del perfil del sitio LTC1 tiene un cambio neto que puede ser correlacionado con diferentes actividades culturales desempeadas durante el proceso de construccin del montculo, que tuvo lugar durante ca.1000 - 500 aos 14C AP.
23213828|En la presente revisin del gnero de orqudeas sudamericano, Chloraea, se consideran vlidas 46 especies y 1 variedad. Dos de las especies, C. elegans y C. septentrionalis, se describen por primera vez y se hace la nueva combinacin. C. disoides var. picta, Se da una clave para identificar las especies basada en caracteres florales, especialmente los de los ptalos y el labelo. Han sido dibujadas todas las especies y su distribucin est indicada en una serie de mapas. Estos sealan que, con excepcin de 2 especies Chloraea bella y Chloraea memebranacea de la regin oriental, la distribucin del gnero es casi endmica de los Andes, encontrndose las especies desde el norte del Per hasta la Tierra del Fuego. In the present revision of the Southamerican genus Chloraea (Orchidaceae) 46 species and 1 variety are considered valid. Two species, C. elegans and C. septentrionalis, are described as new and the new combination C. disoides var. picta, is proposed. A key based on floral features, specially those of the petals and the labellum, is given for their identification. All the species have been drawn and their distribution indicated on a series of maps. These show that, with the exception of 2 species Chloraea bella and Chloraea membranacea of the oriental zone the distribution of the genus is wholy Andean, ranging from northern Per to Tierra del Fuego.
23211703|Se observa que la estructura anatmica de las especies filas del gnero Cassia converge con la de otras plantas filas, adaptadas a climas secos, diferencindose de las dems especies de Cassia. Es caracterstica la presencia de una epidermis gruesa, cutinizada, de una hipodermis desarrollada, parnquima cortical dividido en dos zonas (la exterior en palizada) separadas por fascculos de fibras esclerenquimticas, unidos o no entre s por escleritos; en varias especies se observa la presencia de pigmento rojo en la hipodermis y en el mesfilo; la presencia y distribucin de drusas y maclas de oxalato de calcio vara. 23215560|In the present paper the karyotypes of four diploids and one tetraploid species of Hippeastrum (Amaryllidaceae) are described. The nomenclature used for chromosome morphology, is that proposed by Levan et al. (1964): m chromosome (Centromeric index Ci = short arm  100/total chromosome length = 50-37.5), sm chromosome (Ci = 37.5-25) and st chromosome (Ci = 25-12.5). The nomenclature proposed by Battaglia (1955), for the description of chromosomes with satellite was used. The results obtained are: H. argentinum (Pax) Hunz.: 2n = 22, 8 m + 8 sm + 6 st; H. rutilum (Lam.) Herb.: 2n = 22, 8 m + 8 sm + 6 st; H. agliae (Cast.) Hunz. et Coc.: 2n = 22, 8 m + 8 sm + 6 st, in these three karyotypes the pair st n 10 has a terminal microsatellite in the short arm (Figs. 1, 2, 3, 4). H. vittatum (L'Herit.) Herb.: 2n = 22, 8 m + 6 m + 8 st, the pair st n 11 has a terminal microsatellite in the short arm (Figs. 2, 4). H. petiolatum Pax: 2n = 44, 16 m + 16 sm + 12 st. All the karyotypes are bimodal because m chromosomes are shorter than sm and st chromosomes (Figs. 1, 2). In general, the species studied here had the same basic karyotype (4 m + 4sm + 3 st), only H. vittatum possesses a derived karyotype involving small changes. This basic karyotype is common to the eight species in which the karyotype has been studied. Because of this, we can consider this karyotype as fundamental in Hippeastrum. In a single individual of H. argentinum a heteromorphic pair of chromosomes was found. So far 25 species of the genus have been studied cytologically, 21 of these have only diploid level. The scarcity of polyploidy in the genus (16 %) might be a consequence of the absence of chromosome repatterning in a primary speciation (Cuadros 1, 2). Results of other authors concerning cytological data are also discussed.

23217316|Chromosome studies in Phytolacca dioica, P. tetramera and P. bogotensis (Phytolaccaceae). Chromosome studies and observations were made on Phytolacca dioica, P. tetramera and P. bogotensis. The chromosome number of the first species is confirmed, the last two are reported for the first time. P. dioica is a tetraploid (2n = 36) with very small somatic chromosomes (0.5 - 1.4 m). P. bogotensis is also a tetraploid (2n = 36) with normal meiosis behaviour forming 18 bivalents. The size of its somatic chromosomes varies between 1 to 1.8 m. The karyotype is composed by 14 m - sm and 4 st - t chromosomes. There is a terminal satellite in the short arm of a st - t chromosome. P. tetramera is an octoploid (n= 36) and its meiosis shows the formation of up to 5 quadrivalents. It has larger chromosomes than P. dioica, which belongs also to the same subgenus and section.

23215700|Se realiz un estudio de los caracteres epidrmicos e histologa de los fololos de tres especies de Adesmia, que habitan regiones ridas de: Patagonia austral y Tierra del Fuego, en Argentina y zona central de Chile. Desde el punto de vista ecolgico, A. salicornioides es la que presenta mayor nmero de caracteres xeromrficos. A. balsamica y A. resinosa poseen caractersticas epidrmicas y foliolares semejantes entre s y ambas presentan solamente algunos de los caracteres considerados como ndices de xeromorfismo. La presencia de una capa de cutina discontinua entre la epidermis y el mesfilo, encontrada en estas especies, puede considerarse como carcter relacionado con hbitats ridos. A study of the epidermal characters and histology of the leaflets of 3 species of Adesmia (Leguminosae) was carried out. These species belong to the arid regions of Southern Patagonia and Tierra del Fuego in Argentina and to the central zone of Chile. From an ecological point of view, A. salicornioides presents more xeromorphic characters than the other two species. A. balsamica and A. resinosa are very similar to each other in their epidermic and leaflets characters, and only present some of the features which are considered xeromorphic. The presence of a discontinuous cutine layer between the epidermis and mesophyll founded in this species of Adesmia is probably related to arid habitats.

23218128|A revision of the genus Chuquiraga (Compositae-Mutisieae). The genus Chuquiraga as here treated comprises 19 species of xerophyllous bushes of South America; the history and systematic relationships within the genus and with other genera,and the morphology, geographical distribution and economic importance of the species are discussed. The taxonomic treatment includes a description of the genus, keys to the sections, series and species, and a list of excluded names. All the taxa are described and illustrated and distribution maps are given. In many cases, nomenclatural problems, intraspecific variability and affinities between the species are also analyzed. In this revision a new infrageneric classification is proposed, the genus being divided into two sections: Acanthophylla nov. sect., and Sect. Chuquiraga with two series-Parviflorae nov. ser. and Ser. Chuquiraga. Other taxonomical novelties are: Two new subspecies are described (Ch. spinosa Less. subsp. australis and subsp. huamanpinta) and three changes of status are proposed (Ch. spinosa subsp. rotundifolia (Weddell) nov. stat., Ch. ulicina subsp. acicularis (Don) nov. stat. and Ch. erinacea subsp. hystrix (Don) nov. stat.). The name Ch. parviflora (Gris.) Hieron., which had been reduced to synonymy of Ch. oppositifolia Don, is rehabilitated, and the morphological and geographical differences between both species are discussed. A new epithet is proposed (Ch. morenonis (O. Ktze) nov. stat.) for Ch. argentea (Speg.) Speg., name invalidated by an earlier homonym. The name Ch. spinosa (Ruiz et Pav.) Don, erroneously used to designate the taxon here described as Ch. spinosa Less. subsp. huamanpinta, is excluded form the genus. The following names are reduced to synonymy for the first time: Ch. erinacea f. pulvinata Cabrera; Ch. incana Phil.; Ch. insignis var. armata Weddell; Ch. johnstonii Tovar; Ch. jussieui var. lancifolia (H. et B.) Koster; Ch. kingii Ball; Ch. oppositifolia var. macrantha Gay; Ch. oppositifolia var. macrocephala Weddell; Ch. pseudoruscifolia Muschler; Ch. revoluta Field et Gardn; Ch. ulicina var. incana (Phil.) 23226850|Ten members of the tribe Cariceae (Cyperaceae) occur on the Juan Fernndez Archipelago: four species of Carex and six of Uncinia. Eight of the ten species occur on Alejandro Selkirk Island (= Masafuera; 50 km2) while four are known from Robinson Crusoe Island (= Masatierra; 48 km2). Carex fernandezensis, C. stuessyi, Uncinia aspericaulis, and U. macloviformis are newly described from the archipelago and all are endemic to the islands. Only two species, Carex berteroniana and Uncinia douglasii, both endemics, are of frequent occurrence and each occurs on both islands. Another endemic, Uncinia costata, is known only from the type locality on Alejandro Selkirk. The three remaining species, Uncinia phleoides, U. tenuis, and Carex phalaroides, the last here reported for the first time from the archipelago, also occur on the South American mainland. Lectotypes are chosen for the names Uncinia costata and U. tenuis f. firmula. Additionally, a new section of Carex, sect. Pellucidae, is circumscribed in this paper for the sectional placement of C. stuessyi and cognate species. En el Archipilago Juan Fernndez se encuentran diez miembros de la tribu Cariceae (Cyperaceae): cuatro especies de Carex y seis de Uncinia. Ocho de las especies se hallan en la Isla Alejandro Selkirk (= Masafuera; 50 km2), y cuatro en la Isla Robinson Crusoe (= Masatierra; 48 km2). Se describen cuatro nuevos taxones endmicos para el Archipilago: Carex fernandezensis, C. stuessyi, Uncinia aspericaulis, y U. macloviformis. Slo dos especies endmicas, Carex berteroniana y Uncinia douglasii, son frecuentes en ambas islas. Otro endemismo, Uncinia costata, es conocido slo en la localidad de coleccin del tipo en Alejandro Selkirk. Las tres especies restantes, Uncinia phleoides, U. tenuis, y Carex phalaroides, se encuentran tambin en el continente Sudamericano, y se cita aqu por primera vez C. phalaroides para el archipilago. Se lectotipifican los nombres Uncinia costata y U. tenuis f. firmula, y se describe una nueva seccin de Carex, sect. Pellucidae, para ubicar a C. stuessyi y taxones afines.

23223904|Structural anatomy of seedlings of Cupressus lusitanica Mill., C. macrocarpa Hartw. and C. sempervirens L. (Cypress) cultivated in Argentina was studied. Seedlings of these species were fixed at eight different stages of the germination process. Anatomical features of root, hypocotyl, cotyledonary node, cotyledons and epicotyl were described. The root-hypocotyl-cotyledon vascular transition was analized. In the root and in most of the hypocotyl length, the protoxylem exhibits exarch position. At the cotyledonary node the metaxylem differentiates gradual- and laterally divergent from the protoxylem. In sections of the upper zone of the hypocotyl, close to the cotyledonary node, the protoxylem shows an endarch position. In the epicotyl, the undifferentiated procambium alternates with the cotyledonary vascular bundles. The number of xylematic poles is equal to the number of cotyledons in thr three species. Se estudi la estructura anatmica de las plntulas de Cupressus lusitanica Mill., C. macrocarpa Hartw. y C. sempervirens L. (Ciprs) cultivados en la Argentina. Plntulas de las mencionadas especies fueron fijadas en ocho etapas diferentes de la germinacin. Se describieron los caracteres anatmicos de la raz, el hipoctilo, el nudo cotiledonar, los cotiledones y el epictilo y se analiz la transicin vascular raz-hipoctilo-cotiledn. En la raz y en la mayor parte del hipoctilo, el protoxilema presenta posicin exarca. En el nudo cotiledonar, el metaxilema se diferencia progresiva y lateralmente divergente desde el protoxilema. En secciones de la zona superior del hipoctilo, muy cerca del nudo cotiledonar, el protoxilema muestra una posicin endarca. En el epictilo, el procmbium no diferenciado alterna con los haces vasculares cotiledonares. El nmero de polos xilemticos es igual al nmero de cotiledones, en todas las especies estudiadas.

23217342|Exomorphological Numerical Taxonomy of four South American species of Elytrigia (Gramineae). The exomorphic characters of the following four South American species of Elytrigia were studied: E. attenuata (Kunth) Covas, E. breviaristata (A. Hitchc.) Covas, E. scabrifolia (Doell) Covas, E. tilcarensis (J. H. Hunz.) Covas. Numerical methods were applied to estimate the degree of similarity. Clusted analysis was performed on 14 morphological characters of 100 individuals and ordination by principal components analysis was done on the same characters of the four species, based on basic matrix data MBD-2 (Table 2). Both numerical methods indicate a strong similarity between E. attenuata and E. breviaristata. E. scabrifolia and E. tilcarensis show a low degree of similarity with all other species studied. These results are in close agreement with cytogenetic data from interspecific hybrids and with the ecological characteristics of the species but are not congruent with protein electrophoretic data, which have been published elsewhere (Hunziker and Ferrari, 1986).
23215057|In the mountains of Crdoba in central Argentina, a curious peach tree has become established in the wild, called  duraznero de palo  because the drupe has only little greenish, non edible flesh. This is described as Prunus persica var. aposarca nov. var. and interpreted as a filogenetic regression. Economically this variety is of interest for grafting because of its strong root system, but germination of the stones is very low, unless a cold treatment is applied. In connection with this variety a general subspecific system for P. persica is proposed, with subspec. floriplena nov. ssp. for the double-flowered sorts. The origin, genetic constitution of the species and an experiment on leaf evaporation are discussed.

The author has completed a critical study of the Argentine Festuca species (excepting those of Patagonia, which were already monographed by Parodi in 1953). Parodi and F. weberbaueri Pilg. are common to the regions studied in this work and to Patagonia (Parodi, 1953). According to the width of their blades, the Festuca species of Argentina can be divided into two big groups: one of those with flat blades, of more than 1 m high, which usually have extravaginal innovations, and the other with conduplicate blades of less than 3 mm wide, composed of plants of few cm high, up to 1 m, with intra-, seldom, extravaginal innovations. 23222957|The morphology, distributional patterns of phenolic compounds and meiotic behaviour of several individuals of G. incisa (Hook.) Tronc., G. pulchella (Sweet) Tronc. and six natural putative hybrids from the province of Corrientes (Argentina) were analyzed. Both species belong to welldifferentiated morphological groups and possess taxon-specific chromatographic compounds. Putative hybrids are morphologically intermediate and their chromatograms show almost total addition of the compounds of the parental species. Two numerical techniques (principal component analysis and distance diagram) are congruent, and both show the intermediacy of the putative hybrids. Despite the morphological and chromatographical similarities of the hybrids, their meiotic behaviour presents highly significant differences in chain bivalents, circle bivalents, univalents and chiasma frequency. The results obtained suggest that some genic combinations of parental species are more disharmonious than others. According to Jackson's (1984) model, the parental species would be polymorphic and/or polytypic for mutations that cause changes in the site of attachment of genome to the nuclear membrane. The ability of the chromosomes to pair in the F1 hybrids will depend on the distance of the nuclear site attachment of its two parental genomes, and pairing at the diploid level would be controlled by a relatively simple gene system.
23218067|This paper deals with the leaf and stem anatomical characters (including the epidermical ones) of the genus Munroa Torrey. The main conclusions derived from this study are: Munroa is a C4 genus, K-PS-NAD-me. It has all the characteristics assigned to this category: double bundle sheath and the chloroplasts in the Kranz sheath cells are centripetally placed. The genera Munroa, Blepharidachne, Dasyochloa and Erioneuron can be separated by the anatomical features of the stem.
23215615|This paper describes a study of the foliar fiber sclereids of Byttneria coriacea. Their size ranges between 55-380 . Their shape is very variable: they can be twisted in different ways or they may have 1, 2 or more branches. The walls are quite thick, but not very lignified; pits are very scarce. The sclereids are restricted to the mesophyll which they cross in all directions, also forming a netlike subepidermal layer specially on the adaxial face of the leaf. The range of density of sclereids is very wide, going from a few branches crossing the areoles to a remarkable network through the blade.

darwiniana.2.1.174|Plant species that coexist and share pollinators may experience inter-specific competition for pollinator service or interference of improper pollen. To avoid the latter, plant species may use different areas of the pollinators body to deposit their pollen, either by different floral architectures or by different floral lengths. We evaluate here the existence of this pattern of differential use of body areas of pollinators in 33 sphingophilous communities of subtropical Argentina. We use null models to evaluate if the plants deposit the pollen overdispersed relative to what would be expected by chance either in different body parts or at different heights in the proboscis of hawkmoth pollinators. We found that 42 native plants species are pollinated by hawkmoths in subtropical Argentina. We observed a significant and positive correlation between the operative length i.e. the distance between anthers and stigma from nectar of the flowers and the mean length of the proboscis of hawkmoth pollinators. However, both the average diversity of pollen deposition sites and the average difference of operative length between sphingophilous plant species present in the same community were not significantly different than expected under a null model. When analyzing the results in individual communities, nine communities showed a diversity of pollen deposition sites significantly higher than expected by chance and two communities showed a difference in the operative length greater than expected by chance. These results suggest that other factors such as the degree of generalization in pollination, phenology and / or the use of distinctive floral signals may be avoiding competition for pollinators between coexisting plants species.

23222960|This paper deals with the androsporangium development, androsporogenesis and androgametogenesis of 3 Argentine species of Cucurbitaceae, with emphasis in the mechanism of anther dehiscence and the possible physical link between the gametogenic cell and the siphonogenic nucleous within the androphyte (pollen grain). The following are the main conclusions: a) The androsporangium wall develops according to the basic type established by Davis (1966), with 2 or 3 middle layers in different areas of the same androsporangium wall. The tapetum is of the secretory type with uninucleate cells. Sporogenous cells of Cayaponia citrullifolia (Griseb.) Cogn. y C. bonariensis (Mill.) Mart. Crov. show different ability to divide mitotically before meiosis. Meiotic cytokinesis is simultaneous and produces tetrahedric tetrads. Androphytes are 2-celled when shed. b) Endothecium cells exhibit ringed or spiralled fibrous thickenings on their tangential walls, like a folding hood. During the dehiscence the endothecial cells compress along their tangential axis. In Cayaponia citrullifolia and C. bonariensis the epidermal cells also compress under endothecial pression and the androsporangium wall contracts over itself. But in Cucurbitella duriaei (Naudin) Cogn. the epidermal cells resist endothecial pressure and the androsporangium wall contracts more on its inner side than on the outer one, bending towards the loculus. Both dehiscence mechanism are in relation to the androecium structure. c) The androgametogenesis suggests some kind of physical link between the gametogenic cell and the siphonogenic nucleous, which together form the male germ unit (Owens, 1992). This linkage could be established during or immediately after the mitosis of the androspore. According to some figures published in the literature, the gametogenic cell seems to be linked to the siphonogenic nucleous in other species of Cucurbitaceae and it is also possible that the male gametes could be linked to the siphonogenic nucleous within the pollen tube.

41825694|We have analyzed the ethnobotany and anatomy of five aromatic species with medicinal or edible use, highly valued in Argentine Patagonia: Valeriana clarionifolia, V. carnosa (Valerianaceae), Azorella monantha, Osmorhiza chilensis and Eryngium paniculatum (Apiaceae). We focused on the characterization of the secretory structures of the underground organs and their possible link to sensory perceptions and uses given by the people. Ethnobotanical work was conducted in two Mapuche indigenous communities of the province of Neuqun and in two communities of Chubut, with a total of 53 interviews. The anatomical work consisted of structural and ultrastructural observation of the secretory structures. Informants indicated that E. paniculatum is mainly used to treat digestive and liver disorders; O. chilensis for vision problems, and A. monantha as urinary and antitussive; also underground organs of these three species are eaten raw and/or cooked. Valeriana species are mainly used as analgesic, digestive, antitussive and in cultural syndromes. The taste and smell are the main sensory properties used to recognize and use the Valeriana and O. chilensis species. Azorella monantha and E. paniculatum are recognized by their morphological characteristics, but also are valued for its taste and smell. The microscopic observations revealed the presence of schizogenous secretory cavities in O. chilensis, E. paniculatum and A. monantha, and abundance of starch. In species of Valeriana periderm is observed with a high content of essential oils like drops. We conclude that these species have organoleptic attributes originated in specialized anatomical structures, which partly explain their food and/or medicinal uses. Se analiza la etnobotnica y anatoma de cinco especies aromticas de uso medicinal y/o comestible altamente valoradas en la Patagonia argentina: Valeriana clarionifolia, V. carnosa (Valerianaceae), Azorella monantha, Osmorhiza chilensis y Eryngium paniculatum (Apiaceae). El principal nfasis ha sido la caracterizacin de las estructuras secretoras de sus rganos subterrneos y su posible vinculacin con las percepciones sensoriales y usos dados por los pobladores. El trabajo etnobotnico se realiz en dos comunidades indgenas Mapuches de la Provincia de Neuqun y en otras dos de la Provincia de Chubut, con un total de 53 entrevistas. El trabajo anatmico consisti en la observacin estructural y ultraestructural de las estructuras secretoras. Los informantes indicaron que E. paniculatum es principalmente usada para tratar trastornos digestivos y hepticos, O. chilensis para problemas de la visin y A. monantha como urinaria y antitusiva; adems los rganos subterrneos de estas tres especies se consumen crudos y/o cocidos. Las especies de Valeriana son usadas principalmente como analgsicas, digestivas, antitusivas y en sndromes culturales. El sabor y el aroma son las principales propiedades sensoriales usadas para reconocer y usar las especies de Valeriana y O. chilensis. A. monantha y E. paniculatum son reconocidas por sus caractersticas morfolgicas, aunque tambin se valoran por su sabor y aroma. Las observaciones microscpicas revelan la presencia de cavidades secretoras esquizgenas en O. chilensis, E. paniculatum y A. monantha y abundante presencia de almidn. En las especies de Valeriana se observa la peridermis con elevado contenido de aceites esenciales como gotas. Se concluye que estas cinco especies poseen atributos organolpticos originados en estructuras anatmicas especializadas, los que en parte explicaran sus empleos alimenticios y/o medicinales.

41825710|This paper analyzes the distribution of vascular plants species endemic to the southern central Andes (south-western Bolivia and north-western Argentina). All 540 species endemic to the study regions (approx. 720600 km) have been included in the analysis. The main part of the endemic species is found in semiarid habitats between 1500-3500 m asi pointing to the topographically complex plateau, slope, and valley system of the southern central Andes as the main locations for its endemic flora. The distribution of the endemic species within arid sites is in contrast with that of vascular plant diversity in general, as the most diverse habitat of the region is the moist subtropical Tucumano-Bolivian Yungas forest of the eastern Andes slope. A total of 17 well defined and partly overlapping distribution patterns were indentified. The broadest distribution pattern defines a general area of endemism for the southern central Andes. This area extends through nearly the entire region and is defined by species that are widespread within the region in desert to sub-humid environments of the high Andes, slopes, or valleys. Nearly all other areas of endemism are nested within this broad distribution pattern as successively north-south overlapping areas along the slopes and valleys of the Andes and the Pampeanas Range. Despite the distributional bias of endemism towards the arid sites almost half of the endemic species are restricted to a few high endemic areas that lie in juxtaposition to the main rainfall zones. These areas contain the widest habitat ranges in terms of altitude and rainfall within the region with the endemic species being equally variable in altitude and moisture requirements. Previous defined phytogeographic units were not recognized among the distribution patterns. However, the northern part of the Prepuna can be defined as two partly overlapping distribution patterns. Este trabajo analiza la distribucin de especies de plantas vasculares endmicas de la porcin sur de los Andes centrales (sudoeste de Bolivia y noroeste de Argentina). En el anlisis se incluyeron 540 especies endmicas de la regin estudiada (aproximadamente 720.600 km). La mayora de las especies endmicas se halla en ambientes semiridos, entre 1500-3500 m s. m., encontrndose principalmente en valles, laderas y mesetas del topogrficamente complejo sur de los Andes centrales. Las reas de endemismos aqu halladas se presentan consecuentemente en ambientes ridos y no en ambientes hmedos subtropicales de las Yungas tucumano-bolivianas, a pesar de que en esta ltima regin la diversidad de plantas vasculares es mayor. Se identificaron un total de 17 patrones de distribucin bien definidos, y parcialmente solapados. El patrn de distribucin ms amplio define un rea general de endemismos para los Andes centrales. Esta rea se extiende a lo largo de casi toda la regin y est delimitada por especies que se distribuyen en ambientes desrticos a sub-hmedos en laderas, valles o regiones altoandinas. Casi todas las restantes reas de endemismo se encuentran anidadas dentro del patrn de distribucin amplio antes citado, superponindose en el sentido norte-sur a lo largo de pendientes y valles de los Andes y de las Sierras Pampeanas. A pesar del sesgo observado en la distribucin hacia ambientes ridos, aproximadamente la mitad de las especies endmicas estn restringidas a unas pocas reas de alto endemismo, las que se encuentran en yuxtaposicin con las zonas ms lluviosas de la regin. Estas reas de alto endemismo incluyen los rangos de habitat ms amplios de la regin en trminos de altitud y precipitacin, siendo las especies endmicas igualmente variables en sus requerimientos de humedad y elevacin. 23230185|A cytogenetic analysis using surface spreading and air drying was performed to analyze the mitotic chromosomes of Karwinskia calderonii, K. parvifolia and K. subcordata. The results confirm a diploid number 2n = 24 and a basic number x = 12. All species showed a somatic complement characterized by small meta- and submetacentric chromosomes. The smallest pair of each complement carried a secondary constriction and a satellite. Morphological and numerical constancy in the chromosome complements agree with previous studies in other species of the genus. Results suggest some kind of nucleotypic differentiation related to geographic factors as latitude and altitude. Se observan constancia numrica y similitud morfolgica en los complementos cromosmicos de las especies estudiadas del gnero. Los resultados sugieren algn tipo de diferenciacin nucleotpica asociada a factores geogrficos como la latitud y la altitud.

41825707|This work is an ethnobotanical approach to the diversity of groups and local varieties of peaches and the criteria to delimit these ethnotaxa. It also describes management practices that accompanies the maintenance of this culture in a northwestern Argentinian community. A main classification was proposed, the cultivarieties group, defined as the set of varieties together under one common name which is the result of the sum of attributes derived from various locally defined criteria. A subcategorization known as etnovarieties, defined by specific characteristics, was also established. This first approach demonstrates the transcendental value that the incorporation and ownership of a foreign resource acquires as a representative element of the landscape and cultural context of the community, which is displayed on the deep knowledge of the inhabitants to shape a classification and incorporate the agricultural practices associated to this crop. Este trabajo constituye una aproximacin etnobotnica a la diversidad de grupos y variedades locales de duraznos y los criterios para delimitar esos etnotaxones. Adems, se describen las prcticas de manejo que acompaan la conservacin de este cultivo en una comunidad del noroeste argentino. Se estableci una clasificacin principal, denominada grupos de cultivariedades, la cual se define como el conjunto de variedades reunidas bajo un nico nombre vulgar, resultado de la suma de atributos y diversos criterios definidos localmente. Asimismo, se estableci una subcategorizacin en etnovariedades definidas por caractersticas particulares. Este primer acercamiento evidencia el valor trascendental que adquiere la incorporacin y apropiacin de un recurso forneo como elemento representativo del paisaje y del contexto sociocultural de la comunidad, el cual se expresa en el profundo conocimiento que poseen los pobladores para disear una clasificacin e incorporar prcticas agrcolas asociadas a este cultivo.
23223204|Caesalpinia L. sensu lato, is a pantropical genus with approximately 150 species: 40 of them occur in South America. There is great morphological variation within Caesalpinia: it includes trees, shrubs, and perennial herbs, some scandent, armed or not; hair-covering is diverse; pedicels are jointed or not; flowers with imbricated and falling sepals; legume chartaceous to woody, unarmed or echinate, frequently with dendromorphus hairs. Its species inhabits forests and semi-deserts. Two subgenera are currently accepted in this genus: Caesalpinia, with species in the New and Old World, characterized by not winged fruits and subgenus Mezoneuron (Desf.) Vidal ex Herendeen & Zarucchi, a subgenus of Old World species with winged fruits. Caesalpinia still needs further detailed studies in order to clarify its generic delimitation at a worldwide level. Hoffmannseggia Cav. sensu stricto, includes nearly 20 species growing from southern United States, N of Mexico, Andean and semi-deserts zones of Peru, Bolivia to Chile and Argentina;13 of these species occur in South America. This genus is probably a derived evolutionary unit from primitive Caesalpinia like group and it is mainly defined by herbaceous plants, sub-stemless and with gemmiferous roots, pedicels not jointed, flowers with sepals generally valvate, persistent, and legume without dendromorphus hairs.

23226694|Lippia integrifolia and L. boliviana are related species that share the presence of appendices in anthers, apparently glandular. Several authors distinguished this species by leaf shape and margin. Collections coming from northern Salta (Argentina) display intermediate characters among both species. To evaluate whether there is a morphological basis to distinguish L. integrifolia from L. boliviana, phenetic relationships among 40 specimens including both species and their varieties were studied. A matrix of 46 morphologic characters was analyzed by cluster and ordination methods. Both the dendrogram and the distribution of the specimens in the principal components (PCA) analysis suggest that a precise limit between both species does not exist, and no characters to differentiate them were found. Consequently, L. boliviana is placed under the synonymy of L. integrifolia. A description of the species, the synonym list, a figure and map of distribution are included. Lippia integrifolia y L. boliviana son especies afines que comparten la presencia de apndices en las anteras, aparentemente glandulares. Diversos autores las distinguen por la forma y el margen foliar. Colecciones procedentes del N de Salta (Argentina), presentan caracteres intermedios entre ambas especies. Se estudiaron las relaciones fenticas entre 40 ejemplares de ambas especies y sus variedades para evaluar la validez de los taxones y determinar si existen caracteres que permitan diferenciarlos. Se analiz una matriz de 46 caracteres morfolgicos con mtodos de agrupamiento y de ordenacin. Tanto el fenograma como la distribucin de los ejemplares en el anlisis de componentes principales (PCA) sugieren que no existe un lmite preciso entre ambos taxones y no se hallaron caracteres que permitan diferenciarlos. 23224217|This research is focused on the study of Klebsormidium nitens vegetative and reproductive cells. The following aspects have been considered for the identification of this species, which is a new record for Argentina: morphological characters, growth habits, aperture of zoosporangial cells, zoospore germination patterns and types of reproduction. As regards its life cycle, vegetative multiplication through an easy fragmentation of the thallus into short filaments was the prevailing mode of reproduction. Under adverse conditions, false (or pseudo) branches were formed from which new filaments were born. Asexual reproduction was induced "in vitro". Biflagellate zoospores with subapically inserted flagella came out from a pore in the lateral wall of sporangial cells. After swimming for a few minutes, zoospores withdrew the flagella, and germination was strictly unipolar. The basal cell presented a rudimentary holdfast with a fine mucilaginous attaching disc. After successive mitosis and cytokinesis a filament was formed which became planctonic after an eight-celled stage. The absence of a holdfast has so far been considered a diagnostic character of the genus, and for this reason the reconsideration of this feature at the generic level has been proposed. Sexual reproduction was not observed. The chromosome number found in K. nitens was n=6. A comparison among chromosome number, nucleus size and filament width with other species of Klebsormidium suggests a basic chromosome number x=6 and polyploidy as one of the processes involved in the evolution of Klebsormidium species. Se estudiaron las clulas vegetativas y reproductivas de Klebsormidium nitens, primera cita para la Repblica Argentina. La identificacin de la especie se realiz utilizando caracteres morfolgicos, hbito de crecimiento, la forma de apertura de los zoosporangios, forma de germinacin de las zosporas y el modo de reproduccin. Con respecto a su ciclo de vida, la forma de reproduccin ms frecuente fue la vegetativa, por simple fragmentacin del talo en filamentos cortos. Bajo condiciones adversas se produjeron pseudoramificaciones, a partir de las cuales se originaron nuevos filamentos. La reproduccin asexual fue inducida ''in vitro". Zosporas biflageladas con insercin subapical de los flagelos salieron por un poro lateral. Las zosporas despus de nadar unos minutos retrajeron los flagelos y la germinacin fue estrictamente unipolar. La clula basal present un rudimentario pie de fijacin acompaado de un delicado disco de fijacin mucilaginoso; sucesivas mitosis y citocinesis originaron un filamento, el cual pas a vida planctnica al superar las ocho clulas. La ausencia de un pie de fijacin ha sido considerada hasta el momento un carcter diagnstico del gnero; la presencia de dicho pie en K. nitens sugiere que la validez de este carcter para definir el gnero debera ser revisada. No se verific reproduccin sexual. El nmero cromosmico hallado en K. nitens fue n = 6. Comparaciones entre el nmero cromosmico, el tamao del ncleo y el ancho del filamento con otras especies de Klebsormidium sugiere un nmero bsico x = 6 y a la poliploida como uno de los procesos involucrados en la evolucin de las especies del gnero.
23223191|The phytolith morphology belonging to the leaves of 8 species of Stipa (S. brachychaeta Godr., S. charruana Arechav., S. filiculmis Delile, S. hyalina Nees, S. neesiana Trin. et Rupr., S. papposa Nees, S. philippii Steud. and S. trichotoma Nees), present in the prairies of Entre Ros Province, is described. A new terminology and descriptive methodology to define the phytolith assemblage of each species is used. Cluster analysis (UPGMA) and principal component analysis (PCA) were performed on the data of 49 morphological characters from the 8 phytolith assemblages (OTUs). The results define three groups, the first group include S. filiculmis and S. trichotoma assemblages, the second one with S. hyalina and S. neesiana assemblages and the third one with (S. brachychaeta + S. charruana) + (S. papposa + S. philippii) assemblages. The 8 phytolith assemblages show Arundinoideae affinity (sensu Twiss, 1992), and differ from the typical phytolith assemblages of other Poaceae subfamilies.
23230247|This contribution introduces an inventory of the species of Poaceae from Colombia, and an analysis of the species diversity according to the natural regions of Colombia, the altitudinal gradients, annual rainfall and systematic distribution. The inventory was based on about 5800 vouchers collected throughout 96 fieldtrips along the 10 greatest natural regions of Colombia (Amazon, Andes, Caribbean, Caribbean Islands, Choc Biogeogrfico, Guayana, Orinoquia, Sierra Nevada de Santa Marta, Cauca valley, and Magdalena valley), on the study of vouchers of different herbaria with important collections for the flora of Colombia (CAUP, COAH, COL, CUVC, CHOCO, HFAB, HUA, HUQ, JAUM, MEDEL, MEXU, MO, NY, PSO, RSA, SI, UDBC, UIS, US, VALLE, and VEN), and on an exhaustive bibliographic research. Poaceae is represented in Colombia by 840 species and 173 genera. There are 74 species and one genus (Agrostopoa) endemic to Colombia. On the other hand, there are 83 species introduced and naturalized, and 50 introduced and cultivated. The richest genera are Paspalum (89 especies), Panicum (42), Festuca (36), Eragrostis (29), Calamagrostis (25), Chusquea (25), Digitaria (24), Axonopus (21), Setaria (20), Cenchrus (18), Poa (17), Muhlenbergia (16), Andropogon (15), Aristida (15), Agrostis (14), Lasiacis (12), Urochloa (12), Pariana (11), Sporobolus (11), Arthrostylidium (10), Cortaderia (10), Nassella (10), Neurolepis (10), and Schizachyrium (10). As partial results of this research, 10 new records were described for the colombian territory. The most diverse Colombian regions are Andes, Orinoquia, Caribbean, and Guayana, with 583, 233, 186, and 179 species, respectively. The Andean Region shows the highest endemism values (57 species). The most diverse altitudinal gradient belongs to the lowlands (below 1200 m s.m.). In Colombia, the subfamilies of Poaceae show a distribution related to the altitude above the sea level and with the rainfall patterns. Thus the Panicoideae are more diverse in the wet lowlands and wet subandean areas, the Pooideae are more diverse in the high Andes (pramos), the Chloridoideae in dry areas, the herbaceous bamboos in the Amazon Region, and the woody bamboos in the Andean Region. The grasses constitute the sixth richest family in the Colombian flora, following the Orchidaceae, Asteraceae, Rubiaceae, Fabaceae, and Melastomataceae. 23222561|Meiotic behavior of six interspecific hybrids was studied. The hybrids between species with n = 16 chromosomes showed regular meiosis with 16 bivalents; they varied considerably in pollen viability (5-60%). These results suggest the existence of cryptic structural hybridity. The structural divergence between A. quitensis (2n = 32) and the grain species A. caudatus (2n = 32) and A. hypochondriacus (2n = 32) is higher than that observed between A. quitensis (2n = 32) and the wild species A. hybridus (2n = 32). The pollen viability of the A. hybridus (2n = 32)  A. quitensis (2n = 32) hybrid is lower than that observed in its parents; these results suggest that there is some degree of reproductive isolation and consequently they are not co-specific. The A. cruentus (2n = 34)  A. quitensis (2n = 32) hybrid showed 15II + 1III in all cells. This fact supports the hypothesis that n = 17 would have its origin in a n = 16 ancestor through primary trisomy. The hybrid between A. hybridus (2n = 32) and A. spinosus (2n = 34) showed 8II + 17I as the most frequent configuration, suggesting that both species would have a  = 8 genome with high homeology; moreover this fact, together with the secondary association found in all studied species and hybrids, supports the hypothesis that present species (x = 16) of the genus Amaranthus (2n = 32) are polyploids (basic number  = 8) and that consequently n = 16 is a derived basic number. The number n = 17 (x = 17) would have appeared later by primary trisomy. The study of A. dubius (2n = 64)  A. spinosus (2n = 34) hybrid suggest that there would be autosyndetic pairing between A. dubius chromosomes and allosyndetic pairing between A. dubius and A. spinosus chromosomes. It is therefore concluded that A. dubius would be an allooctoploid that would have stabilized at 2n = 64 by an aneuploid process, being A. spinosus one of its parental species.
23225108|A novel technique, mixing surface spreading and air-drying (splash) to study plant chromosomes is used to determine the possibility of a response in the genotype-environment for three legumes. These species are typical of Mexican arid and semi-arid areas, from populations occurring in localities with different climatic conditions. The species studied are Prosopis laevigata and Acacia schaffneri, from Municipio Santiago de Anaya, State of Hidalgo (20 16 N) and P. laevigata and Acacia farnesiana from Municipio Bermejillo, State of Durango (25 49 N). Four features are evaluated: total chromosome length, karyotype, polysomatic frequency, and seed weigth. This study corroborates in Prosopis laevigata a diploid number of 2n=28 and determines statistically significant interpopulation differences (= 0,01) in chromosome total length; the karyotype formula shows no change (2m+10sm+2st); and the polysomatic frequency does not exceed 10%. In the studied species of Acacia, diploid chromosome numbers of 2n=26 are recorded, and no statistically significant interspecific differences (= 0,01) in total chromosome length are found. However, with the use of this mixed technique of spreading and air-drying, different karyotypic formulas, here reported for the first time, are obtained, namely: 9m+2sm+2st for A. farnesiana, and 9m+4sm for A. schaffneri. Both species of Acacia show a similar polysomatic frequency, not surpassing 30%. No significant differences (= 0,01) are found in seed weigth between Prosopis strains and between species of Acacia. The results indicate a kind of adaptation in close relationship with environmental requirements that modify chromosomal characters via natural selection. These environmental requirements do not necessarily affect other nucleotype-dependent characters, such as seed weight. Se emplea una tcnica de extendido en superficie y secado al aire (splash) para cromosomas vegetales a fin de analizar la posible respuesta genotipo-ambiente de tres especies de leguminosas tpicas de las zonas ridas y semiridas mexicanas, ubicadas en poblaciones con caractersticas climticas diferentes. Las especies estudiadas fueron Prosopis laevigata y Acacia schaffneri del municipio de Santiago de Anaya, estado de Hidalgo (20 16' N) y P. laevigata y Acacia farnesiana del municipio de Bermejillo, estado de Durango (2549' N). Los parmetros evaluados fueron las longitudes cromosmicas totales, el cariotipo, la frecuencia de polisomata y el peso de las semillas. En Prosopis laevigata se corrobora un 2n=28 y diferencias interpoblacionales estadsticamente significativas (=0,01) en las longitudes cromosmicas totales, sin modificacin de la frmula cariotpica (2m+10sm+2st) con frecuencia de polisomata que no rebas el 10%. En las especies del gnero Acacia se registraron nmeros cromosmicos diploides 2n=26 sin diferencias interespecficas estadsticamente significativas (= 0,01) en las longitudes cromosmicas totales; no obstante se obtuvieron frmulas cariotpicas diferentes, reportadas por primera vez empleando una tcnica de extendido y secado al aire: 9m+4sm para A. schaffneri y 9m+2sm+2st para A. farnesiana. En ambas especies la polisomata tuvo una frecuencia similar sin rebasar el 30%. Para Prosopis y Acacia no se encontraron diferencias significativas (= 0,01) en relacin al peso de la semilla. Los resultados obtenidos sealan una clase de adaptacin en estrecha relacin con exigencias ambientales que modifican caractersticas cromosmicas va seleccin natural. Estas exigencias no necesariamente afectan otras caractersticas dependientes del nucleotipo. como el peso de las semillas.
23218936|Chromosome studies on Anthericum ciliatum var. argentinense (Liliaceae). The somatic (2n = 32) and meiotic chromosomes (n = 16) of Anthericum ciliatum (Kunth in H. B. K.) Sprengel var. argentinense Hauman have been studied for the first time. The karyotype is composed of 11 m pairs + 3 sm pairs + 2 st pairs; pair 2 bears macrosatellites. 23218064|As a commemoration of the centennial of Charles Darwin's death a brief account of his life and works is presented. His family background, youth, studies, the voyage of the Beagle around the world and his monumental production despite his illness is considered. Doubtless his major contribution was to convince his contemporaries that evolution did occur and that natural selection was the factor responsible for evolutionary change and adaptation. His pioneering studies of ecology, psychology, ethology, floral biology, plant movements, hormonal action, inbreeding depression, etc., are briefly reviewed as well as his major geological contributions, such as the origin of atolons and coral reefs and his correct estimate of the age of Earth. His work and personality, which makes him one of the most important scientists and thinkers of all times, undoubtedly will be admired and remembered for many future generations.
