23223184|The structure and anatomy of floral trichomes and nectaries of 4 species of Tecomeae (Bignoniaceae) are studied. All taxa exhibit pluricellular glandular trichomes of different forms and distribution in calyx, corolla and ovary wall and bear a conspicuous floral nectary except for Catalpa bignonioides Walter. In this species the floral nectary is reduced and appears to be a vestigial organ without a secretory function. The nectary of Argylia radiata (L.) D. Don, Podranea ricasoliana (Tanfani) Sprague and Pandorea jasminoides (Lindl.) K. Schum. comprises epidermis and secretory parenchyma without intercellular spaces. Secretory tissue is supplied by phloem. Raised nectarial stomata were found only in P. ricasoliana, whereas they are at the same level of the epidermis in the remainder species. Extrafloral nectaries were found in flowers of P. jasminoides and P. ricasoliana in the outer surface of the calyx. Those of P. jasminoides are cupular and vascularized while those of P. ricasoliana are patelliform and nonvascularized.

23222514|Xeromorphic leaf characters of Nassauvia lagascae (Compositae). The xeromorphic leaf characters of Nassauvia lagascae (Don) Meigen and its varieties, N. lagascae var. lanata (Phil.) Skottsberg and N. lagascae var. globosa Skottsberg, referred to section Caloptilium of subgenus Nassauvia, are described. All are herbaceous perennial plants, forming loose hemispherical mats on stony, gravel soils of the high Andean mountains at 3300- 4000 m above sea level. The adaptative characters show a reduction in leaf surface (microphyllia) and a ribbed and furrowed lamina at the upper, more exposed adaxial part. These ribs are formed by compact adaxial caps of sclerenchyma, as girders between vascular bundles and the adaxial epidermis. The number of vascular bundles increases from the apical to the basal part of the lamina, 1 at the top, 5-9 at the ribbed zone and 10-13 at the leaf sheath. The mesophyll is composed by a palisade parenchyma of 8-9 layers of small, oval cells compactly arranged and 3-4 layers of spongy parenchyma with conspicuous arm cells. An extensive air cavity is sometimes formed very early in leaf development between the abaxial epidermis and the adjacent mesophyll. The epidermal characters include thick external periclinal walls and conspicuous pitted anticlinal walls, stomata protected in the adaxial furrows and sunken in cavities produced by a pronounced overarching and outbulging of its neighboring cells; these cavities observed in surface view are limited by peristomatal rims. In old leaves a progressive thickening of the external and internal periclinal walls of the epidermal cells including the occlusive ones occur; likewise a partial occlussion of the pores and substomatal chambers is produced by the neighboring cells of stomata and as a consequence numerous non functional stomata, some of them lignified, alternate at this stage with the functional ones. A dense indumentum is present in N. lagascae var. lanata and N. l. var. globosa, whereas in N. l. var. lagascae the pubescence is sparse. Therefore these plants possess a highly specialized leaf structure with clear xerophytic adaptations. A discussion of all the mentioned characters in comparison to other xeromorphic anatomical strategies established by several authors in different plants is also provided. Brief comparative references to N. revoluta, a species with a rather similar leaf anatomy previously described by other authors, is also given.

23222954|Flower phases and flower visitors of Vigna longifolia (Benth.) Verdcourt were studied in Parque Rivadavia (Concordia, Entre Ros province, Argentina). Flowers are flag-blossom in structure, although the alighting place here is the left-hand wing petal. Standard and wings (yellow) are atractive to visitors. Under UV lighting each floral part exhibits a different colour (in violet range) which changes from phase to phase. Four floral phases were recognized from anthesis to wilting (24 hs.). In the second and third phases the stigma is receptive. Pollen is presented in the tuft of hairs of the style, is abundant and reacts positively to peroxidases in all phases, and its main cytoplasmic reserve is starch. Pollenkitt, sufficiently abundant so as to maintain pollen grains pasted together, contains lipids and proteins. Pollen viability is 84%. Amongst the three flower visitors observed, Megachile sp. is the only one that triggers the pollen transfering and stigma exposing mechanism (nototribic, between head and thorax). Ants (Camponotus sp.) visited extrafloral nectaries continually, keeping flower visitors away most of the time. The development of the ovary in flowers isolated for 24 and 48 hs. and the pollen tube growth in those isolated for 48 hs., as well as the analysis of the P/O relationship suggest that this species is a facultative xenogamous-facultative autogamous. However, the seed production allows us to conclude that some incompatibility system should exist (fecundation efficiency: 51%).

23212951|"Contributions on the knowledge of the austral species of Grammitis. Anatomy of Grammitis magellanica Desv., and its form nana." In the first part of this paper, the author reports some data on the geographic distribution of the Grammitis billardieri Willd. complex. This group, as constructed here, contains six species, two of them living in the southern part of Chile and Argentina. This complex presents an austral distribution, entirely around the Antarctic, with a remarkable insular character. Also, the author considers Grammitis magellanica as a different species from the Australian plants. In the second part, the author studies the anatomy of Grammitis magellanica and its form nana, giving special emphasis on the rhizome and stipe structure. Grammitis magellanica presents a dorsiventral rhizome, with a dissected solenostele, with a large ventral perforation. In the stipe, only one vascular strand, with two terminal protoxylematic groups, is present. These anatomic patterns fortify the seggregation of the Grammitidaceae as a natural family. Observations on the venation pattern, epidermis, stomata and hairs, are also given. The systematic status of the form nana, under the light furnished by the comparative data (size of stomata, epidermal cells and spores), is discussed. According to these, the presence of polyploid series is suggested.
23223221|The floristic composition and species richness of the western (moister) and eastern (dryer) areas of the high Andean region of Nahuel Huapi National Park (Argentina) were compared. Species lists were compiled for the two sectors from collections in the alpine area of 20 mountains of the Park (10 from each sector) from 1993 to 1997. A total of 232 species, 111 genera and 48 families were recorded. Asteraceae (with 70 species), Poaceae (17), Apiaceae (12), Fabaceae (11) and Scrophulariaceae (11) are the predominant families in the area, and Senecio (with 22 species), Nassauvia (12), Acaena (7), and Perezia (7) are the best represented genera. There are six endemic species in this protected area. The most frequent life forms are perennial herbs and subshrubs, followed by shrubs, and annual species are nearly inexistent. Species richness was found to increase in relation to the precipitation decrease from west to east: 149 species were found in the moister western sector and 220 in the dryer eastern sector. Some families and genera are more represented or appear exclusively in one of the two sectors. We discuss current ecological and past historical factors that could explain this variation in species diversity and composition.

23222539|Revision of the Argentine species of Cerastium L. (Caryophyllaceae). I. Ten species of the genus Cerastium were analyzed, using mainly material from the Argentinian herbaria. Three species are naturalised: C. fontanum Baumg. subsp. vulgare (Hartman) Greuter & Burdet, in the South Andes, in cold and wet places; C. arvense L., in the Andes between Salta and Tierra del Fuego and Malvinas Islands and C. glomeratum Thuill. in modified soils, in the whole country. Cerastium tucumanense is here lectotypified. All the species are described, mapped (excluding C. glomeratum) and a key is included for their identification.

23215043|The present paper is an anatomical study of the leaf nectaries of 65 species of Byttneria (Sterculiaceae) which comprise the whole area of the genus and its morphological variations. The first bibliographic account on this topic is that of Nieuwenhuis (1907) who describes the nectaries of B. pilosa; later Zimmermann (1937) mentions the nectaries of B. pilosa and B. cordata. Finally Hall illustrates the external aspect of these glands in B. dahomensis, B. ivorensis and B. guinensis. This paper includes an analysis of the bibliography on nectaries taking special account of the nectaries of Malvaceae, which are very similar to those of Byttneria. For the anatomical study herbarium material was used and for the ontogenetical one, fresh material of cultivated plants. A list of the samples studied is given at the end of every species description. In Byttneria, there is generally one nectary per leaf, situated on the underside of it, on the central vein. In certain species, there are 3 or 5 nectaries per leaf, which are distributed on the principal veins. In excepcional cases, there are also nectaries on the petioles. This genus presents 2 fundamental types of nectaries, which are named respectively, uniapertured and multiapertured. The former present, when examined superficially, a single aperture bordered by lip-shaped prominences.

23225124|Information about fungi of the orders Cyttariales, Helotiales, Ostropales, Pezizales, Rhytismatales and Thelebolales (Discomycetes) collected in Patagonia, Tierra del Fuego and adjacent antarctic areas (Patagonia), and information about their associated organisms was located, abstracted, keyboarded, edited and validated. The largest single information sources were dried reference collections in Argentina and elsewhere, and published information as listed in this work's bibliography. Other records were derived from fresh collections, other reference collections and field observations. Information is stored in a computerized system of relational databases for taxonomic, nomenclatural, bibliographic and biological observations data. This system allows storage of parallel data in different languages, and distinguishes original information from current opinion about what that information may mean. In the Biological Records Database, 5029 separate records were created for observations on the spatial and temporal occurrence of living organisms in the region. Of these 2613 were Discomycetes, with records derived as follows: Patagonia and Tierra del Fuego (Argentina, 1854; Chile, 687); adjacent antarctic areas (72). Excluding synonyms, these Discomycetes represented 361 species and subspecific taxa (160 genera, 22 families and 7 orders) the remaining records were organisms associated with these Discomycetes as follows: 163 of animals (8 species, 8 genera, 6 families and 5 orders); 2 of chromistans; 223 of fungi (52 species, 54 genera, 26 families and 13 orders); 2028 of plants (159 species, 122 genera, 59 families and 39 orders). Each of these different taxa (and each known synonym) is represented by a separate record in the Taxonomic & Nomenclatural Database. Information about relevant bibliographic sources is stored in more than 120 records in the Bibliographic Database. The databases were used to produce the present checklist of names given to Discomycetes observed in Patagonia. A typical entry comprises the fungus name, author(s), and information on the original place of publication of the name, together with any known synonyms (classification at generic level and above largely follows the 9th edition of Ainsworth & Bisby's Dictionary of the Fungi, Kirk et al., 2001). This is followed by basic information derived from the databases: the number of times the fungus has been recorded from the region, the date of the earliest record from the region, months in which the fungus has been observed in the region, geographical distribution by country (and within countries by an appropriate subnational division), associated organism and substrata, a list of reference collection numbers identifying preserved specimens and sometimes living isolates of each fungus, and bibliographic citations identifying any published sources of the information. The status of each name is indicated and, where appropriate, synonyms are provided and cross-indexed. The list is accompanied by an explanatory introduction, a taxonomic index, indexes by countries and subnational divisions of the region, by taxonomy of associated organisms and by substrata, and a bibliography. No new taxa are described. Apart from four new nomenclatural combinations, no new scientific names of any sort are knowingly introduced. En la Biological Records Database, 5029 registros fueron creados para observaciones sobre la ocurrencia temporal y espacial de los organismos vivos de la regin. 23218134|On the correct scientific name of the scented camomile (Matricaria recutita L., Asteraceae). 23226840|Gracilaria chilensis (Gracilariales) is an agarophyte red alga belonging to class Florideophyceae. The purpose of this study was to describe the hair formation mechanism. Thalli were maintained in culture with enriched seawater under controlled conditions of light and temperature. Hair formation was induced on portions of thalli growing in a nitrogen-free culture medium. Light (bright field) microscopy, transmission and scanning electron microscopy techniques were used. Hairs develop from large ovoid hair-producing cortical cells (HPCs). These cells are multinucleate, contain small plastids, and abundant endoplasmic reticulum apically positioned. Each hair begins as a protuberance initially covered by a multilaminar wall, this is, in turn, ruptured along with the thallus wall as the protuberance elongates. Hairs are formed when cytokinesis occurs at the base of the protuberance. An asymmetric pit plug is formed between the hair's base and the HPC. Hairs are unicellular, with a vacuole and numerous nuclei. They have an active growth, and leave a concentric scar on the wall after detachment. Hair formation mechanism in G. chilensis is also compared with that observed in other species of the same class. In nitrogen-free culture media, the thallus of G. chilensis grows less, but the number of hairs increases. Gracilaria chilensis es un alga roja agarfita perteneciente a la clase Florideophyceae. En este estudio se describe la formacin de pelos en talos mantenidos en cultivo en agua de mar enriquecida, bajo condiciones controladas de luz y temperatura. La induccin de los pelos fue realizada colocando porciones de talos en un medio de cultivo carente de compuestos nitrogenados. Se emplearon tcnicas de microscopa ptica y electnica de transmisin y barrido. Los pelos se desarrollan a partir de clulas corticales ovoides grandes. Estas clulas formadoras de pelos (CFPs) son multinucleadas, poseen pequeos plstidos y una abundante red de retculo endoplasmtico de disposicin apical. La formacin de los pelos comienza con el desarrollo de una protuberancia, inicialmente cubierta por una pared multilaminar, la cual se rompe junto con la pared del talo, con la consecuente elongacin de la protuberancia. El pelo queda establecido cuando se produce una citocinesis en la base de la protuberancia, formndose una conexin citoplasmtica obliterada o "pit plug" asimtrica entre la base del pelo y la CFP. Los pelos son unicelulares, poseen una vacuola y numerosos ncleos. Tienen un crecimiento activo dejando, al caerse, una cicatriz de forma concntrica en la pared. Se compara este proceso con el descrito en otras especies de la clase. En medios de cultivo carentes de nitrgeno, el crecimiento del talo de G. chilensis fue menor, aumentando el nmero de pelos.
23222527|A comparative study of diploid and tetraploid populations of Grindelia chiloensis (Asteraceae). Two cytotipes have been found in G. chiloensis, a resinous perennial herb from Argentina. 23218079|The diversity found in the foliar architecture of the species of the genus Prosopis could be adequately expressed through six models with four variants. These models have been established according to the form and symmetry of the leaflets, the number of venous traces in the secondary pulvinules, and the venation characters determined by the behaviour of the primary and secondary veins. The characters of the venation of the major order have proved to of little taxonomic importance due to their strong intraspecific variations. The occurrence of the different models among the species of Prosopis lead us to conclude that the sections and series in which the genus is divided constitute natural groups of species with regard to the foliar architecture.
23230232|A hybrid, named tricepiro, was obtained in 1972, by crossing a hexaploid triticale (2n=6x=42) and an octoploid trigopiro (2n=8x=56). The lines achieved include the tricepiro Don Ren INTA, which has shriveled kernels, and FA-L2, which has smooth ones. The relationship between the heterochromatin content of the rye chromosomes, the seed weight, the presence of meiotic abnormalities and the kernel shriveling has been documented previously in other intergeneric hybrids. The purpose of this study was to determine the average percentage of heterochromatin content in the rye chromosomes of the two tricepiro lines mentioned above and to relate this feature to some characteristics of the meiosis and seeds. We confirmed that the two lines have the same total chromosome number (2n=42) and the same number of rye chromosomes (14). We found that both lines have a complete chromosome mating until late diakinesis, but differ in the percentage of cells with univalents outside the equatorial plate in Metaphase I (Don Ren 42.85% and FA-L2 14.00%). In addition, the two lines differed in their meiotic index (Don Ren 66.47% and FA-L2 87.90%) and seed weight (Don Ren 0.029  0.000 g and FA-L2 0.038  0.001 g). The C-banding in rye chromosomes in mitotic metaphase indicated that the average percentage of heterochromatin content did not differ significantly between the two lines. In contrast to our expectations, the meiotic behavior and seed characteristics were not related to the heterochromatin percentage of the rye chromosomes of the tricepiro lines studied. Confirmamos que las dos lneas tienen el mismo nmero cromosmico (2n=42) y el mismo nmero de cromosomas de centeno (14). 23230245|We analyzed pollen morphology of Tropaeolum argentinum, T. atrocapillare, T. capillare, T. incisum, T. meyeri, T. patagonicum, T. pentaphyllum, T. polyphyllum, T. porifolium, T. trialata, T. tuberosum subsp. silvestre, T. warmingianum subesp. warmingianum and T. willinkii to provide supplementary data for the delimitation of these species. The exine is tectate, perforate with reticulum supratectate, heterobrochate, angustimurate. Differences among the taxa are discussed, and a palynological key for the Argentinean species of Tropaeolum is presented. 23226708|In this study we aimed at testing two hypothesis about the biogeography of South America: (1) the existence of a marked discontinuity in the Andes of central Peru that separates the floras of northern and southern South America and (2) the occurrence of a more or less continuous semi-deciduous forest in South America during the Pleistocene. We conducted a search for different sources of published information on the flora (inventories) of 19 dry regions in South America as well as one region in Central America and another in North America. In order to analyze the data, we employed ordination and classification techniques, which give a more objective picture of the phytogeographical relationships. Additionally, we evaluated similarity scores between the regions. We found 1,421 woody and herbaceous genera for the 21 regions. These regions form two groups: one mostly in northern South America and the other one restricted to the southern half of the hemisphere. Within the latter, further subdivisions are discernible. Almost all the northern group is made up of tall, deciduous and semi-deciduous forest types. The southern group regions mainly range from very dry forests to desert scrub. Our results support the existence of a floristic discontinuity in relation to the drier flora of the Andes. The southern flora (from southern Peru to northern Argentina and Chile) constitutes a floristic group quite different from that of northern South America. The Chaco region, although more floristically related to the southern group, seems to constitute the connecting link between these northern and southern floras. Within the flora of southern South America, the coastal desert seems to be the connection between hot and cold semi-deserts. Our data also support the hypothesis of the existence of pleistocenic lowland forests in most parts of South America which, however, probably extended up to Mexico. En este estudio nos trazamos el objetivo de poner a prueba dos hiptesis sobre la biogeografa sudamericana: (1) la existencia de una marcada discontinuidad en los Andes del centro de Per que separa las floras del norte y sur de Sudamrica y (2) la existencia de un bosque semideciduo ms o menos continuo en Sudamrica durante el Pleistoceno. De esta manera, intentamos profundizar nuestra comprensin de las relaciones de la flora sudamericana. Realizamos una bsqueda de diferentes fuentes de informacin publicada sobre las floras (inventarios) de 19 regiones secas de Sudamrica as como una de Centroamrica y otra de Norteamrica. A fin de analizar los datos, empleamos tcnicas de ordenacin y clasificacin, las cuales brindan informacin ms objetiva sobre las relaciones fitogeogrficas. Adems, evaluamos ndices de similitud entre las regiones. Encontramos 1.421 gneros leosos y herbceos en las 21 regiones. stas forman dos grupos: uno mayormente en el norte de Sudamrica y el otro restringido a la mitad austral del continente. Dentro del ltimo se pueden distinguir ulteriores subdivisiones. Casi todo el grupo norteo est compuesto por bosques altos, semideciduos. Las regiones del grupo sureo van de bosques muy secos a matorral desrtico. Nuestros resultados apoyan la existencia de una discontinuidad florstica en relacin con la flora seca andina. La flora surea (del sur de Per al norte de Argentina y Chile) constituye un grupo florstico bastante diferente del presente en el norte de Sudamrica. El Chaco, aunque florsticamente ms afn al grupo del sur, parece constituir el nexo de conexin entre las floras nortea y surea. Dentro de la flora de Sudamrica, el desierto costero parece conectar a los semidesiertos calientes y fros. Nuestros datos tambin respaldan la hiptesis de la existencia de bosques pleistocnicos de tierras bajas en la mayor parte de Sudamrica. Posiblemente estos se extendieron incluso hasta Mxico.

23226841|Sporophyte morphology of Asplenium dareoides was reviewed, and development and morphology of its gamethophytes were studied for the first time from spore culture on mineral agar. Spores germinated 10 days after sown, and cultures reached a low percentage of germination (1 to 5%). Filamentous phase was initiated at 15 days. Gametophytes followed the Aspidium type of development, which leads to a hairy adult state, with cylindrical, marginal and superficial hairs. The morphological study of the sporophyte was based on foliar architecture, indument, epidermal patterns of pinnulae and indusium, spore size (mean values between 28.9 and 39.7 m) and spore morphology. Gametic chromosome number found was n = 72. Morphological and palynological characters of A. dareoides do not support the close relationship with A. flabellifolium, recently suggested from molecular data. Se revis la morfologa del esporfito y se estudi por primera vez el desarrollo y la morfologa del gametfito de Asplenium dareoides, a partir de esporas cultivadas en un medio nutritivo solidificado con agar. Las esporas germinaron a partir de los 10 das en un porcentaje muy bajo (1 al 5%). La fase filamentosa se inici a los 15 das. Los gametfitos siguieron un modelo de desarrollo de tipo Aspidium, y en la madurez presentaron pelos marginales y superficiales, cilndricos y algo ensanchados en el pice. El estudio morfolgico del esporfito se bas en la arquitectura foliar, el indumento, el modelo epidrmico de las pnnulas y de los indusios, y en la morfologa y el tamao de las esporas (longitud media de 28,9 a 39,7 m). 23222963|This is the second paper of a chemotaxonomic serial study of the subtribe Phaseolinae Benth. in Argentina, which comprises the generic complex Phaseolus-Vigna-Macroptilium. Chromatographic patterns of 8 species of the genus Vigna Savi were determined. Cluster analysis and ordination by principal coordinates analysis were applied to 34 chemical characters (flavonoids). Chemical evidence seems to support the taxonomic treatment proposed by Marchal, Mascherpa & Stainier (1978b) for the American Vigna. Argentinian species of the large subgenus Sigmoidotropis can be grouped according to the sections proposed by these authors. Taxonomic distance between V. peduncularis and V. luteola, the only pantropical representative of the typically African subgenus Vigna, suggested that the section Pedunculares of the subgenus Sigmoidotropis is the nexus between these two groups. Closely related to Sigmoidotropis, the subgenus Lasiospron shows a different affinity with the section Caracallae: V. longifolia is neared to V. hookeri (Caracallae-Sigmoidotropis) than V. lasiocarpa, the other species of Lasiospron. These results are in agreement with the morphological differences observed between both species, and suggest the possibility of introducing two sections in this group.

41825698|The presence of Oenanthe crocata in Buenos Aires province adds a new species to the adventive flora of Argentina and America. This is a toxic plant native from Europe; its toxicity is due to the presence, particularly in roots, of oenanthotoxin, a polyacetylenic alcohol. In its countries of origin, cases of poisoning and death of cattle and humans have been reported by the ingestion of the radical tubercles. The identification of the species was corroborated by comparing the nrDNA ITS region of the argentine material to all the nucleotide sequences available at GenBank, and by performing a maximum likelihood phylogenetic analysis o Oenanthe species. Moreover, Oenanthe divaricata is referred to the synonymy of O. crocata for the first time. This contribution describes and illustrates this new record, provides a distribution map and points the differential characters with other apioids that grow in Argentina. Se trata de una planta txica, originaria de Europa; la toxicidad se debe a la presencia, particularmente en las races, de enantotoxina, un alcohol poliacetilnico. En los pases de origen se han reportado casos de envenenamiento y muerte en ganado y seres humanos debido a la ingestin de tubrculos radicales. La identificacin de la especie se corrobor con la comparacin de la regin ITS de ADN nuclear ribosomal del material argentino con las secuencias nucleotdicas disponibles en GenBank y con un anlisis filogentico de mxima verosimilitud de las especies de Oenanthe. Adems se remite, por primera vez, Oenanthe divaricata a la sinonimia de O. crocata. En este aporte se describe e ilustra la nueva cita, se provee un mapa de distribucin y se sealan los caracteres diferenciales con otras apio ideas que crecen en Argentina.

darwiniana.3.1.5|We analyzed distributional data of vascular plants of the Patagonian province, in order to contribute to its biogeographic regionalization. 23222959|This paper deals with the anatomical leaf characters of Prosopis nigra (Grisebach) Hieronymus. The adaptive features of leaflets from plants growing under extreme conditions were studied. It was found that every individual analysed exhibits the same syndrome: xerophytism. Many characters are common to all specimens (reduction of leaf size, isolateral mesophyll, increase of pallisade chlorenchyma, high stomata density, presence of unicellular trichomes and tetrahedric cristals) and several others characters show a response to special environmental conditions (frequency of hairs and stomata in the upper and lower surface, cuticular thickness and leaflets breadth and length).

23228244|Artifact, ecofact and vegetal evidences recuperated from domestic and ceremonial deposits on village establishments of Early Formative (1500 - 400 b. C.), corresponding to the Tilocalar and Tarajne Phase, indicates that in gorges of the western slope of the Puna de Atacama (2500 - 3500 m) hunting practices were maintained in tandem with the consolidation of pastoralism practices. C- 500 b. C.) emphasizing the control of the piedmont oases. Evidencias de artefactos, ecofactos y vegetales provenientes de depsitos habitacionales y ceremoniales de asentamientos aldeanos del Formativo Temprano (1500  400 a. C.), correspondientes a la fase Tarajne y Tilocalar, indican que en las quebradas de la vertiente occidental de la Puna de Atacama (2500  3500 m s. m.) se mantuvieron las prcticas de caza mientras se consolidaba el pastoralismo. En este escenario la explotacin de recursos vegetales cultivados y silvestres fue complementaria y no decisiva para la ms temprana subsistencia durante el Formativo, de modo que la expansin agraria eclosion durante los siguientes eventos (400 a. C - 500 d. C.) enfatizndose el control de los oasis piemontanos.
23223195|Reproductive biology of Panicum spathellosum Dll was studied in two natural populations from Buenos Aires province, Argentina. In this species the inflorescences are composed of biflowered spikelets. The opening of the flowers is basipetal both in the principal and primary axis. Each spikelet has a lower staminate flower and an upper pistillate, chasmogamous and protogynous flower. The latter has also 3 staminodia. The stigmatic branches of the upper flower were exposed and 1 day later the staminodia arose. All the stigmas were exposed in approximately 8 days. Afterwards the stamens of each lower flower appeared and the entire exposition was completed in 3 days. It took nearly 13 days between the presentation of the stigmatic branches to the whole emergence of the androecium. Pollen grains had an 85.5 % of viability and contained starch, proteins and lipids as reserve substances. Some experiences were made to analyze the reproductive system of this species. It was proved that it is cross-pollinated and there was neither geitonogamy nor apomixis. A 60-81 % of caryopsis formation was obtained by cross-pollination. Caryopsis showed a 75 % of germination after sowing. A new type of "sexuality" within the spikelet of Panicum is here described. In P. spathellosum the lower flower is staminate and the upper one pistillate. The present study suggests that P. spathellosum has improved cross-pollination throughout diclinous monoecy and temporal separation of floral anthesis.

23225121|Prosopis ferox (Mimosaceae) is a spiny bush or tree, distributed in southern Bolivia and northwestern Argentina. Populations of P. ferox from Jujuy grow at high elevations (2400 to 3700 m). There is in this species a great morphological variability, especially in fruit dimensions and the number of seeds per fruit. These characteristics are important because of its use as forage. With the aim of analyzing the genetic variability among and within populations, a seed protein electrophoretic study of different accessions from the province of Jujuy was performed. The polipeptidic patterns obtained by SDS-PAGE showed a total of 26 bands. The analyzed populations could be distinguished by their protein profiles, and intrapopulation variability (polymorphism) was found in some of them, while others were monomorphic. The polymorphism indexes found in P. ferox were comparable to those previously found in P. ruscifolia. The genetic variability found among populations of P. ferox, using seed proteins analysis, suggests the existence of ecotypes. Prosopis ferox (Mimosaceae) es una especie arbustiva o arbrea espinosa que se distribuye desde el Sur de Bolivia hasta el noroeste de la Argentina. En la provincia de Jujuy se encuentra a grandes alturas (entre los 2400 y los 3700 m s.m.). Existe una gran variabilidad morfolgica, especialmente en cuanto a las dimensiones del fruto y la cantidad de semillas por fruto, ambas caractersticas importantes debido al uso de esta planta como forraje. Con el objeto de verificar si existe adems variabilidad gentica, se realiz un estudio electrofortico de protenas seminales de rboles procedentes de distintas localidades de la provincia de Jujuy. Los patrones polipeptdicos obtenidos por SDS-PAGE presentaron en total 26 bandas. Cada poblacin se caracteriz por sus patrones de presencia-ausencia de bandas, habindose encontrado variabilidad intrapoblacional (polimorfismo) en algunas de ellas, siendo otras genticamente homogneas. Los ndices polimrficos en poblaciones de P. ferox son comparables a los obtenidos previamente en P. ruscifolia. La variabilidad gentica interpoblacional hallada por medio del estudio electrofortico de las protenas seminales hace suponer la existencia de ecotipos.
23211924|The famous descriptive botanical work, Hortus Elthamensis of J. J. Dillenius, published in 1732, is one of the classicals of the last prelinnean period and an important sourcebook for Linnaeus' Species Plantarum. Notwithstanding this fact, the Hortus is up to the present practically unknown to Southamerican botanists. Studying the copy purchased for the library of the Instituto de Botnica Darwinion (San Isidro), the commentarist was struck by the large number of Southamerican, and especialy Argentine, species first described by Dillenius in his Hortus; species which, with few exceptions, Linnaeus renamed and published afterwards in his Species Plantarum (1753). The present commentary is an attempt to explain the importance of Dillenius and his notable botanical achievements, especially the Hortus Elthamensis, to modern Southamerican botanists, and to give them a guide for a thorough interpretation of his species and the accurate and beautiful plates of his work; The matters especially considered are: A rsum of the life of J. J. Dillenius (1684-1747) and his importance in botanical history; A brief characterization of the Hortus Elthamensis; An investigation of the collector who sent botanical specimens from Buenos Aires to Sherard and Dillenius in 1726-1727; this collector, a Dr. Mylam. was probably the first to accomplish such a task in Argentina. Thanks to Mylam and Dillenius no less than 13 Argentine species were described by Linnaeus, several of them as "bonariensis". In the whole, 40 species of the Argentine flora are described and excellently figured by Dillenius in his Hortus Elthamensis, and many others are of importance as type species of accepted genera; In a note (pages 377-378) the commentarist exposes his ideas about the four principal periods into which southamerican botanical history may be divided; There follows a commented list of the Argentine species of plants described by Dillenius, as well as other species and such cultivated ones as deserve more interest; Finally a complete interpretation of the 325 dillenian plates is presented, based on the important work of this kind by Druce and Vines (1907, pag. 157-184), but with many corrections now necessary in order to put the names in accordance with modern botanical nomenclature (International Code of 1952). This interpretation follows the order of Dillenius' plate numbers; An alphabetical index to all binomials cited and a bibliography about the subject complete the commentary. Reproductions of 16 dillenian plates include all the Argentine species of the Hortus Elthamensis and a few others, all of which are of botanical and artistical merits; the frontispiece is a pencil copy by the Argentine artist Nelly de Troncoso of the portrait published by Druce and Vines, 1907.

23223183|This paper deals with the interpretation, description and typological characterization of the inflorescences of the genera belonging to the tribe Verbeneae. These genera are: Glandularia Gmelin, Hierobotana Briquet, Junellia Moldenke, Tamonea Aublet, Verbena Linn and Urbania R. A. Philippi, all of them represented in South America. All the cases belong to the polytelic type of synflorescences. Florescences of almost all genera are dense spikes with decussate bracts. Only Tamonea has loose, spiciform racemes with disperse bracts. Floral prophylls are always absent. The heterothetic pleiobotryum is the most frequent branching form, present in Verbena, Glandularia and Hierobotana. Urbania and Junellia have monobotrya. Homothetic pleiobotrya characterize all species of Tamonea. Heteroblastic development of the branches can be observed in several species of Junellia. In these cases flowering can be restricted to the brachyblasts, a frequent specialization in woody plants. The heterothetic paniculiform pleiobotryum has been mentioned for several families of the Angiospermae as a primitive or central form, from which other forms derived through processes such as condensation, reduction and truncation. In Verbeneae this non specialized "paniculodium" is present in Verbena and Glandularia. Condensation of the florescences, to compose more or less functionally discrete subunits, appears in Verbena ser. Pachystachyae and Glandularia subgen. Paraglandularia. Reduction of the enriching zone occurs in Urbania and most Junellia species. Such reduction and decrease of flower number in the florescences could be related to the xerophyllous nature of these species. Truncation of the main florescence, such as the homogenization and racemization of the distal paracladia, have been produced in Tamonea giving rise to an homothetic pleioraceme. Tamonea shows few affinities with the remaining genera of Verbeneae. It differs from them in several inflorescence characters and gynoecial features previously studied by other authors. Because of all these characters, the place of this genus within the Verbenoideae should be reconsidered.

23223193|Calix glands were studied in the Atacama endemic Dinemandra ericoides Adr.Juss.(Malpighiaceae). Their anatomy and development are described for the first time. These oil-secreting glands (elaiophores) are anatomically different to other calix elaiophores known in the family and to other flower glands in the same species. The calix glands lack a preformed pores for oil release. The oil has to be exposed actively by the pollinator by the breakage of the cuticle. Form and position of the elaiophores are correlated to the mode of oil collection by species of Centris. The elaiophore of Dinemandra is compared in its anatomy to floral and extrafloral glands known in other members of the family.

23224214|The pollination biology of Habenaria parviflora (Orchidaceae: Habenariinae) was studied in Picinguaba, So Paulo State, southeastern Brazil in order to broaden our knowledge on the pollination biology and functional morphology of this terrestrial orchid genus. Plants are self-compatible but pollinator-dependent. The recorded pollinators were crane-fly (Diptera: Tipulidae) females and pyralid moths (Lepidoptera: Pyralidae). The pollination mechanism is the same regardless of the kind of pollinator: the pollinaria are fixed on the insect proboscis through the glove-like viscidium and removed when the insects leave the flowers. A pollinarium-carrying insect visiting another flower will brush the stigmatic surfaces and leave clumps of massulae, thus effecting pollination. This mode of pollinarium fixation is, as far as we know, reported for the first time for the genus Habenaria and is a clear consequence of viscidium's morphology. The involute, glove-like viscidium is a unique flower feature among neotropical Habenaria species. Flower features promoting cross-pollination are briefly discussed. This is also the first report of orchid pollination by crane-flies (Tipulidae) in the neotropics. Se estudi la biologia floral de Habenaria parviflora (Orchidaceae: Habenariinae) en Picinguaba, Estado de So Paulo, sudeste del Brasil, con la finalidad de incrementar el conocimiento sobre la biologa de la polinizacin y morfologa funcional de este gnero de Orqudeas terrestres. Estas plantas son autocompatibles, pero polinizador-dependientes. Los polinizadores registrados fueron hembras de Tiplidos (Diptera: Tipulidae) y polillas Pyralidae (Lepidoptera: Pyralidae). El mecanismo de polinizacin es el mismo, independientemente del tipo de polinizador: los polinarios se fijan a la probscide de los polinizadores a travs de su viscidio en forma de guante, y son removidos cuando los insectos dejan las flores. Cuando visita otra flor, un insecto que lleva polinrios los rozar contra las superfcies estigmticas, dejando acmulos de msulas, efectuando as la polinizacin. Hasta donde se sabe, este tipo de fijacin de polinarios es informado por primera vez para el gnero Habenaria y es una clara consecuencia de la morfologa del viscidio. El viscidio involuto, en forma de guante, es una caracterstica nica entre las especies neotropicales del gnero Habenaria. Los caracteres florales que favorecen la polinizacin cruzada son discutidos brevemente. ste es tambin hasta donde sabemos, el primer registro de polinizacin de orqudeas por Tiplidos (Tipulidae) en los neotrpicos.

The other eight taxa studied are polyploid and for them previous records exist; some of our results are new numbers for these taxa. Comparing the karyotypes among each other and with those which belong to closely related species, the relationship among them according to the intra- and interchromosomic variations (Fig. 7) was studied and the possible mechanisms responsible for the great chromosome variation in the genus are discussed.

23223220|Interspecific crossing was conducted between diploid cytotypes of two Paspalum species of the subgenus Anachyris in order to investigate their genomic relationship and to evaluate the possibilities of gene exchange between these species as a tool for their genetic improvement. Paspalum simplex was the female parent. The F hybrids showed stoloniferous growth habit which is characteristic of the male parent, P. procurrens. Regular meiotic behavior in the F hybrids demonstrated that both species have significant homology in their genomes. Embryological studies and seed production analysis under self-and cross-pollinated conditions demonstrated that the hybrids, like their parents, are sexual and self-sterile but cross-compatible. Both, the high level of crossabitity of the parents and the degree of fertility observed in F hybrids and in backcross progenies, indicated the feasibility of gene exchange between these species. Morphologically, P. simplex and P. procurrens are easily recognized as different species. Notwithstanding, the high crossability and the high level of fertility observed in hybrids and backcrossed progenies contrast with the lack of intermediate forms observed in herbaria and during field trips. Diploid cytotypes of both species seem to be restricted to western areas of the phytogeographic Chaco province, from Bolivia to Argentina. However, divergent evolution likely occurred in correlation with latitude and specific soil requirements. Diploid P. simplex was found in the southwestern Chaco province on clayey soil while P. procurrens was collected in the northwest of the province, growing on sandy soil.

23222560|In 11 species of Nicotiana representing 4 floral biotypes it is intended to determine if structural parameters of the nectaries (nectary volume, number and diameter of its stomata, nuclei diameter of the secretory cells, and nectary size relative to the whole ovary) show any reciprocal relationships or if they respond to the syndrome's physiological requirements. Though the chiropterophilous species exhibit, as can be expected, the largest nectaries, other syndromes do not have significantly different mean nectary volumes. Considering parameters other than nectary volume, species cannot be asigned to any particular syndrome based on nectary character. A correlation between nectary volume and size relative to the whole ovary does exist, probably pointing out a correspondence between the development of glandular and non-glandular parts of the ovary. On the other hand, nectary volume appears to be correlated with the size of the secretory cell nuclei and, among the sphingophilous species, also with the stomata diameter.

23215661|A second species of the verbenaceous genus Parodianthus Troncoso, 1941, is described from central Argentina (northermost Sierras de Crdoba): P. capillaris nov. spec. It differs from the type species, P. ilicifolius, by its low, creeping habit and the linear or filiform leaves. A special type of "exocristalliferous hairs" is described, common to both species and therefore adding to the generic diagnosis, in which a small linear crystal is present on the tip of the hair.
23216501|A taxonomic revision of the american Rhynchospora rugosa (Vahl) Gale sensu stricto and some close related species was made. The afro-asiatic-australian R. chinensis Nees et Meyen ex Nees, R. lavarum Gaudich. and R. brownii Roem. et Sch. were segregated from R. rugosa under which, different authors, considered them like subspecies or synonyms. R. brownii is a widespread pan-tropical species with a disjunct area. It is represented in a New World by its new subsp. americana. The majority of material mentioned as R. rugosa, from Africa, Asia and Australia is R. brownii subsp. brownii. The other american species which have been studied here are: Rhynchospora marisculus Nees, R. brasiliensis Bck., R. pungens Liebm. and R. barrosiana nov. spec. They all belong to sections Glaucae Clarke and Marisculae Kkenthal. Although R. jubata Liebm. and R. globularis (Chapm.) Small ex Gale are not related to R. rugosa, have also been described in this paper in order to make clear their identities. All the above mentioned species have been described and illustrated; the distribution of R. rugosa, R. brownii, R. barrosiana, R. marisculus and R. pungens is given on maps. Some observations about the achenes' epidermis are given too. Several critical and type specimens have been studied and arranged in a list of collectors. A key for this set of species is given.
23222563|The flowering periods, breeding systems and the isolation barriers in four species of Bromus (B. catharticus Vahl, B. brevis Ness., B. parodii Covas et Itria, and B. bonariensis Parodi et Cmara Hernndez) and five of its artificial interspecific hybrids were studied. The crossability (the feasibility of a determined interspecific cross) was calculated in each of the made breeding crosses. Furthermore, the importance of the breeding systems (Chasmogamy vs. cleistogamy) and the existence of pre or postcygotic isolation barriers in the speciation process are discussed. It is concluded that: B. catharticus would be the most advanced species with greater reproductive isolation and that it would possess derivative characteristics such as a short life cycle (annual or biannual), high percentage of cleistogamy and a very wide geographic distribution. Quite the contrary, B. bonariensis would be the most primitive one, being perennial, strictly chasmogamous and with a restricted geographical and ecological distribution. B. parodii (perennial) and B. brevis (shortly perennial or annual) would occupy an intermediate position. The biosystematic data presented here support the species rank for the studied entities.

23228353|Se estudiaron las modalidades de aprovechamiento de las plantas entre los Selknam de Tierra del Fuego (Argentina) y se presentan aqu los resultados obtenidos a partir del anlisis de los restos de madera carbonizada y sin carbonizar del sitito Ewan, ocupado a principios del siglo XX para la realizacin de un ritual de iniciacin. Los resultados permitieron una mejor comprensin de las estrategias de aprovechamiento de las plantas entre las sociedades cazadoras-recolectoras. La identificacin de las especies empleadas y el registro de las principales caractersticas morfomtricas permiti documentar el aprovechamiento del "ire" (Nothofagus antarctica). Esta especie, dominante en el entorno, fue utilizada para la construccin de la vivienda y como combustible. En ambos casos se seleccionaron troncos de forma y tamao adecuados. Los resultados del trabajo arqueobotnico y su confrontacin con los datos etnogrficos evidenciaron la importancia de los recursos vegetales dentro de la dinmica socioeconmica de este grupo humano. Los recursos vegetales, ms all de su rol alimentario, fueron relevantes en otros aspectos tales como la tecnologa, la construccin, el combustible y debieron constituir una ventaja considerable en el mbito de los bosques de la zona central de Tierra del Fuego. We studied the different ways of plant use among the Selknam from Tierra del Fuego (Argentina). In this paper we present the results obtained from the study of carbonized and non carbonized wood remains recovered at Ewan site, which was occupied at the beginning of the XXth century to celebrate an initiation ceremony. Results allowed a better understanding of the strategies of plant use in hunter-gatherer societies. The identification of the species used, and the analysis of their principal morphometric characteristics characterize the use of the "ire" (Nothofagus antarctica). This species, dominant in the surroundings, was used to build the dwelling as well as for fuel. For both uses, stems with suitable form and size were selected. Archaeobotanical results and their confrontation with the ethnographic data support the importance of vegetable resources within the socio-economic dynamics of the selknam society. Vegetable resources, beyond their use as food, were important in other aspects, such as technology, hut construction, fuel, and they certainly represented a considerable advantage in the area of the forests of the central zone of Tierra del Fuego.

The species are described and illustrated. A brief description of vegetative anatomy, pollen grains and, fruit and seed morphology is added. These anatomical and morphological characters contribute to differenciate the genus Bomarea from Alstroemeria.

23217317|Chromosome size, nuclear volume and DNA content in Bulnesia (Zygophyllaceae). Bulnesia comprises eight species, seven of them are diploid (2n = 26) and one (B. bonariensis) is polyploid (2n = 104) with regular meiotic chromosome behavior (52 bivalents). The diploids have significant differences in karyotype symmetry, total chromosome length (TCL), nuclear volume (NV) and DNA content. Those with highest (B. retama, B. chilensis) and lowest DNA content (B. sarmientoi) possess the most asymmetrical karyotypes and several morphological and physiological specializations. Apparently and, contrary to other groups, in Bulnesia both modifications of DNA content (increase, decrease) would occur together and would have been accompanied with drastic alterations of the karyotype. Disjunct populations of B. retama from Ica (Per) and La Rioja (Argentina) were compared and no differences were found in their total chromosome length (TCL) and other karyotype parameters despite small but significant differences in DNA content, seed size and seed proteins patterns found by previous authors. Both populations have a small metacentric pair of chromosomes, devoid of heterochromatin, and this suggests that heterochromatin is not distributed at random. The ratio DNA content/NV is lower in the octoploid B. bonariensis than in the diploids; this could indicate a relatively high nuclear volume in the octoploid. NV is positively correlated with TCL (r = 0.96) and with DNA content (r = 0.86). DNA content and TCL also show positive correlation (r = 0.72), although B. retama and B. chilensis show a higher DNA content than expected, on the basis of their respective TCL values. This could be due to the fact that both species have the highest percentage of heterochromatin (demostrated by C-banding). The tighter heterochromatin coiling may explain the higher DNA content per unit of chromosome length of these two species. High DNA content could produce rapid growth because fewer cells are required to make up a given volume of tissue. This could be highly adaptive in xeric environments where B. retama and B. chilensis are found. Bulnesia comprende ocho especies, siete diploides (2n = 26) y una poliploide (B. bonariensis, 2n = 104) con comportamiento meitico regular (52 bivalentes). Los diploides poseen diferencias significativas en simetra del cariotipo, longitud cromosmica total (TCL), volumen nuclear (NV) y contenido de ADN. Las especies con mayor (B. retama, B. chilensis) y menor contenido de ADN (B. sarmientoi) poseen diversas especializaciones morfolgicas y fisiolgicas y muestran los cariotipos ms asimtricos del gnero. A diferencia de otros grupos, en Bulnesia se habran producido disminucin y aumento en el contenido de ADN, acompaadas de drsticas alteraciones del cariotipo. Se compararon dos poblaciones disyuntas de B. retama de Ica (Per) y La Rioja (Argentina), que no presentaron diferencias en la longitud del cariotipo y otros parmetros cariotpicos a pesar de que en estudios anteriores de otros autores se han encontrado pequeas pero significativas diferencias en el contenido de ADN, tamao de la semilla y protenas seminales. Ambas poblaciones poseen un par de cromosomas pequeos metacntricos desprovistos de heterocromatina, lo cual indicara que la heterocromatina no estara distribuida al azar. La relacin contenido de ADN/volumen nuclear es menor en el octoploide B. bonariensis que en los diploides; esto podra indicar un volumen relativamente mayor en el octoploide. El volumen nuclear est positivamente correlacionado con la longitud total de los cromosomas (r = 0,96) y con el contenido de ADN (r = 0,86). El contenido de ADN y la longitud total de los cromosomas muestran una correlacin positiva (r = 0,72), aunque B. retama y B. chilensis poseen mayor contenido de ADN que el esperado sobre la base de sus respectivas longitudes cromosmicas. Esto se debera a que ambas especies tienen el mayor porcentaje de heterocromatina, lo cual fue demostrado por tcnicas de bandeo C. El mayor contenido de ADN por unidad de longitud cromosmica se explicara por la mayor espiralizacin que posee la heterocromatina. Un alto contenido de ADN podra producir crecimiento rpido debido a que un volumen dado de tejido se alcanza con un menor nmero de clulas. Esto podra ser altamente adaptativo en ambientes xricos donde se encuentran B. retama y B. chilensis.
23213050|Contribution to the knowledge of the neotropical "Salviniaceae".  I. Salvinia oblongifolia Martius. 23223224|The pollen of Paspalum unispicatum (Scribn. et Mer.) Nash shows some anomalous types, such as: dyads and tetrads with partially divided monads, inaperturates, anomalous monoaperturates, biaperturates and triaperturates grains. In this paper the morphometric features of "normal" and anomalous pollen grains were compared, and their potential viability tested with aceto-carmine coloration. A comparative analysis of the pollen of upper and lower flowers showed that the abnormalities are independent of the position of the flowers. These anomalous types were also found in Paspalum decumbens Rottb., and Paspalum urvillei Steud. The anomalous pollen grains probably result from meiotic chromosome abnormalities in these tetraploid species.
23225101|The Lower Delta of Paran river in Buenos Aires is a wide costal freshwater wetland of 2,071 km2. In this study, native, herbaceous plant communities of the Lower Delta islands were identified and described in order to propose a conceptual model for the interpretation of the spatial distribution of plant communities. The main hypothesis was that the hydrological regime and the landscape pattern are key factors determining the regional heterogeneity and conditioning the presence and abundance of species and plant communities. Values of cover-abundance for each species were estimated in 177 plots placed in 21 sites in the region. Soil samples were also taken. A total of 62 species and 19 plant communities were identified. Plant communities form a heterogeneous mosaic and they are characterized by a low species richness and the dominance of few graminoid type plants and even less representation of broadleaf plants. The presence and distribution of plant communities in the area are determined by two main factors: (1) the water permanence related to the position along the topographic gradient, and (2) the origin and dynamical action of the water supply, both affected mainly by the connection with the main water channels and the location of plots in relation to the regional gradient of the fluvial estuary. El sector bonaerense del Bajo Delta del Ro Paran conforma un extenso humedal costero de agua dulce sometido a mareas (2.700 km2). El presente trabajo se propuso identificar y describir las comunidades de herbceas nativas de las islas y proponer un modelo conceptual que permita interpretar la expresin espacial de las mismas. Se parti de la hiptesis de que el rgimen hidrolgico y el patrn de paisaje son los factores principales que determinan la heterogeneidad de la regin y condicionan la presencia y abundancia de las especies y comunidades vegetales. En 21 sitios de muestreo se realizaron un total de 177 censos en los que se identificaron 62 especies, se estim la abundancia-cobertura por especie y se tomaron muestras de suelo. Se delimitaron 19 comunidades vegetales que conforman un mosaico heterogneo, se caracterizan por su baja riqueza especfica y la dominancia de unas pocas especies de tipo graminoide y en menor medida de latifoliadas. La presencia diferencial de las comunidades en la regin y su composicin especfica se relacion con dos factores principales de variacin. El primero fue la permanencia del agua relacionado con la posicin topogrfica de los censos, el segundo correspondi al grado de conexin de las comunidades con los cursos de agua principales y por su localizacin con relacin al macrogradiente de influencia fluvial-esturica regional.
23230217|Although Grewioideae is known as the only stenopalynous subfamily of Malvaceae, previous published pollen analyses suggest morphological variation. To test if that structural variation could have taxonomic value, pollen morphology of 16 species of the genera Corchorus, Heliocarpus, Luehea, Mollia and Triumfetta (Malvaceae, Grewioideae) distributed in southern South America was analysed by light and scanning electron microscopy. Pollen grains are 3-zonocolporate, isopolar, radially symmetrical, subspheroidal to prolate, and medium to large in size. Exine sculpture varies from a bireticulate reticulum with perforated lumina to densely tectate-rugulate or tectate-microreticulate. Pollen morphological characteristics from light microscopy were used in a multivariate analysis to assess variation within and among the genera. Principal components analyses (PCA) clearly separate five groups based on pollen shape and size, colpus length, endoaperture height and width, and exine thickness. The species here studied share the Grewia pollen type, like most species of Grewioideae and Byttnerioideae, but the palynological characters analyzed have little taxonomic value at genus or species level. Aunque Grewioideae es conocida como la nica subfamilia estenopalnica de Malvaceae, los anlisis de polen publicados sugieren una variacin morfolgica. Para comprobar si la variacin estructural podra tener valor taxonmico, la morfologa del polen de 16 especies de los gneros Corchorus, Heliocarpus, Luehea, Mollia y Triumfetta (Malvaceae, Grewioideae) distribuidas en la regin austral de Amrica del Sur fue analizada con microscopa ptica y electrnica de barrido. Los granos de polen son 3-zonocolporados, isopolares, radiosimtricos, subesferoidales a prolatos y de tamao mediano a grande. La escultura de la exina vara desde un birretculo con perforaciones en el lumen a un tectum densamente rugulado o microrreticulado. Los caracteres morfolgicos de polen obtenidos con microscopio ptico fueron utilizados en un anlisis multivariado para evaluar la variabilidad dentro y entre los gneros. El anlisis de componentes principales (PCA) permiti diferenciar cinco grupos sobre la base de forma y tamao del grano, largo del colpo, ancho y alto de la endoabertura y espesor de la exina. Las especies estudiadas comparten el polen tipo Grewia caracterstico de la mayora de las especies de Grewioideae y Byttnerioideae, pero los caracteres polnicos analizados son de reducido valor diagnstico a nivel genrico y/o especfico.

23223875|The genus Baccharis is represented in Argentina by 96 species, the infrageneric classification of which is presented in this paper. A succinct summary of the history of Baccharis infrageneric taxonomy is provided. The 96 Argentine species are placed into 15 sections: Angustifoliae, Aristidentes, Baccharis, Caulopterae, Cuneifoliae, Cylindricae, Discolores, Molinae, Nitidae, Oblongifoliae, Paniculatae, Pedicellatae, Pseudobaccharis, Subliguliflorae -sect. nov.- and Trinervatae. These sections are briefly described, and a key to differentiate them is given. Twelve out of the 96 species are positioned into the infrageneric classification system for the first time, whereas 42 species which had been previously classified are here relocated to other sections. Twenty-two generic, subgeneric, sectional and subsectional names are considered as new synonyms. The relationships among the sections are discussed. El gnero Baccharis se halla representado en la Argentina por 96 especies, cuya clasificacin infragenrica se estudia en este artculo. Se realiza una breve revisin de la historia de la taxonoma infragenrica de Baccharis. Las especies argentinas son ubicadas en 15 secciones: Angustifoliae, Aristidentes, Baccharis, Caulopterae, Cuneifoliae, Cylindricae, Discolores, Molinae, Nitidae, Oblongifoliae, Paniculatae, Pedicellatae, Pseudobaccharis, Subliguliflorae -sect. nov.- y Trinervatae. Se describe brevemente cada una de estas secciones, y se provee una clave que permite diferenciarlas. Doce de las 96 especies son colocadas por primera vez dentro del sistema de clasificacin infragenrica; en tanto otras 42, que ya haban sido clasificadas previamente, son reubicadas en otras secciones. Son considerados como nuevos sinnimos 22 nombres de gneros, subgneros, secciones y subsecciones. Se discuten las relaciones entre las secciones.
23215602|Studies on in-vitro germination of pollen grains and pollen tube growth in Arachis aff. villosa, A. pintoi, A. glabrata, A. aff. benthamii and A. lignosa have been made. The "hanging drop" method was used. The effect of sucrose, maltose, glucose and boric acid was studied in various concentrations. The best germinative substratum was composed of sucrose (15-20 %) + boric acid (100 ppm + agar 0,5 %). In order to obtain maximum results, pollen grains should remain between 6 to 12 hours in the germinator. Longevity on the grains in natural condition durings the complete day in which the dehiscence of the anthers is produced, was also studied.

23226842|A surface spreading and air-drying method to obtain for the first time the somatic karyotype of a population of Guazuma ulmifolia var. ulmifolia was used. 23215741|The paper consists of a floristic and estructural description of a forest stand of Nothofagus dombeyi ("coihue") in the Lago Gutirrez area in the southern andean region of Argentina. Five strata are recognized: two tree layers, a tall shrub-small tree stratum, a small shrub stratum and a herbaceous one. Plant species per strata are listed with its importance values. Trees more than 10 cm dbh, were studied by quarter point technique; saplings, seedlings, shrubs and herbs were recorded in frequency and density quadrats. A diametric classes pyramid of N. dombeyi is made to analyze the population structure of the dominant tree, and an attempt is made to explain the dynamical aspects of this population, the abiotic factors (light intensity, summer drought, aridization of climate) that affect it and the role of the species in the forests where it occurs.

23230186|We evaluated the effect that nectar guides have on the efficiency in pollination of flowers in Alstroemeria aurea (Alstroemeriaceae), a herbaceous, xenogamous plant, which blooms in temperate forests of southern South America. The flowers were manipulated in situ and subjected to three treatments: flowers with nectar guides (FCG, not manipulated, control); flowers without nectar guides (FSG, flowers with nectar guides that were obscured) and control-control (CC, flowers in which the nectariferous tepals were covered by other nectariferous tepals to test the possible effect of double petals). The efficiency of pollination was evaluated as a function of visitation frequency, quantity of pollen deposited on the stigmas of visited flowers and quantity of accumulated nectar. Our results show that the absence of nectar guides significantly affected the efficiency of visits by pollinators ( = 18.97, df: 2, p <<0.004) the quantity of pollen grains deposited on stigmas (F = 19.39; Gl: 2, p <<0.0001) and the accumulated volume of nectar (F = 12.87, df: 2, p <<0.005). The FSG were less visited, received fewer pollen grains per stigma and had a higher volume of accumulated nectar, unlike the FCG and CC. About 90% of all floral visits were accomplished by Bombus ruderathus (84.11%) and B. dahlbomii (8.41 %), that possess well developed sensory perception (responding to nectar guide patterns in the flowers). We propose that the absence of nectar guides from the flowers of A. aurea, eliminated orientation patterns assisting visitors, indicating access to rewards, and consequently affected their pollination. Evaluamos el efecto de las guas de nctar sobre la eficiencia de polinizacin en las flores de Alstroemeria aurea (Alstroemeriaceae), una planta herbcea xengama, que florece en los bosques templados del sur de Sudamrica. Las flores fueron manipuladas "in situ" y sometidas a tres tratamientos: flores con guas (FCG, no manipuladas, control); flores sin guas (FSG, flores a las que se les cubrieron las guas) y control-control (CC, flores a las que se les cubrieron los tpalos nectarferos con otros tpalos nectarferos, evitando el posible efecto del doble ptalo). La eficiencia de polinizacin fue evaluada en funcin de la frecuencia de las visitas, la cantidad de polen depositado en los estigmas y la cantidad de nctar acumulado en las flores visitadas. Nuestros resultados demostraron que la ausencia de las guas de nctar afect de manera significativa la eficiencia de visitas de los polinizadores ( = 18.97; gl: 2; p<< 0.004), la cantidad de granos de polen depositados sobre los estigmas (F= 19.39; gl: 2; p<< 0.0001) y el volumen de nctar acumulado (F= 12.87; gl: 2; p<< 0.005). Las FSG fueron menos visitadas, obtuvieron menor cantidad de granos de polen por estigma y presentaron mayor volumen de nctar acumulado, a diferencia de las FCG y CC. Cerca del 90% de todas las visitas florales fueron realizadas por las especies Bombus ruderathus (84.11%) y B. dahlbomii (8.41%), consideradas especies con alto desarrollo sensorial, que responden a los patrones de las guas de nctar en las flores. Proponemos que la ausencia de las guas de nctar de las flores de A. aurea, elimin los patrones de orientacin que serva a los visitantes para indicar el acceso a la recompensa, y en consecuencia afect su polinizacin.
23227144|A new species of Uncinia (Cyperaceae), U. austroamericana, is described and illustrated from austral South America and from the Tristan da Cunha archipelago in the south-Atlantic Ocean. 23223242|The leaf architecture of Tipuana Benth., Cascaronia Griseb. and Bergeronia Micheli, is described and compared, evaluating the importance of these foliar characters in their taxonomy. Each genus presents characters that allow their differentiation: in Tipuana tipu (Benth.) Kuntze, the basal pairs of secondary veins have an eucamptodromous model, with simple intersecondary veins which move through the intercostal area towards the margin; the last marginal venation is looped. In Cascaronia astragalina Griseb., secondary veins have capillary thickness and the last marginal venation is incomplete. In Bergeronia sericea Micheli, there are abaxial prominent secondary veins, and tertiary veins emerging in rigth angles; the last marginal venation is fimbrated. The venation characters observed are similar to those previously cited for different genera of Dalbergieae and some cited in other tribes of Papilionoideae. However, they cannot define, for themselves, the taxonomic position of the three genera and must be considered together with other morphological and reproductive structures.

23228250|The most recent studies about the genus Tabebuia and Handroanthus recognize two and six native species in Argentina, and one exotic cultivated species of Handroanthus in urban streets. 23218906|Morphological and histochemical studies on the starch grain of Dioscorea campestris Griseb. (DIOSCOREACEAE). The Pizzolato test for calcium oxalate crystals was applied to Dioscorea campestris. A blackening of intraamylar localization was obtained with this technique (silver nitrate and concentrated hydrogen peroxide). Nevertheless, the X-ray diffraction and crystal analysis were both negative for calcium oxalate and calcium respectively. The starch have single or semicompound granules, a great part of them have pores or holes in distal position with respect to the hilar region: sometimes there are 2 pores, with one of them in lateral position. The unmodified granules show the granule surface free from pores or cracks. The hole is supposed to be a conical crater erosion, a feature which is typical of the particular kind of starch granules highly resistant to liquefying -amylase; the central portion is extensively affected as the erosion is in advance. The blackening produced by the positive Pizzolato test is related to that central portion of the damaged grains. Microchemical tests with Fehling solution also revealed high concentrations of reducing sugars at these sites. It is possible that the silver reaction is due to the free reducing groups produced by hydrolysis of the internal central core, giving a false positive test for crystals. The X-ray diffraction powder diagrams obtained, yield data for a crystalline structure of amylose corresponding to the A-type starch.

23230214|Vernonia setososquamosa (Asteraceae, Vernonieae) has been considered by several authors as a synonym of V. remotiflora, as a variety of this taxon or a quite different, independent species. We analyzed chromosome and pollen morphology of both entities looking for information to clarify the status of V. setososquamosa. The latter taxon showed a somatic chromosome number of 2n=2x=30 with the karyotype composed of 22m + 6sm + 2st, while on the other hand V. remotiflora presented 2n=2x=28 and a karyotype formula having 22m + 4sm + 2st. The pollen of both entities was tricolporate, echinolophate, with lacunae disposed in a regular pattern; however, V. setososquamosa presented polar lacunae, whereas V. remotiflora did not. The results support the treatment of V. setososquamosa and V. remotiflora as different species. 23218071|A taxonomic and nomenclatural assessment of species of the genera Bartramia, Bartramidula and Conostomum from the Andean-Patagonian region as well as from antarctic and subantarctic areas is presented, drawing attention to the characters of taxonomic value, both at generic and specific level. Spore morphology observed by SEM proved to be a relevant feature for the distinction of the genera here studied. Spore ornamentation together with the detailed structure of leaf cross-section were found to be useful characters at specific and varietal level. These characters have helped in the circumscription of species, resulting in a substantial reduction in the number of taxa known for the area. A short description of the family and a key to all the genera of Bartramiaceae found in the region, integrate this study with three previously published papers (Matteri 1968, 1973, 1981). The 3 genera, 8 species and 1 variety are treated in a synoptic style, including keys, brief descriptions with the local synonymy, together with useful taxonomic notes and data on habitat and distribution.

23217334|Embryological studies in Desfontainia spinosa (Desfontainiaceae). This paper deals with the embryology of D. spinosa Ruiz et Pav.; the following are the main conclusions: A) Embryological conclusions:  Anther walls: Its development corresponds to an archaic form within the basic type of Davis (1966), in which there are three or four middle layers. The tapetum is of the secretory type and the endothecium cells develop U-form thickenings on the radial walls and internal tangential wall.  Microsporogenesis: There is a simultaneous formation of tetrahedral tetrads.  Ovule: It is anatropous, crassinucellate and has only one integument. The internal epidermis of the integument differentiates itself in an endothelium. At the moment of anthesis, transfer cells stem from the endothelium and underlying layers, in the micropilar region.  Growth of the pollen tube and fertilization: The growth of the pollen tubes starts in the epidermis of the stigma, going through the transmiting tissue of the style and ovary and finally, the secretory epidermis of the placenta and funicle. Several callose plugs are formed in its way. The fertilization is porogamous; the pollen tube discharges inside one of the synergids.  Endosperm: The development of the endosperm corresponds to cellular megatype, isopolar type, longitudinal subtype, i. e. 1211 according to the EODP system (Di Fulvio, 1983). At the beginning of the proembryo's globular phase, the cells of the micropylar and chalazal regions develops haustorial characteristics and do not contain reserve materials. These cells will be digested by the embryo during development and the same occurs with the cells of the central zone. The rest of the tissues, with food reserves identified as protein bodies, persists in the completely developed seed.  Episperm: It is derived from the external epidermis of the ovule and is represented by a layer of sclereids whose radial and internal tangential wall are thickened, lignified and profusely pitted. The external tangential walls formed by pectic compounds, are also thickened. Around the micropyle there is also a bundle of sclereids which have evenly thickened, lignified walls with numerous pits. The episperm is scarcely known in the Loganiaceae but, morphologically, the sclereid layer of D. spinosa resembles the one described in Fagraea. B) Taxonomical conclusions: As Loganiaceae s. l. is one of the tropical families whose embryology is not very well known it is still premature to try to arrive to final conclusions. Nevertheless, the results obtained in this work indicate that: 1. The characteristics of cellular endospermogenesis and the presence of an endothelium would justify the separation of Desfontainia from Loganiaceae s. str. As regards the isopolar type of endospermogenesis, it coincides with Polypremum (Buddlejaceae) and Mitrasacme (Loganiaceae). The nature of the cellular endospermogenesis is different to Buddleja where only the micropylar cell contributes to the development of the storage tissue and the other cell forms 4 chalazal haustoria. On the other hand, the isopolar type of endospermogenesis and the presence of endothelium are characteristics of the families with cellular endosperm belonging to the order Solanales; for that reason Polypremum, Mitrasacme and Desfontainia are, probably, better referred to the Solanales rather than to the Gentianales or Scrophulariales. 2. As Desfontainia posseses many morphological differences with any of the families included by Cronquist in Solanales, it only could be incorporated in this order as an independent family.

23612318|Rare and narrowly endemic species are more vulnerable to extinction due to their restricted geographical distribution. the genus Petunia has 14 species and most of them are endemic to a restricted area. Four Petunia species that grow in Southern Brazil were studied: P. bonjardinensis, P. reitzii, P. integrifolia subsp. depauperata, and P. exserta. We presented a preliminary study on the genetic diversity of five populations of Petunia, using allozyme markers. For the genetic analyses, allozyme electrophoresis was carried out and eight enzyme systems were reliably scored. Standard measures of allozyme diversity were calculated. The highest genetic diversity and the highest fixation index was found in the two studied populations of P. bonjardinensis (P = 90, p = 2.2 and 1.9, e = 0.33 and 0.30, F = 0.31 and 0.27); this species occurs in small isolated patches, that may restrict gene flow among populations. Petunia reitzii showed the second highest genetic diversity values (P = 78, p = 1.78, e = 0.28), and Petunia integrifolia subsp. depauperata showed moderate values (P = 40, p = 1.4 and e = 0.11). Petunia exserta did not show any polymorphic locus. Our results show the urgency of preserving the studied population of P. exserta that did not show any allozyme variation and occurs in a very particular and threatened habitat. Las especies raras y estrictamente endmicas son ms vulnerables a la extincin debido a su distribucin geogrfica restringida. El genero Petunia tiene 14 especies y la mayora de ellas son endmicas de reas restringidas. Se presenta un estudio preliminar de la diversidad gentica de cinco poblaciones de Petunia utilizando marcadores de alozimas. Para los anlisis de electroforesis de alozimas se llevaron a cabo ocho sistemas enzimticos. Se calcularon las medidas estndar de diversidad. La mayor diversidad gentica y tambin el ndice de fijacin ms alto se encontr en las dos poblaciones estudiadas de P. bonjardinensis (P = 90, p = 2.2 y 1.9, e = 0.33 y 0.30, F = 0.31 y 0.27); esta especie se encuentra en pequeas zonas aisladas entre s, lo que puede dificultar el flujo gnico interpoblacional. Petunia exserta no mostr loci polimrficos. 23216474|The Life-history of two species of Brown Algae, a croustaceous (Ralfsioid) and Scytosiphon lomentaria (Lyngbye) Link, from Puerto Deseado (Patagonia Argentina), has been followed in culture. Cultures from swarmspores of unilocular sporangia of "Ralfsia sp." in nature, develop into haplostichous disc. These crusts form polistichous erect fronds (Scytosiphon phase) similar to Scytosiphon pigmaeus Reinke, with plurilocular organs at maturity. Its zoospores give rise to discoid thalli identical to mother plant. The zoospores of Scytosiphon lomentaria develop parthenogenetically into small haplostichous crustaceous discs or filamentous prothalli giving off erect fronds with plurilocular organs. This species exhibits that there is no alternation of dimorphic generations in our cultures.
