23223889|Nuptial nectary characteristics were investigated in 37 taxa of Bignoniaceae. A nuptial nectary associated to the floral axis was found in all species. Two main types can be distinguished according to their degree of development and functionality: 1) vestigial and non-secretory and 2) well-developed and secretory. The former is characteristic of Clytostoma spp., while the latter is found in the remaining species. Two subvarieties of the secretory type of nectary can be discerned according to their position and shape: 1) annular, found in Adenocalymma, Amphilophium, Anemopaegma, Arrabidaea, Dolichandra, Eccremocarpus, Macfadyena, Melloa, Pithecoctenium, Tabebuia, and Tecoma, and 2) cylindrical, found in Argylia, Cuspidaria, Jacaranda, Mansoa, Parabignonia, Pyrostegia, and Tynnanthus. Anatomically, two tissues are distinguished: 1) a single-layered epidermis covered by a cuticle and a variable number of stomata, and 2) a secretory tissue composed of compactly arranged parenchyma cells. Both nectary size and nectary/ovary ratio were usually larger in lianas (Bignonieae) than in trees (Tecomeae). Nectary type proved to be consistent among species of same genus but not among genera of same tribe. Nectary features such as vascularization, presence of trichomes and nectary type were constant within the analyzed species and therefore have a reliable taxonomic value. Se investigaron las caractersticas de los nectarios florales en 37 especies de Bignoniaceae. Se encontr un nectario nupcial asociado al eje floral en todas las especies, pudindose distinguir dos tipos principales de acuerdo a su grado de desarrollo y funcionalidad: 1) vestigial y no secretor y 2) bien desarrollado y secretor. El primero es caracterstico de las especies de Clytostoma mientras que el segundo est presente en el resto de las especies estudiadas. Dos variedades del tipo secretor pueden discernirse de acuerdo a su posicin y forma: 1) anular, encontrado en Adenocalymma, Amphilophium, Anemopaegma, Arrabidaea, Dolichandra, Eccremocarpus, Macfadyena, Melloa, Pithecoctenium, Tabebuia, y Tecoma y 2) cilndrico, presente en Argylia, Cuspidaria, Jacaranda, Mansoa, Parabignonia, Pyrostegia, y Tynnanthus. Anatmicamente se distinguen dos tejidos: 1) una epidermis monoestratificada, cubierta por una cutcula y con un nmero variable de estomas y 2) un tejido secretor compuesto por clulas parenquimticas dispuestas en forma compacta. Tanto el tamao del nectario como la relacin nectario/ovario fue usualmente ms grande en lianas (Bignoniaceae) que en rboles (Tecomeae). El tipo de nectario fue invariable entre las especies de un mismo gnero, pero no as entre los gneros de una misma tribu. Las caractersticas de los nectarios analizados en este estudio como la vascularizacin, la presencia de tricomas y el tipo de nectario fueron constantes en las especies analizadas, adquiriendo por lo tanto un importante valor taxonmico.
23216514|Se da a conocer en este trabajo la presencia de estomas paralelocticos en las epidermis foliares de las 4 especies del gnero sudamericano Mora: M. excelsa, M. paraensis, M. gongrijpii y M. megistosperma. Este tipo se encuentra junto al paractico con el que est relacionado ontogenticamente en una proporcin variable en las distintas especies; la autora en un trabajo anterior los haba incluido en este ltimo tipo. Se caracterizan los estomas paralelocticos por poseer clulas subsidiarias en forma de "C" que alternan a cada lado de las oclusivas, decreciendo su tamao de afuera hacia adentro. En Mora existen slo 3 clulas subsidiarias, caso poco frecuente ya que por lo comn poseen 4. En este estoma hay una estrecha relacin entre ontogenia y estado adulto ya que la observacin de este ltimo permite deducir su desarrollo, por lo que es posible hacer correlaciones con tipos menos complejos de similar ontogenia inicial y ello puede tener importancia desde un punto de vista taxonmico. La presente es la segunda referencia a este tipo estomtico en las Leguminosas-Cesalpinioideas; en la misma se han hecho adems algunas consideraciones acerca de la terminologa existente en los estomas de las dicotiledneas. Parallelocytic stomata are recorded for the leaf epidermis of the 4 species of the South American genus Mora: M. excelsa, M. paraensis, M. gongrijpii y M. megistosperma. They were previously described by the author as paracytic in a former paper. Both types, which are related on developmental basis, are present in variable number according to the species. The parallelocytic stoma possesses a series of alternating, increasingly larger "C"-shaped cells as one proceeds from the guard cells outward, surrounding the latter; in Mora there are a rather unusual number of 3 subsidiary cells, instead of 4. In this type there is a close correlation between ontogeny and adult pattern, being possible therefore to establish relations with less complex types of stomata of similar initial ontogeny what could be important from the taxonomic point of view. The present is the second reference of parallelocytic stomata for the Leguminosae-Caesalpinioideae. Considerations about the complex terminology on dicots stomata are also given.

23222974|Corethron criophilum Castracane was grown under different conditions of daylength and light intensity in order to analyse the species response in terms of duplication rate, cell volume and the ratio surface/volume (S/V). The species was isolated from net samples collected in Baha Paraso (64 48 S - 62 23 W) Antarctica, during March 1989. Differences in the duplication rate were evident between the three photoperiods selected at higher light intensities (60 and 140 E m. sec). At low intensities (0,35 E. m. sec) we did not observe differences in growth between the photoperiods, and the duplication rate was close to zero. Data on cell volume and S/V ratio of the cell population under different growth conditions are presented. An increment in the higher relative surface (S/V) population fraction, in coincidence with shorter photoperiods was observed. On this basis, the following hypothesis to be tested is proposed: If the light conditions become worse, the population reacts producing a differential growth of the cells having a smaller volume and a bigger relative surface.

23223918|Inflorescences of Zizaniopsis bonariensis (Balansa & Poitr.) Speg. and Z. villanensis Quarn were typologically studied. The inflorescences of these species are polytelic; a main florescence and a paracladial zone were noticed. The last one consists of a reduced subzone of short paraclades and a well developed subzone of long paraclades. There is also an important variation in the sexuality of the florescences. In Z. bonariensis the main florescence and the coflorescences of the paraclades of higher order are represented by a pistillate spikelet whereas the coflorescences from lower order paraclades are staminate spikelets. A high concentration of staminate florescences at the proximal regions of the inflorescence is also seen. Zizaniopsis villanensis has a predominance of staminate florescences at a distal position of the inflorescence, with the pistillate ones at the base of the inflorescence. Se estudiaron tipolgicamente las inflorescencias en Zizaniopsis bonariensis (Balansa & Poitr.) Speg. y Z. villanensis Quarn. En ambas especies la inflorescencia es politlica y est constituida por una florescencia principal y por una zona paracladial. En esta ltima se pueden reconocer una subzona de paracladios cortos reducida y una subzona de paracladios largos muy desarrollada. Se presenta tambin una variacin importante en la esporidad de las florescencias. En Z. bonariensis la florescencia principal y las coflorescencias de los paracladios de orden principal estn representados por espiguillas pistiladas, mientras que las coflorescencias de los paracladios de orden inferior son espiguillas estaminadas. Una ms alta concentracin de florescencias estaminadas se observa en la regin proximal de la inflorescencia. En tanto que, Z. villanensis presenta una mayor proporcin de florescencias estaminadas en la regin distal de la inflorescencia con florescencias pistiladas en las partes proximales de la inflorescencia.

23227931|Achenes of the thirty seven Valeriana species from the southern Andes were described, illustrated and compared by scanning electron microscopy and stereomicroscopy. It is shown that the detailed analysis of the achenes provides excellent taxonomic characters (e.g. fruit shape, sterile locules development, fruit-coat surface) to distinguish among the southern Argentina and Chile taxa. Results are contrasted with the systematics of this genus. Four informal groups are established, and a key to the South-Andean species of Valeriana is provided, based on achene morphology. Se describen, ilustran y comparan los aquenios de 37 especies de Valeriana de los Andes australes, a travs de microscopa electrnica de barrido (MEB) y estereomicroscopa. Se muestra que el anlisis detallado de los aquenios provee excelentes caracteres taxonmicos (forma del fruto, grado de desarrollo de los lculos estriles y superficie del fruto) que permiten separar los taxones de Argentina y Chile austral. Los resultados son contrastados con la sistemtica del gnero. Se definen cuatro grupos informales, y se presenta una clave para identificar las especies andinas de Valeriana basada en la morfologa de los frutos.

23228352|Experimental approach was used to characterize quantitative macromorphological attributes of intermediate and final food products and residues that might have reached the archaeological record as macrobotanical remains of Prosopis chilensis and P. flexuosa (white and black "Algarrobo" respectively). General morphology of beans and seeds of these species are provided. Unrefined and refined flour, aapa, aloja and arrope were elaborated following traditional techniques registered by the author along the Hualfn Valley, Catamarca Province, Argentina, during previous works. It was concluded that quantitative analysis of macrobotanical remains of Prosopis, together with qualitative features, allowed the identification of different stages in the preparation and processing of Algarrobo. Distinguishing between black and white algarroba is essential to interpret Prosopis macroremains. The proportion of different categories of seeds and endocarps may help to distinguish the production of unrefined and refined flour. The last one may indicate the elaboration of patay, ulpo or aloja. Aapa and aloja residues are characterized mainly by rolled, folded or loosening of testa seed and their quantities are diminished or increased with respect to the initial amount of flour used depending on entire or fragmented seeds are being considered. The arrope residues are identified by the presence of closed endocarps, which are fully recovered after processing in their totality, and large pieces of epicarp. Except for the arrope residues, the majority of the Prosopis archaeological assemblage is considered to represent a very low proportion of the ancient processed volume of each dynamic context. Mediante una aproximacin experimental se caracterizan los atributos macromorfolgicos cuantitativos de productos intermedios y residuales derivados de Prosopis chilensis y P. flexuosa (Algarrobo blanco y Algarrobo negro respectivamente) que potencialmente podran llegar a formar parte del registro arqueobotnico. Se elabor harina no refinada y refinada, aapa, aloja y arrope, siguiendo tcnicas tradicionalmente utilizadas en el Valle de Hualfn, Catamarca, Argentina, las cuales fueron registradas por la autora en trabajos previos. Se concluye que el anlisis cuantitativo de restos macrobotnicos de Prosopis, en conjunto con el cualitativo, permite la identificacin de diferentes etapas de procesamiento del Algarrobo. Para ello resulta esencial la distincin entre las dos especies. La proporcin de diferentes categoras de semillas y endocarpos es til para distinguir la harina refinada de la no refinada. Esta ltima podra indicar la manufactura de patay, ulpo o aloja. Los residuos de la aapa y aloja se caracterizan por presentar semillas con testa plegada, enrollada o levantada, o carecer de ella, y sus cantidades se encuentran disminuidas o aumentadas con respecto a la cantidad inicial de harina utilizada dependiendo de si las semillas que se recuperan son enteras o fragmentadas. Los residuos del arrope se identifican por poseer grandes piezas de epicarpo y porque todos los endocarpos correspondientes a la cantidad de artejos utilizados inicialmente en su preparacin se encuentran presentes. Dichos endocarpos se encuentran cerrados, y excepto en el caso de los residuos de arrope, se considera que la mayora de las asociaciones arqueolgicas de restos de Prosopis representa una proporcin muy baja del volumen de materia que le dio origen en su contexto dinmico del pasado.
23222955|Flower phases and flower visitors of Macroptilium bracteatum (Nees & Martius) Marchal & Baudet were studied in Parque Rivadavia (Concordia, Entre Ros province, Argentina). Three flower phases were recognized from flower opening to wilting (24 hs). The stigma is receptive during phases one and two. Pollen reacts positively to peroxidases in all phases, its viability is 82% and its main cytoplasmic reserve is starch. Pollenkitt contains lipids and proteins. Nectar is present in all three phases. Among the six flower visitors observed, Bombus atratus Franklin (dominant) and Centris sp. (rare) triggered the pollen transfering and stigma exposing mechanism (nototribic). The development of the ovary and of the pollen tubes in flowers isolated for 24 and 48 hs. as well as the analysis of the P/O relationship and fructification under controlled conditions suggest that this species is a facultative xenogamous.
23215558|Se estudia el efecto que la orientacin de segmentos de raz de Diplotaxis tenuifolia tiene sobre el modo de formacin de yemas adventicias. Estos rganos se originan a partir de clulas del parnquima floemtico y de los radios xilemticos perifricos. Generalmente se forman sobre la superficie de corte del extremo proximal, sin que exista una proliferacin celular ("callo") previa, la que es abundante en el extremo distal. En cambio, si la orientacin de los segmentos es invertida durante el perodo de regeneracin (extremo distal hacia arriba), las yemas adventicias pueden formarse en ambos extremos. Mientras en el extremo proximal siguen el mismo modelo anterior, en el extremo distal se originan sobre el callo a partir de ndulos cribovasculares. Tambin en ese callo se inician primordios radicales. When root sections of Diplotaxis tenuifolia are put to regenerate in a vertical position with the proximal end upwards, several adventitious buds are formed either at or near the proximal end. These structures are differentiated from cells of both the phloem parenchyma and the xylem rays, without requiring the proliferation of the cells ("callus") as a previous step. On the other hand, when the root sections are put to regenerate in an inverted position (proximal end downwards), the buds are formed at both ends but those located at the distal end are originated from meristematic nodules. These nodules are the first sign of differentiation in the callus resulting from the proliferation of the phloem parenchyma cells.

23230205|The genus Erythrina in Argentina is composed of three native species: E. crista-galli var. cristagalli, E. falcata and E. dominguezi, the first two taxa are morphologically very similar and it is difficult to identify them based on herbarium material. The aim of this contribution is to review the Argentinean taxa of Erythrina, to study their morphological intraspecific variation and to propose new characters to delimit them clearly. Three hundred samples from herbaria and new collections from Salta, Jujuy and Tucumn (Argentina) were analyzed. Most E. crista-galli populations from northwestern Argentina are characterized, and differ from those of the rest of the country, by the elliptical leaflets, larger flowers, long pedicels, tubular-campanulate to urceolate calyx and the falcate and acute keel. Based on those populations a new variety, E. crista-galli var. longiflora, is proposed. The descriptions of two exotic species E. similis and E. poeppigiana, cultivated as ornamentals, are included. Se analizaron 300 ejemplares de herbario y nuevas colecciones efectuadas en Salta, Jujuy y Tucumn (Argentina). La mayora de las poblaciones de E. crista-galli del noroeste se caracterizan, y difieren de las del resto del pas, principalmente por los fololos elpticos, flores de mayor tamao y pedicelos largos, el cliz tubular-campanulado a urceolado y la quilla falcada y muy aguda. 23217337|Chromatography studies in seven species of Vicia (Leguminosae). The leaf alcoholic extracts of six native Argentine species of Vicia (subg. Vicilla, sect. Australis: V. gramineae, V. macrogramineae, V. epetiolaris, V. montevidensis, V. nana and V. pampicola) and one adventitious species (subg. Vicia, sect. Vicia: V. sativa subsp. nigra) were studied by bidimentional paper chromatography. Eighty phenolic compounds were found in 107 individuals that were studied. 23228243|In this paper, an ethnobotanical-ethnoarchaeological study of different local landraces of Cucurbita maxima subsp. maxima, Cucurbitaceae, was carried on. The aim was to evaluate if different qualitative and quantitative seed characters of these local landraces, as well as those which came from plants resulting from cultivation or husbandry, get together or not in different morphotypes which materially reflect the diversity locally recognized, as well as local practices. The construction of these morphotypes is proposed as a way to recognize local landraces and different forms of Man - plant interactions in archaeobotanical samples. Domesticated plants are the result of actions derived from selection criteria socially built and transformed, therefore they can constitute different morphotypes which act as carriers of social meanings. For this reason we believe that an ethnoarcheological ethnobotany which generates models to contrast in paleoethnobotanical work will be a good option. Macroscopical morphological descriptors commonly used in archaeobotany were employed together with new micromorphological ones. It was concluded that quantitative micromorphological characters are the most adequate ones to create morphotypes which correspond with locally recognized landraces and with husbandry practices locally developed upon vegetable populations. En este trabajo se realiza el estudio etnobotnico-etnoarqueolgico de diversos cultivos locales de Cucurbita maxima subsp. maxima, Cucurbitaceae. El objetivo es comprobar si los caracteres cuantitativos y cualitativos de las semillas procedentes de los mencionados cultivos, as como tambin de plantas resultantes de prcticas de cultivo o cuidado, se agrupan o no en morfotipos diferenciales que reflejen materialmente la diversidad localmente reconocida y los distintos comportamientos involucrados. La generacin de dichos morfotipos se propone como una va para explorar si es factible reconocer cultivares locales y distintas formas de relacin hombre - planta en muestras arqueobotnicas. Las plantas domesticadas son el producto de la puesta en prctica de criterios de seleccin socialmente construidos y por lo tanto susceptibles de constituir morfotipos diferenciales que operen como portadores de significados sociales. De all que podamos hablar de una etnobotnica etnoarqueolgica generadora de modelos a contrastar en el trabajo paleoetnobotnico. Se aplicaron los descriptores morfolgicos macroscpicos comnmente empleados en paleoetnobotnica y arqueobotnica para el estudio de semillas de Cucurbita sp., as como tambin un conjunto nuevo de descriptores micro morfolgicos. Se constat que los caracteres cuantitativos micro morfolgicos son los que mejor sirven para crear morfotipos que se corresponden con los cultivares localmente reconocidos y con las prcticas de cultivo o cuidado ejercidas sobre las poblaciones vegetales.

23217328|Pollen dimorphism and pollen viability in Tripogandra diuretica (Commelinaceae). One of the principal features of the genus Tripogandra is the possession of two staminal whorls which differ in length and in the shape and colour of the anthers (heterandry). In T. diuretica (C. Martius) Handlos the external, episepalous whorl, has three short stamens with white anthers (lower anthers) and white pollen. The internal one, epipetalous, consists of three long sigmoidal stamens with a tuft of moniliform violet hairs; the anthers are yellow (upper anthers) and the pollen is cream-coloured. The pollen of the lower anthers is 1-anacolpate of 17  21,5 m, with a tectate, baculate exine and a perforate tectum ornamented with small granules. Its cytoplasm and its two nuclei stain deeply in acetocarmine; its is viable, germinating easily in 10% sucrose. The pollen of the upper anthers is also 1-anacolpate, but of bigger size, 22  25,5 m. It has also a tectate, baculate exine with a perforate tectum, but ornamented with small granules plus spherical processes. Like the viable pollen it has also two nuclei, but both, nuclei and cytoplasm stain weakly with acetocarmine. It is inviable and it does not germinate in sucrose in any concentration (5-35%). Meiosis in the upper anthers is delayed with respect to meiosis in the lower ones. The differences between both kinds of pollen in T. diuretica, are less marked than in the others species of Tripogandra for which dimorphous pollen has been described.
23222516|Unreduced gametes and genomic relations in three species of Turnera (Turneraceae). Reciprocal hybridizations were made between T. grandidentata, 2n = 4x = 20, and two diploid species (2n = 2x = 10), T. krapovickasii and T. caerulea. The hybrids were studied cytologically to determine the relationship between these species. Besides triploid hybrids, two hybrids from unreduced egg cells were obtained, and one spontaneous hybrid was found. Meiosis in the T. grandidentata  T. krapovickasii triploid hybrid was very irregular with numerous laggards and some bridges; mean pairing relationships were 4.94 I, 4.81 II and 0.13 III. T. grandidentata  T. caerulea triploid hybrid showed only cells with bivalents and univalents and mean chromosome association of 5.41 and 4.8 II. Meiosis in T. krapovickasii  T. grandidentata tetraploid hybrid showed some laggards and bridges, with a mean chromosome association of 1.03 I, 6.48 II, 0.22 III and 1.35 IV. Meiosis in T. grandidentata  T. caerulea pentaploid hybrid showed only cells with 10 II + 5 I. In a previous paper the genome of T. krapovickasii was designated as AkAk. The present results indicate that T. grandidentata and T. krapovickasii have homeologous genomes while T. caerulea has a different one. The genomic formulas AgAgArAr and CC are proposed for T. grandidentata and T. caerulea, respectively. It is likely that polyploid species of Turnera erose probably through a sexual polyploidization process involving unreduced gametes.

23228357|We studied different functional attributes on two Schoenoplectus californicus (C. A. Mey) Sjak marshes that appear as very similar communities in terms of structure and dominant species, although they are settled on opposite ends along a fluvial-tidal gradient in the Lower Delta of the Paran River. Obtained results showed a significantly higher net aboveground primary production (NAPP) in the marsh directly affected by tides (1999.41  211.97 g m year). In the upstream site, less prone to tidal flooding, S. californicus had a lower NAPP (1299.17  179.48 g m year) and the system showed a higher ability to keep the produced biomass within the marsh, with significantly higher amounts of standing dead biomass (1316.00  336.01 vs. 112.40  55.05 g m), as well as higher organic contents in soils (16.20  0.12 % vs. 0.70  0.08 %). Results of the present study suggest that high energy overland flows may change the marsh functioning from a stable system accumulating organic matter to an aggressively growing marsh with higher rates of mineral accumulation. Mey) Sjak que son muy similares en su estructura y especie dominante, pero aparecen en los extremos opuestos a lo largo de un gradiente de influencia fluvial-mareal en el Bajo Delta del ro Paran. Los resultados mostraron una productividad primaria neta area (PPNA) significativamente ms alta en el pajonal afectado directamente por la marea (1999.41  211.97 g m ao). En el sitio aguas arriba, menos proclive a la inundacin por mareas, S. californicus tuvo una menor PPNA (1299.17  179.48 g m ao) y el sistema mostr una mayor capacidad para retener la biomasa producida dentro del pajonal, con cantidades significativamente mayores de biomasa muerta en pie (1316.00  336.01 vs. 112.40  55.05 g m) y mayores contenidos de materia orgnica en el suelo (16.20  0.12 % vs. 0.70  0.08 %). Los resultados obtenidos en este trabajo sugieren que los flujos superficiales de alta energa pueden cambiar el funcionamiento de estos pajonales, de un sistema estable acumulador de materia orgnica a un pajonal de rpido crecimiento, con altas tasas de acumulacin de sedimentos minerales.

23213092|A perfect stage has been found for the imperfect Hypocreodendron sanguineum P. Henn. previously discussed by the authors, for which the new genus Discoxylaria is proposed, and the binomial D. mirmecophila n. sp. applied to this fungus. 23222953|Five species of Solanum (S. commersonii Dunal, S. tarijense Hawkes, S. chacoense Bitter, S. gourlayi Hawkes and S. acaule Bitter), which present a great diversity with respect to their taxonomic relations, ploidy levels and modes of reproduction, were utilized (a) to establish if there exists cross-incompatibility between them, and (b) to gain information about the genetic nature of this barrier to hybridization. Cross-incompatibility prevents hybrid zygote formation in those crosses that involve S. tarijense as female parent and S. acaule as male parent, and in the crosses S. chacoense  S commersonii and S. gourlayi  S. commersonii. The hypothesis that cross-incompatibility is controlled by genes independent of the S locus explains the compatibility relations which emerge from the data obtained, and the existence of multiple sites of pollen tube growth inhibition in the pistils. I conclud that these 5 species became differentiated for the genes or gene complexes which control the processes that govern pollen-pistil interaction in each of them. The results obtained from the crosses between S. chacoense, S. tarijense and their interspecific hybrids affirm that the unilateral incompatibility which both species present would be determined by few genes with independent effects and gametophytic expression. Such reproductive isolation barrier would be an accidental by-product of the adaptative divergence which has accompanied the allopatric evolution of both species.

23215578|The genus Leucheria belongs to the family Compositae, tribe Mutisieae, subtribe Nassauviinae. It is an important component of the Andean flora of southern South America and it occur in the Andean region from central Peru to Tierra del Fuego, most of Chile extra-Andean, Patagonia and Malvinas Islands. Leucheria has been proposed by Lagasca in 1811. Since the last century the following genera: Lasiorrhiza Lagasca, Chabraea De Candolle, Ptilurus Don, Eizaguirrea Remy, Clybatis Philippi and Mimela Philippi are considered synonymous of Leucheria. Under Leucheria and its synonymous have been proposed more than 200 names. This paper reports the result of a Systematics Revision of Leucheria, undertaken in an attempt to dispels the confusion that has prevailed in this taxon, to delimit species clearly and to provide means of identification. The present investigation is based on 4 years of study, including field works and an examination of specimens of numerous herbaria of South America, United States and Europe, having seen many type specimens. The design of this revision is: A. General Part B. Special Part, comprising the taxonomy C. Bibliography and Index to Names. The General Part comprising chapters on: History of the Genus, Generic relationships (with a key to the genera of the subtribe Nassauviinae), Morphological Analysis, Palynology, Cytology, Distribution and Ecology and Evolution. The Special Part comprising the key to the 46 recognized species of Leucheria, an accurate description of all the species and illustration of most of them. In every species a complete synonyms, range, critical notes, key to the next lower taxa (when they exist) and citation of representative specimens, have been given. A list of "Invalid Names" and a list of "Excluded Species" complete this part. Finally a well considered selection of literature and Index to Names have been included.

23213893|En los tallos de Anthobryum triandrum se produce una temprana formacin de sber, de espesor mximo a nivel de los nudos y constituido por clulas de gran tamao muy alargadas anticlinalmente. El felgeno se origina en clulas corticales externas del tallo, pero al ser concrescente ste con la vaina estipular que es decurrente, queda el sber en una posicin aparentemente interna por lo que ha sido citado errneamente como  pericclico . El desarrollo de este tejido en tallos de distinta edad muestra que siempre las clulas recientemente formadas son muy alargadas en sentido radial y que las ms externas se van comprimiendo y aplastando hasta formar una masa compacta. Se ha investigado adems la formacin de este tejido en algunas especies de Frankenia, de caractersticas similares a las de Anthobryum triandrum; la diferencia estriba en que en Frankenia la vaina estipular no es decurrente. There is in the stems of Anthobryum triandrum an early occurrence of cork which attains its greatest thickness at the nodes. This cork is composed of large cells, radially elongated in transections. The phellogen arises in the outer cortical cells of the stem, concrescent with the stipular sheath; this sheath is decurrent with the stem and that is why the cork apparently rests in an internal position and was erroneously considerated as  periciclic  by some authors. The development of this tissue in stems of different ages was studied; in all of them the younger cells are radially elongated and the outer cells are gradually compressed and crushed forming a compact structure. This cork was investigated also in some species of Frankenia, being similar in its characters to that of Anthobryum.

23216454|In this paper the authors study the occurrence of natural hybridization among some species of Prosopis from Sect. Algarobia, Series Ruscifoliae and Series Chitenses. The methods used consisted of field observations, exomorphological analysis and bidimensional paper chromatography. The species and the different interspecific combinations are analysed separately. They conclude it is possible to recognise three main areas where hybridization occurs spontaneously. They analyse the different possibilities of fertilization of the hybrids and the pre and postzygotic isolation barriers that could be active in the genus Prosopis. Finally, they consider which are the main factors that allow the establishment and survival of the hybrids, as well as which are the taxonomic and biological ranks, they believe, the entities studied deserve.

Porlieria microphylla would be tetraploid with 2n = 52 (x = 13). Plectrocarpa tetracantha is diploid with n = 13 (x = 13) showing regular meiosis with 13 bivalents. In the genus Bulnesia the somatic chromosomes have been studied in seven species; six of them are diploid with 2n = 26 (x = 13): B. arborea, B. carrapo, B. foliosa, B. retama, B. sarmientoi y B. schickendantzii. The other species, B. bonariensis would be tetraploid with 2n = 52. Polisomaty is frequent in this genus. This rises some doubt on the somatic counts made in Porlieria microphylla and Bulnesia bonariensis. The behaviour of the meiotic chromosomes was also studied in five of the species of Bulnesia (B. arborea, B. carrapo, B. foliosa, B. retama and B. schickendantzii); it was found that it was regular in all of them, with the occurrence of 13 bivalents. B. retama has chromosomes of considerable longer size than the other species, its karyotype is formed by 4 m + 12 sm + 10 st. The remaining species seem to posees more symetric karyotypes than this of B. retama, even when it was not possible to determine them precisely because of the small size of the chromosomes. Likewise B. schickendantzii have a karyotype formed by 14 m + 12 sm. The asymetry of the karyotype and the larger size of the chromosomes observed in B. retama seem to be correlated with a greater specialization and adaptation to dry regions. Sericodes greggii posses 2n = 30 (x = 15). This fact suggests that this genus is not closely related to Larrea (x = 13) as it has been proposed on the basis to the exomorfology of flowers and fruits. The basic number x = 15 postulated for Sericodes is new for the family Zygophyllaceae. Pintoa chilensis is diploid and presents 2n = 20 (x = 10).
23223259|Eleocharis tucumanensis Barros grows in the high mountains of Argentina, Bolivia and Chile. The anatomical structure of culms was studied and showed it is a C species. A complete description, illustrations, and SEM micrographs of the achenes are given.
23222528|Chromosome studies in Bomarea and Alstroemeria (Alstroemeriaceae). Chromosome numbers were determined and observations were made on the meiotic behavior of Bomarea setacea (Ruiz et Pavon) Herbert (n = 9) from Colombia, here investigated cytologically for the first time, Bomarea edulis (Tussac) Herbert (n = 9), Alstroemeria psittacina Lehmann (n = 8) and Alstroemeria aurea Graham (n = 8). The materials from the last three species were collected in Argentina. The differences in chromosome number and size between Alstroemeria L. and Bomarea Mirbel are emphasized, the latter genus having smaller chromosomes. Other morphological differences are also pointed out. It is suggested that Alstroemeria (x = 8) may have derived from Bomarea (x = 9) by translocation of essential genetic material to other chromosomes, loss of a centromere and addition of repetitive DNA in all chromosomes.

23225115|Carex microglochin (Cyperaceae), a member of Carex sect. Leucoglochin, is a bipolar species that, for the most part, occurs in the northern part of the Northern Hemisphere and in the Andean region of South America. A majority of past and present workers have treated the northern plants as subsp. microglochin, whereas the southern plants have been referred to subsp. fuegina. However, it is demonstrated in this paper that two closely-related yet taxonomically-distinct species. C. camptoglochin and C. microglochin, occur in South America, these differing both morphologically and ecologically. Regarding the South American distribution of these two species, it is documented below that: (1) C. microglochin occurs sporadically throughout nearly the full extent of the Andes; (2) C. microglochin and C. camptoglochin grow sympatrically in both the boreal and austral parts of South America; and (3) C. camptoglochin occurs as a disjunct on the Falkland Islands (Islas Malvinas). Carex microglochin (Cyperaceae, Carex, sect. Leucoglochin) es una especie bipolar. La mayora de los autores, han considerado las plantas del hemisferio Norte como subsp. microglochin, mientras que las plantas del hemisferio Sur se refirieron a la subsp. fuegina. En esta nota se demuestra que este ltimo taxn corresponde a dos especies estrechamente relacionadas aunque taxonmicamente distintas, C. camptoglochin y C. microglochin, ambas en Sud Amrica, las que difieren tanto en su morfologa como en su hbitat. En relacin con la distribucin sudamericana de estas dos especies, se documenta que: (1) C. microglochin habita ocasionalmente casi a todo lo largo de los Andes: (2) C. microglochin y C. camptoglochin son simptricas en Sud Amrica, tanto austral como septentrional, y (3) C. camptoglochin habita como disyunta en las Islas Malvinas (Falkland Islands).

23222987|The main reproductive aspects of this South American species, a potential crop for arid lands, were studied in garden-grown and wild populations: Pollen-ovule ratios; crossing behavior; reproductive success and plant-pollinator interactions. A high pollen-ovule ratio indicates xenogamy. The species is self-incompatible and produces nearly 90% and 67% of fruit set in outcrossing in garden-grown and wild plants respectively; the flowers are visited by many insects, mainly honey bees, flies and solitary bees.
23218914|The genus Azorella (Apiaceae-Hydrocotyloideae) in Argentina. Azorella comprises about 30 species of mainly Andean cushion plants. This work deals with a morphological and taxonomic revision of Argentine species. At present, 15 species are recognized for this country. The history of the genus, relationships with other genera, morphological features and some aspects of reproductive biology are analyzed; up to date literature on embryology and cytology is briefly presented and discussed. The taxonomic treatment includes a description for the genus, a key to recognize Argentine species and a list of excluded names. A description, illustrations and a distribution map of each species are given. Nomenclatural problems, intraspecific variability and affinities with other species are also analyzed. A. diversifolia Clos is a new record for Argentina. The names A. cespitosa Cav. and A. gilliesii (Hook.) Hook. & Arn. are reduced to synonymy for the first time.

23225122|Synflorescences of 17 species of Melica belonging to the argentinian flora were studied from a typological point of view. These species have polytelic inflorescences with a main florescence and a similar structural pattern in the paracladial zone. Processes of truncation and homogeneization were not observed. Among species, inflorescences mainly differ by the number, divergence and degree of ramification of primary paracladia, and by the progressive or rapid reduction in length of the internodes in the main axis. Prophyllar located paracladia increase the ramification of the antotagma region. Only M. sarmentosa develops paracladia with trophotagma below the flowering unit. Sinflorescencias de 17 especies del gnero Melica presentes en Argentina han sido estudiadas desde el punto de vista tipolgico. Las inflorescencias son politlicas, presentan florescencia principal, no sufrieron procesos de homogeneizacin y/o truncamiento y muestran un patrn similar de desarrollo de la zona paracladial. Las principales variaciones se observan en el nivel del nmero de paracladios primarios, grado de ramificacin de los paracladios primarios, reduccin gradual o brusca de la longitud de los entrenudos del eje principal, disposicin adpresa o divergente de los paracladios. El grado de ramificacin del antotagma se amplifica por el desarrollo de paracladios en posicin profilar. La mayora de las especies (excepto M. sarmentosa) carecen de paracladios largos con trofotagma.

23612304|We present the analysis of plant remains recovered from the archaeological site Cueva Huenul 1, Neuqun Province, Argentina, which provides new insights on the timing of peopling, environment exploitation and use of plant resources. The chronological sequence of the site extends from the Pleistocene-Holocene transition to recent times. The archaeological remains might have been deposited by societies with a hunter-gatherer subsistence. The recovered taxa correspond to native wildlife, which are consistent with the landscape of northern Patagonia, as well as to one domesticated taxon (Lagenaria sp.). The assemblage is studied from a taphonomic perspective to assess the influence of anthropic and natural processes of formation. Finally, these results were integrated with other archaeological and palaeoecological data, allowing a first assessment of human subsistence at the scale of the site. The spatial expansion of this study will provide the basis to study the variation in human subsistence across different environmental settings in northwestern Patagonia. Se presenta el anlisis de los restos vegetales provenientes del sitio Cueva Huenul 1, Provincia de Neuqun, Argentina, el cual aporta nuevos conocimientos sobre el proceso de poblamiento, la explotacin del medio ambiente y el uso de los recursos vegetales. La secuencia cronolgica del sitio abarca desde la transicin Pleistoceno-Holoceno hasta tiempos recientes. Los restos arqueolgicos podran haber sido depositados por sociedades cazadoras-recolectoras. Los taxones recuperados corresponden a especies silvestres autctonas, las cuales concuerdan con el paisaje regional, y a un taxn domesticado (Lagenaria sp.). Se aborda el anlisis tafonmico a fin de evaluar la incidencia antrpica o natural en la formacin del conjunto arqueobotnico estudiado. Finalmente, se integran estos resultados con los datos proporcionados por otros indicadores arqueolgicos y paleoecolgicos, permitiendo una primera caracterizacin de la subsistencia humana en la escala del sitio. La ampliacin espacial de este anlisis permitir evaluar la variacin en la subsistencia en diferentes ambientes del noroeste de Patagonia.

23226844|This is the first revision for the representatives of the genus Caiophora (Loasaceae) in Chile. The genus is widely distributed in the Andes from Argentina/Chile in the South to Central Ecuador in the North, and comprises approximately 60 species. In Chile only five species are present, Caiophora chuquitensis, C. cirsiifolia, C. coronata, C. deserticola sp. nov. and C. rosulata. Caiophora rosulata is here subdivided into two subspecies: western Andean C. rosulata subsp. rosulata (present in northern Chile and southern Peru), and eastern Andean C. rosulata subsp. taraxacoides, stat. and comb. nov. Furthermore C. superba syn. nov. and C. macrocarpa syn. nov. are placed into synonymy under C. chuquitensis, and C. rahmeri syn. nov. is synonymized to C. rosulata subsp. rosulata. These five species comprise the complete range of growth forms known for the genus, i.e., subshrubs, cushionforming herbs, acaulescent, rosulate herbs and vines. For all taxa a key and full morphological descriptions and synonymy are provided, including illustrations, notes on habitat, distribution, floral biology and chromosome numbers. Esta es la primera revisin del gnero Caiophora (Loasaceae) en Chile. El gnero comprende alrededor de 60 especies, y est ampliamente distribuido en los Andes, desde Argentina/Chile en el Sur, hasta el centro de Ecuador en el Norte. Se conocen solamente cinco especies de Chile: Caiophora chuquitensis, C. cirsiifolia, C. coronata, C. deserticola sp. nov. y C. rosulata. El material de Caiophora rosulata se divide entre dos subespecies, C. rosulata subsp. rosulata comb. nov., de los Andes Occidentales (presente en el norte de Chile y el sur de Per, y C. rosulata subsp. taraxacoides stat. y comb. nov., de los Andes Orientales. Los nombres C. superba syn. nov. y C. macrocarpa syn. nov. son sinonimizados bajo C. chuquitensis, y C. rahmeri syn. nov., sinonimizado bajo C. rosulata subsp. rosulata. Estas cinco especies comprenden el rango completo de hbitos conocido para el gnero: sufrtices, hierbas perennes en forma de cojines, hierbas rosuladas acaules, y hierbas trepadoras. Proporcionamos una clave, descripciones morfolgicas y la sinonimia completa para todos los taxones, incluyendo ilustraciones, notas sobre la distribucin, el hbitat, la biologa floral y nmeros cromosmicos.

23225159|Setaria pflanzii is a wild species native to northwestern Argentina, SE of Bolivia and NE of Paraguay, with a potential of forage production and good palatability. Our results indicate that S. pflanzii would be an allotetraploid (2n=4x=36) with regular segregation and a mean of chromosome association of 0.21 I. 17.76 II and 0.02 IV per pollen mother cell. Pollen viability, seed production and embryological observations indicate that S. pflanzii is sexual, mainly autogamous species. 23223891|A total of 81 uses of a veterinary nature were recorded for 61 native and exotic plant species belonging to 54 genera and 37 botanical families, among the peasants of the Argentine Semiarid Chaco. The scientific and vernacular names, parts employed, forms of preparation and administration, and specimens examined are listed for each of the taxa involved. El uso de las plantas en su veterinaria tradicional evidencia una combinacin de diferentes tcnicas teraputicas: antigua medicina hipocrtica, procedimientos mgicos y prcticas religiosas cristianas.

23227130|In this paper we analyze the altitudinal use of the environment in the traditional agricultural practices of an Andean rural community of Salta Province. Argentina. At present, families that used to move periodically among different settlements are gradually turning to be sedentary. This process has resulted in the weakening of the vertical use of the environment, the concentration of agricultural activities into a sole altitudinal level, the loss of some cultigens proper of abandoned areas and in the increase in the pressure of use in permanent locations. Even though ancestral agricultural practices are still in use in the community under study, changes are negatively influencing their preservation. Se analiza el uso altitudinal del ambiente en relacin a prcticas agrcolas tradicionales, en una comunidad rural de la provincia de Salta. Argentina. En el presente, las familias que solan trasladarse peridicamente entre diferentes puestos estn tornndose sedentarias paulatinamente. Este proceso est ocasionando cambios tales como la disminucin de la importancia del uso vertical del ambiente, la concentracin de las actividades agrcolas en un solo nivel altitudinal, la prdida de algunos cultgenos debido al abandono de las reas apropiadas para su produccin y el incremento de la presin de uso en las empleadas de forma permanente. Aunque las prcticas agrcolas ancestrales an se observan en la comunidad estudiada, estn ocurriendo cambios que influencian negativamente su preservacin.
23222522|Identity of Pseudostiffita with Moquinia (Compositae) and considerations on the tribal position of the taxon. The monotypic genus Moquinia DC. has been placed since its creation in the tribe Mutisieae. Such position has been questioned by some authors based on pollen morphology. A comparative study with allied tribes demonstrates that Moquinia shows a clear affinity with Pseudostifftia H. Robinson, regarded by its authors as being included in the tribe Vernonieae. From this study it becomes clear that Pseudostifftia is a synonym of Moquinia, but also that the position of the latter must change from Mutisieae to the Vernonieae, although representing an isolated element within such tribe, supporting thus, Robinson's opinion on the matter. Two species of Moquinia are recognized and differentiated and a new combination is established, Moquinia kingii (H. Robinson) Gamerro.

23223222|Thirty two samples of honeys from the lower valley of the Chubut River were analyzed. Most samples contained less than 2000 grains/g. Honeys were classified as Tamarix gallica (14 samples), Eucalyptus type (1 sample), Medicago sativa (1 sample) and mixed honey (16 samples). Pollen types were identified using a collection of reference pollen slides. Both the pollen from honeys and the pollen from de reference material were subjected to acetolysis. The most important source of nectar in the lower valley of Chubut River honeys is Tamarix gallica, but the importance of Medicago sativa, in spite of its low intra-sample frequence, is also discussed. Asteraceae and Fabaceae are the best represented families followed by Brassicaceae. Pollen of the native vegetation was well represented and allowed to differentiate these honeys from others in Argentina.

23226691|The goal of this research was to reconstruct the vegetational and climatic changes that took place during the late Pleisocene and Holocene in southwestern Syria. This reconstruction was based on palynological data obtained from the analysis of 27 sediments and surface samples (with a total thickness of 4.55 m) collected from Al-Hijaneh Lake basin (late Pleistocene) and from Al-Aouaj River valley (Holocene). Three pollen zones were established. The oldest one (zone A) corresponds to the late Pleistocene lacustrine deposits of Lake Al-Hijaneh. Zones B and C were defined in the Holocene fluvial-lacustrine deposits of the Al-Aouaj River valley. These three pollen assemblage zones are correlated to synchronic and similar C14 dated pollen zones from Syria, Turkey, Iran and Greece. This allows a more definite age determination for the deposits of this study. The region's past climates and vegetation are discussed. 23225123|The purpose of this work was to analyze pollen deposition in an agroecosystem during the spring-summer period and its relationship with vegetation structure in a great detail scale. The study was carried out in the Station of the Instituto Nacional de Tecnologa Agropecuaria (INTA), Balcarce, Buenos Aires Province. Vegetation censuses were carried out in three habitat types of this Pampean agriculture landscape: natural vegetation, park area and corn field. Aeropalynological samples were taken at the corners of the corn field. Plant taxa present in the site were characterized according to different attributes (richness, composition, life form and dispersal type). Taxa present in the corn field were compared with those obtained from the pollen spectrum. The three habitat types differred basically in their life form and composition. 54.16% of the identified taxa in vegetation of the corn field was present in the pollen record. In both vegetation and pollen record, zoophylous types and terophyte forms of life were dominant. The habitat types showed a low qualitative and quantitative similarity at a taxonomic analogies level based on the identified pollen types. As a result of this, the landscape showed a high homogeneity. However, constance analysis of taxa was powerful enough to discriminate the origin of deposited pollen (site, local and regional). En el presente trabajo se analiz el depsito polnico en un agroecosistema durante el desarrollo de los cultivos primavero-estivales y su relacin con la estructura de la vegetacin en una escala de gran detalle. Este estudio se realiz en la Estacin Regional INTA-Balcarce (provincia de Buenos Aires), donde se delimitaron tres tipos de ambientes: natural, parquizado y agroproductivo. En cada uno de ellos se realizaron censos de vegetacin con el objetivo de identificar las fuentes polnicas y, simultnemente, se llev a cabo un muestreo aeropalinolgico en las esquinas del ambiente agroproductivo. Los taxones presentes en la localidad fueron caracterizados a travs de distintos atributos (riqueza, composicin, formas de vida y modo de dispersin). Slo los taxones del ambiente agroproductivo fueron comparados con el registro polnico. Los tres ambientes difirieron bsicamente en su forma de vida y composicin. Slo el 54,16% de los taxones identificados en la vegetacin del ambiente agroproductivo estuvieron presentes en el registro polnico. Tanto en la vegetacin como en registro polnico dominaron los taxones de tipo zofilos y las formas de vida terfitas. A pesar de la alta homogeneidad del paisaje, dado por la baja similitud cualitativa y cuantitativa entre los ambientes en el nivel de las analogas taxonmicas establecidas en base a los tipos polnicos identificados, el anlisis de la constancia de los taxones en la localidad permiti discriminar el probable origen del polen depositado en tres categoras (sitio, local y regional).

23222952|Various aspects of the reproductive biology of the perennial hermaphrodite Colletia paradoxa were studied by combining data over several years from both wild and garden-grown individuals. Flowering extends from summer end to mid winter, with a peak in autumn. The white, entomophilous flowers are adichogamous and last 5-14 days, but pollen transfer takes place only on days 1-3. A mild, vanillin-like odour along with nectar and pollen attracts over 20 insect species, of which 5 are probable pollinators. These are mainly Diptera, but also include the domestic honeybee. Reproduction in C. paradoxa is exclusively sexual and xenogamous, with pollen transfer depending solely on insect vectors. Although flower morphology and phenology do not prevent self-pollination, and geitonogamy can easily take place, autogamy was not detected. Hence, some self-incompatibility mechanism is operative in this species. Only 25% of the flowers initiated fruits, and just 6.1% from the flowers fully developed capsules. Fruit initiation was apparently pollen-limited at the flower level. Higher rates of fruit initiation and fruit ripening occurred late in the flowering period. Many seedless fruits completed development. The seed/ovule ratio in fruits bearing viable seeds was 42.7%. Predispersal (maternal) reproductive success (percent ovules becoming viable seeds) was 2.6%. For mature individuals this corresponded to over 17000 viable seeds per year.

23215666|In 1917, C. M. Hicken described a new monotypical genus of Araceae, Felipponia, as well as a new tribe, Felipponieae. Unfortunately, the name Felipponea had already been used in 1912 by Brotherus for a genus of mosses. Thus Hicken, having recognized this in 1928, created a new name, Felipponiella, for his later homonym of 1917. After a recent study of the type material, kindly sent on loan from the Instituto de Botnica "Darwinion", San Isidro, I came to the conclusion that Felipponia (= Felipponiella) uruguaya Hicken belongs to the earlier described and hitherto monotypical genus Mangonia Schott. The new combination Mangonia uruguaya (Hicken) Bogner is given accordingly in the present paper and the tribe Felipponieae Hicken reduced to the synonymy of the Asterotigmateae Schott emend. Engl. A full description of Mangonia uruguaya (Hicken) Bogner and a key of the genus Mangonia Schott are provided.

23228359|The Poa resinulosa complex includes a group of disjunct but morphologically similar species: P. calchaquiensis, P. pedersenii, and P. resinulosa. Poa resinulosa is described as a new variety of P. ligularis, distinguished by its shorter ligule, shorter leaves and culms, broader blades and minor stomata. El complejo Poa resinulosa incluye un grupo de especies conformado por P. calchaquiensis, P. pedersenii y P. resinulosa, de difcil delimitacin debido a que las entidades son afines en cuanto a su morfologa, aunque presentan distribucin disyunta. Para evaluar y analizar a las especies del complejo Poa resinulosa y especies afnes al mismo complejo, se midieron 40 caracteres morfolgicos y anatmicos en ejemplares de Poa calchaquiensis, P. lanigera, P. pilcomayensis y P. resinulosa. Esos datos se incorporaron a la matriz del conjunto de especies de Poa seccin Dioicopoa confeccionada por Giussani (2000), incluyendo tambin a P. nubensis una nueva especie afn a P. calchaquiensis. Mediante el anlisis de componentes principales y pruebas estadsticas, se circunscribi a las especies del complejo Poa resinulosa. Se describi a P. resinulosa como una variedad de P. ligularis, de la que se diferencia por poseer lgula corta, hojas y caas de menor longitud, menor ancho de la lmina y estomas de menor tamao. Se presenta una clave para la identificacin de Poa ligularis var. resinulosa y taxones afines, y un mapa con la distribucin geogrfica de ambas variedades de P. ligularis.

23223198|Twenty one samples of honey from the northeast of La Pampa province were analized using the techniques proposed by Louveaux et al. (1978). Thirty four types were identified. Eight samples have a mixed floral origin and 13 were monofloral from Prosopis sp. (one sample) and Melilotus sp. (12 samples). The pollen spectrum shows a transition area between the "pampeana" and the "espinal" regions. The characteristic pollen combinations are discussed.
23222553|With the aid of the optical and scanning eletron microscopes, the pollen grains of 20 species of Galianthe Griseb. are described. The grain morphology is homogeneous: 7 (6-8)-colporate, prolate-spheroidal or subprolate; the exine is semitectate-reticulate; the reticulum is complex, with a suprareticulum and an infrareticulum at a lower level. The exine is the most valuable character to regard Galianthe as a separate genus from Borreria Meyer, which has tectate-foveolate grains.

23222999|This is the third paper of a series of chemotaxonomic studies of the subtribe Phaseolinae in Argentina, which comprises the generic complex Phaseolus-Vigna-Macroptilium and the nearly genus Dolichopsis. Chromatographic patterns of 1 species of the genus Dolichopsis and 3 species of the genus Phaseolus were determined, including Phaseolus vulgaris var. aborigineus and primitive landraces and wild forms of Merlo (San Luis), the southernmost locality ever reported for the common bean. Cluster analysis and ordination by principal coordinates analysis were applied to 31 chemical characters (spots). These results corroborate the taxonomic position of these species, according to Marchal, Mascherpa & Stainier (1978) and Lackey (1977, 1983), who proposed the section Euphaseolus, and supported the fact that Dolichopsis is a genus relatively distant from Phaseolus, and more closely related to Vigna and Strophostyles.

23228000|The holotype of Carex sagei comes from central Chile, and this name has long been treated as a synonym of C. fuscula. Recent study indicates, however, that C. sagei is referrable to Carex section Ceratocystis, whereas C. fuscula belongs in section Spirostachyae. It is also demonstrated that C. sagei is the correct name for plants currently called C. barrosii. Carex sagei is known from Argentina, Chile, and the Falkland Islands (Islas Malvinas), where it frequents hydric habitats, such as marshes, wet meadows, and the margins of lakes, from near sea level to about 850 m. El holotypo de Carex sagei proviene de Chile central, y su nombre ha sido tratado desde hace tiempo como sinnimo de C. fuscula. Un estudio reciente indic, sin embargo, que C. sagei is asignable a Carex seccin Ceratocystis, mientras que C. fuscula pertenece a la seccin Spirostachyae. Se demuestra adems que C. sagei es el nombre correcto de plantas actualmente denomindas C. barrosii. Carex sagei crece en Argentina, Chile, e Islas Malvinas (Falkland Islands), donde frecuenta hbitats palustres tales como pantanos, pastizales hmedos y mrgenes de lagos, desde casi el nivel del mar hasta los 850 m s.m.

23223251|Phenetic relationships among 11 species belonging to the genus Berberis from 46 populations of NW Patagonia Argentina, were studied using numerical techniques. The species are B. bidentata Lechl., B. buxifolia Lam., B. cabrerae Job, B. chillanensis Sprag. ex Sandwith, B. darwinii Hook., B. empetrifolia Lam., B. heterophylla Juss., B. linearifolia Phil., B. montana Gay, B. parodii Job and B. serrato-dentata Lechl. Fifty four morphological characters were defined (24 vegetative and 30 reproductive). Forty six populations (with a total of 288 individuals) were analyzed. Two main groups were distinguished from the phenogram. One consists of the populations of 10 spiny species; the other one is only formed by populations of B. serrato-dentata (without - or rarely / with scarce little weak - spines). Numerical analysis allowed to differentiate the species studied and each of the populations within a same species. This may be related to microambiental agents conditioning the phenotype. The results here obtained agree fairly well with the interespecific relationships previously published in the genus Berberis.

23612311|Although plantations have an artificial origin, they modify environmental conditions that can alter native fungi diversity. The effects of forest management practices on a plantation of willow (Salix) and poplar (Populus) over Agaricomycetes basidiomes biodiversity were studied for one year in an island located in Paran Delta, Argentina. Dry weight and number of basidiomes were measured. We found 28 species belonging to Agaricomycetes: 26 species of Agaricales, one species of Polyporales and one species of Russulales. Our findings suggest that forest management practices on plantations of willow and poplar do not affect either the abundance or diversity of Agaricomycetes basidiomes. Aunque los cultivos forestales son comunidades artificiales, modifican condiciones ambientales que pueden alterar la diversidad fngica nativa. Se estudiaron los efectos del manejo forestal de una plantacin de sauces (Salix) y lamos (Populus) sobre la biodiversidad de Agaromycetes durante un ao en una isla del Delta del Paran, Argentina. Se midieron el peso seco y el nmero de basidiomas. Se identificaron 28 especies pertenecientes a los Agaricomycetes: 26 especies de Agaricales, una de Polyporales y una de Russulales. Nuestros resultados sugieren que el manejo forestal de dicha plantacin no afecta la abundancia ni la diversidad de basidiomas de Agaricomycetes.
23217336|Morphoecology of saxatile plants from Cerro de la Ventana, Buenos Aires Province, Argentina. The morphoecology of species which belong to the families Amaranthaceae, Bromeliaceae, Compositae, Leguminosae and Rosaceae is studied. These are all saxatile plants which grow in different types of rocky outcrops and stony soils of Sierra de la Ventana, a low mountain range that presents sharp variations of altitude, slope and exposition. In this study they are grouped according to their life forms and their morphology is described and discussed. The species are then classified into groups in relation to their habitats. The results indicate that the most frequent adaptative features in them are: slightly xeromorphic leaves, and stems, roots and xilopodia with anomalus secondary growth and early cork. Furthermore some of them have photosynthetic tissue with Kranz and CAM structure, aerophores and other special features.

He points out that the binomial stands despite the fact that it is typified in the Linnean herbarium by specimens of E. Ipecacuanhae and E. helioscopia. Croiz. including var. obtusifolia Muell.-Arg. and var. andensis Croiz.; E. portulacoides subsp. nahuelhuapina Croiz. The author points out that the current International Rules of Nomenclature do bind a taxonomist to select as the type of a species a specimen rather than a description or a figure. The choice of the type is ruled by the duty of maintaining existing nomenclature so far as possible, not by other considerations. En una breve discusin, el autor expone su conviccin de que Euphorbia portulacoides L. emend. Spreng. es una especie colectiva con lmites amplios y mal definidos. Expresa que el binomio es vlido a pesar del hecho que en el herbario de Linneo est tipificado por ejemplares de E. Ipecacuanhae y E. helioscopia. Se publican las cuatro subespecies siguientes: E. portulacoides subsp. normalis (O. Ktze.) Crojz.; E. portulacoides subsp. collina (Phil.) Croiz.; E. portulacoides subsp. major (Muell.-Arg.) Croiz., incluyendo las var. obtusifolia Muell.-Arg. y var. andensis Croiz.; E. portulacoides subsp. nahuelhuapina Croiz. El autor sostiene que las Reglas internacionales de nomenclatura obligan al taxonomista a elegir como tipo de una especie un ejemplar, de preferencia a una figura o descripcin. La eleccin del tipo est sujeta al deber de mantener la nomenclatura existente hasta donde es posible, no a otras consideraciones.  (Trad. A. B.)

23223189|Main patterns of synflorescence variation are known for Calceolaria species from northern South America (Troll, 1964, 1967, 1976; Anderson & Molau, 1980) and for few species from southern regions of South America (Troll, 1975, 1976, 1977). Patterns similar to these and new ones are reported in the present paper, as revealed by a study of 35 species from southern South America. According to this study, the basic synflorescence type is found in section Rugosae. Other morphological and caryological data support the view of this section as more ancestral in the southern range of the genus. In three sections exclusive of this southern range (Bellidifoliae, Kremastocheilos and Corymbosae) reduction of the synflorescences is associated to a rosulate habit. Extreme reduction in these groups lead to single flowered inflorescences. Truncation is an other kind of reduction pattern and is found in other groups as isolated events. Different strategies of flower exposition are evident mainly in the rosulate species depending on which part of the synflorescences suffers elongation.

23215540|Silicophytoliths have become recently a new matter of investigation in Natural Sciences, applied to Botany, Ecology, Limnology, Sedimentology, Pedology and Paleontology fields. They are useful in the interpretation of many of their problems. The knowledge of their genetic, morphologic, physical and chemical properties, and of their geobiogenetic circuit, is the matter of this work. At this respect, it is known that certain Families of plants, as Gramineae, Podostemaceae, Cyperaceae and Palmae, are able to yield silicophytoliths, by mineralization of epidermial or other tissues cells. Metabolic processes related with the plant transpiration cause the decay of certain cells and their following sustitution by amorphous silica, according to definite and constant morphological patterns for each species. Their physical and chemical strength help their steadfastness in sediments as microclasts. In this way, they can be affected by depositional processes up to dissolution, or subsist unaffected by them, passing to make recent or fossil biological records.

23218916|Multivariate analysis of morphological variation in diploid and tetraploid populations of Solanum gourlayi (Solanaceae) and related species. Cluster analysis and ordination by principal component analysis (PCA) were applied to 31 morphological characters of diploid and tetraploid cytotypes of S. gourlayi Hawkes and diploids S. vidaurrei Crdenas and S. incamayoense Okada & Clausen. The purpose of these numerical analyses was to determine whether the diploid and tetraploid populations of S. gourlayi are members of the same taxon, and how the diploid cytotype is related to other diploid species. The results confirmed that the diploid and tetraploid populations of S. gourlayi are not sufficiently distinct to be considered different species. However, the degree of morphological distinctiveness and complete geographic isolation of the tetraploid and diploid populations from the province of Jujuy, and the diploids from Salta, allows them to be treated as subspecies of S. gourlayi, S. vidaurrei resembles diploid S. gourlayi while S. incamayoense is clearly a distinct group.

Grande, is believed to be the valid name for the species, R. spiralis L. ex Dum. being a synonym. 23612319|Escallonia alpina and E. rubra (Escalloniaceae) are distributed in the same geographical region in the southern Andes; they are differentiated by few diagnostic morphological characters such as flower arrangement, and type and presence of glands. A morphological gap between both species is absent in some populations; in addition, intermediate forms have been recognized and described as hybrids. The aim of this work is to examine the genetic variation in populations of Escallonia alpina and E. rubra, and to analyze if there is a correspondence between genetic and morphological variability. We studied the morphology of 39 individuals belonging to five populations, which were also used to perform an AFLP analysis. We conducted ordination, clustering and Bayesian assignment analyses to investigate the relationship among individuals, we calculated genetic diversity indices and performed a Mantel test. As a result of the morphological analysis, two populations were assigned to each species, while the remaining population could not be assigned unequivocally to any of the two species, as the individuals exhibited an intermediate morphology. A strong correspondence between traditional morphological characters and the AFLP pattern was observed. Our preliminary morphological and molecular evidence support Escallonia alpina and E. rubra as two distinct species. The variability found in the intermediate population might be the result of inter-specific hybridization or incomplete lineage sorting. Adems, se han reconocido y descrito como hbridos varias formas de transicin entre ambas. El objectivo de este trabajo es examinar la variabilidad gentica poblacional de Escallonia alpina y E. rubra, y analizar si se corresponde con la variabilidad morfolgica observada. Se estudi la morfologa en 39 individuos de cinco poblaciones sobre los que tambin se realiz un anlisis de AFLP. Se investig la relacin entre los individuos mediante anlisis de ordenacin, agrupamiento y de asignacin bayesiana. Adems se calcularon ndices de diversidad y se realiz una prueba de Mantel. 23213799|Se han estudiado los caracteres antomo-sistemticos de las especies del gnero Adesmia y se han analizado en especial ciertos caracteres epidrmicos como tipos de estomas y tricomas, lo mismo que las estructuras secretoras de diversas sustancias como muclagos y taninos. Se han encontrado varios tipos de estomas que caracterizan grupos de especies (series) sistemticamente afines. As los estomas anisocticos estn presentes en la mayora de las series del subgnero Adesenia y los anomocticos en el subgnero Acanthadesenia. Los estemas en roseta, con una peculiar disposicin de las clulas subsidiarias alrededor de las oclusivas, caracterizan series de ambos subgneros. Existen en Adesmia tricomas glandulares y no glandulares; estos ltimos comprenden los tricelulares y los bifurcados. El tricoma glanduloso con una base bulbosa multicelular es caracterstico de la casi totalidad de las especies investigadas y presenta una transicin gradual con las emergencias de base globoso-cnica; entre ambos no se puede trazar una lnea rgida de separacin. Unas pocas especies presentan glndulas peculiares, sobre-elevadas o inmersas en los tejidos y de forma diversa. Con ambos tipos de tricomas, emergencias y glndulas, no fue posible establecer relaciones antomo-sistemticas, dada su variabilidad, a veces, dentro de una misma especie; en otros casos debido a la presencia de un mismo tipo de estas estructuras en especies no afines, alejadas sistemticamente. Otros caracteres estudiados fueron constantes para todas o casi todas las especies del gnero, como la presencia de clulas mucilaginosas en la epidermis de los foliolos y de sacos tnicos en los rganos vegetativos y florales. El estudio comparativo en las distintas especies de las emergencias de los frutos, permiti ordenarlas en grados de creciente complejidad. This paper presents an anatomical study of the species of the large South American genus Adesmia (Leguminosae). Special treatment of the epidermal characters as hairs and stomata, and its taxonomic value in the identification of the species is given. The leaf histology of representative species in each series is also studied. Systematical series are characterized by defined types of foliar stomata: the anisocytic type is present in most series of the subgenus Adesmia and the anomocytic type in the subgenus Acanthadesmia. A third type, the ciclocytic or in rosette is present in species of both subgenera. The hairs are of glandular and non glandular types. The former is represented by the bottle-shaped hair with a bulbous base and the latter includes the three-celled hair with an elongated terminal cell and the two-armed hair. Glandular structures of peculiar form, some of them sessiles and others deep-seated in the leaf tissues, are present in few species. With the trichomes and the glands it was not possible to establish anatomical-systematical relations. Other characters, as the mucilaginous epidermal cells and the tannic sacs of the vegetative and floral organs of the plant occured in most of the investigated species. The fruit walls present some characteristic emergences of different shape and structure which were studied from a comparative point of view.

23223846|The Marcgraviaceae is a small-sized neotropical family with 8 genera and perhaps 110 species mainly distributed in Colombian Amazonia, Costa Rica, Panama and Andean Colombian and Peruvian montane rain forests. Five genera and 27 species were recorded from Colombian Amazonia, where the most diverse genus was Marcgravia (13 species), followed by Souroubea (6 species), Marcgraviastrum (4 species), Norantea and Ruyschia with 2 species each. Based on a phenetic biogeographical classification, comparisons of diversity, distribution, affinity, and endemism among different Neotropical regions are provided. Although the knowledge of the Marcgraviaceae is still incomplete, some features with regard to their diversity and distribution in the Neotropic begin to emerge: 1. The Marcgraviaceae are more diverse in Western Amazonia, particularly Colombian Amazonia, than other areas (e.g., southern Mexico and southern Brazil); 2. Narrow endemic species appears to be low (ca. 24%); 3. Fifty percent of the Marcgraviaceae have a restricted distribution to a phytogeographical Region level; 4. The distribution of the numerous wide-ranging species are more or less patchy; 5. This family showed its highest endemism in northwestern of South America (Peru and Colombia); 6. The geologic history of the Andes has played an important role in the distribution and evolution of the Marcgraviaceae. For instance, most of the species diversity of several genera tends to be concentrated in Central America (Norantea), the Colombian Andean Region (Marcgraviastrum), or Western Amazonia (Marcgravia), and these areas correspond to areas of different geologic age. The Marcgraviaceae seems to have originated in South America and thus probably migrated to Central America. Las Marcgraviaceae son una pequea familia neotropical con 8 gneros y unas 110 especies, principalmente distribuidas en la Amazonia colombiana, Costa Rica, Panam y en los bosques hmedos montanos de la regin andina de Colombia y Per. En la Amazonia colombiana se han registrado 5 gneros y 27 especies, donde Marcgravia es el gnero ms diverso (13 especies), seguido por Souroubea (6 especies), Marcgraviastrum (4 especies) y Norantea y Ruyschia con 2 especies cada uno. Se comentan, sobre la base de una clasificacin biogeogrfica fentica, las afinidades florsticas y se hacen comparaciones de diversidad, distribucin y endemismo entre diferentes regiones neotropicales. Aunque el conocimiento de las Marcgraviaceae es an incompleto, ya es posible reconocer algunas caractersticas de su diversidad, distribucin y endemismo en el neotrpico: 1. Las Marcgraviaceae son ms diversas en la Amazonia Occidental, particularmente en la Amazonia colombiana, que en otras reas (e.g. sur de Mxico y sur de Brasil); 2. El porcentaje de especies endmicas de distribucin restringida es bajo (ca. 24%); 3. El porcentaje de endemismo a nivel de regiones fitogeogrficas es cercano al 50%; 4. La distribucin de las numerosas especies que cubren reas ms amplias en el neotrpico parece ser discontinua; 5. El mayor nmero de especies endmicas se encuentra en el noroeste de Sudamrica (Per y Colombia); 6. La historia geolgica de los Andes ha jugado un importante papel en la distribucin y evolucin de las Marcgraviaceae; por ejemplo, varios gneros muestran una clara tendencia a que la mayor parte de su diversidad especfica se concentre en Centroamrica (Norantea), la regin andina de Colombia (Marcgraviastrum) o la Amazonia occidental (Marcgravia); estas regiones corresponden a reas de edades geolgicas diferentes. Parece ser que las Marcgraviaceae se originaron en Sudamrica y desde all migraron a Centroamrica.

23218065|The present work deals with chromosome studies in 16 taxa belonging to thirteen genera in five tribes - Astereae, Heliantheae. Senecioneae, Mutisieae and Lactuceae - of the Compositae; eleven of them have never been studied before. Astereae: Baccharis magellanica (n = ca. 9),Grindelia tehuelches (n = 6, n = 6 + IB), Grindelia sp. cfr. chiloensis (n = 6) and Haplopappus glutinosus (n = 5) seem to be diploid; H. prunelloides (n = 12 + IIB) is a tetraploid cytotype. Heliantheae: Polymnia connata (n = 16) and Spilanthes stolonifera var. pusilla (n = 13) are diploids but their basic numbers are probably derived. Senecioneae: Senecio bracteolatus has n = ca. 40 + IBand it is octoploid. Mutisieae: the endemic genera Ameghinoa, Brachyclados and Doniophyton have been studied for the first time. Ameghinoa patagonica (n = 26), Brachyclados lycioides (n = 23 + IIB), Doniophyton patagonicum (n = 24), Leuceria glacialis (n = 20), Chuquiraga erinacea (n = ca. 54), Mutisia decurrens (n = 24) and M. spinosa (n = 23) have high chromosome numbers and they are possible ancestral polyploids. Lactuceae: Agoseris coronopifolia is a diploid with n = 9. Studies of chromosome morphology and meiotic behaviour were possible in several species. The significance of the results is discussed in relation to previous counts in the family.

23228240|This work explores the trajectories of plant resources in Northwestern Argentina by means of material evidences of food processing, artefact production and psicoactive consumption. Evidences of useful plants from different archaeological sites located at Puna, Prepuna and Valliserrana areas, between ca. 6500-400 years BP., are analyzed. Every case study includes the milling and/or pounding of plant resources as one of several steps on their processing chains. This characteristic, particularly, allow us to identify the plant resources by means of their use residues (microscopic items such as microfossils) preserved on grinding tools surface (milling tools, mortars and pestles). Ethnographic, ethnoarchaeological and historical information is used to propose modalities for the processing of different plant resources related to production chains of food, psicoactive items and artefacts. En este trabajo se exploran las trayectorias de los recursos vegetales en el Noroeste argentino prehispnico a travs de evidencias materiales de elaboracin de alimentos, confeccin de tecnofacturas y consumo de psicoactivos. Con este objetivo, se analizan registros de plantas tiles procedentes de distintos sitios de la Puna, la Prepuna y del rea Valliserrana, abarcando el lapso ca. 6500-400 aos AP. Todos los casos analizados tienen en comn que en ciertos puntos de sus cadenas de procesamiento/consumo fueron sometidos a algn tipo de trituracin o molienda, lo cual ha permitido identificarlos a travs de sus residuos (indicadores microscpicos constituidos por microfsiles) contenidos en los artefactos empleados para esa tarea (molinos, morteros y manos). A la luz de la informacin etnogrfica, etnoarqueolgica e histrica se proponen modalidades de procesamiento de los recursos tiles y se los relaciona con cadenas de produccin de bienes durables y consumibles.

23225165|After the revision of the genus Lantana in Brazil by Silva (1999), Chamissos's concept of the genus was re-established. Therefore, the species of Lantana sect.
