23223903|The flowers of Cucurbita maxima subsp. andreana are solitary. Staminate flowers can be found mainly on proximate portions of the branches while the pistillate are on distal portions. Each staminate flower has five monotecal stamens and ca. 90,000 pollen grains, while each pistillate one presents ca. 300 ovules. The axial nectary is symmetric, occupying an area of ca. 100 mm, positioned on the hypanthium, and supplied by phloem and xylem. The following morphological and anatomical parameters of the nectary were considered in order to compare both flower types: nectary surface; distribution, number and size of the stomata; number and diameter of the starch granules and cellular and nuclear diameter of the cells of nectariferous and non-nectariferous tissues. The non-secreting parenchyma showed the highest nuclear and cellular diameter but the lowest value of the nuclear/cell size relationship. No significant differences were found between the cells of the nectary epidermis and those of the secretory tissue. The nectary showed a higher number of starch granules in bud-stage compared to open flowerstage. This fact would indicates that there is a starch accumulation in the nectary until nectar secretion. The results obtained here allow us to relate morpho-anatomical traits with the nectar secretion pattern and with different aspects of the reproductive biology. Cucurbita maxima subsp. andreana tiene flores solitarias. Las estaminadas se hallan principalmente en las zonas proximales de las guas, mientras que las pistiladas estn sobre las zonas distales. Cada flor estaminada tiene cinco estambres monotcicos y ca. 90.000 granos de polen, mientras que cada flor pistilada contiene ca. 300 vulos. El nectario es axial, simtrico, ocupa un rea de ca. 100 mm, est irrigado por floema y xilema y se encuentra sobre el hipanto. Los parmetros morfolgicos y anatmicos del nectario que se compararon entre ambos tipos de flores fueron los siguientes: superficie del nectario, distribucin, nmero y tamao de los estomas, dimetro y nmero de grnulos de almidn y dimetro celular y nuclear en las clulas del tejido nectarfero y no nectarfero. El parnquima no secretor mostr los valores ms altos de dimetro nuclear y celular pero los ms bajos en la relacin tamao nuclear / tamao celular. No se encontraron diferencias significativas entre las clulas de la epidermis nectarfera y las del tejido secretor. En el nectario se observ un mayor nmero de grnulos de almidn para el estado de pimpollo que en las flores abiertas. Esta observacin indicara que se produce una acumulacin de almidn en el nectario antes de la secrecin del nctar. Los resultados obtenidos aqu nos permiten relacionar caracteres morfo-anatmicos con los patrones de secrecin del nctar y diferentes aspectos de la biologa reproductiva.

23218908|The different elements of the secretory tissue of Ipomoea purpurea (L.) Roth (Convolvulaceae), and their distribution in the plant are described. Articulated non-anastomosing laticifers are present and also schizo-lysigenous glands, which secrete lipophilic substances and are only functional in the young parts of the plant. These glands, described here for the first time, remain as "residual vesicles" in the adult leaves.
23225156|In this contribution, the tribe Lantaneae is considered in a broad sense. The morphology and typology of inflorescences in Lantana, Neosparton, Xeroaloysia, Acantholippia, Aloysia, Phyla, Bouchea, Chascanum, Stachytarpheta, Lampaya and Diostea are analyzed; Lippia has been treated in a previous paper. Inflorescences in Lantaneae belong to the polytelic type. Florescences are, in most species, spikes or sometimes spike-like racemes, varying in arrangement, spacing and number of flowers. Floral bracteoles are only present in Bouchea and Chascanum Sect. Chascanum. The most frequent pattern of the compound inflorescence is a homothetic (di) pleiobotryum with specialized long and short paracladia. This pattern, characteristic of Lantana, Phyla and Xeroaloysia, is also present in most species of Aloysia and one species of Acantholippia. Two Aloysia species have a paniculiform heterothetic pleiobotryum. Bouchea, Chascanum and Stachytarpheta have similar inflorescence. Most of their species inflorescences are dichasially ramified heterothetic pleiobotrya. Neosparton, Lampaya, Diostea and Acantholippia generally have monobotrya, which it could be interpreted as a result of reductive tendency related to the xeromorfic syndrome of these genera. The results of this study are compared with several taxonomic systems proposed for the Tribe Lantaneae. La tribu Lantaneae es considerada aqu en un sentido amplio. Se analiza la morfologa y tipologa de las inflorescencias en Lantana, Neosparton, Xeroaloysia, Acantholippia, Aloysia, Phyla, Bouchea, Chascanum, Stachytarpheta, Lampaya, Diostea. El gnero Lippia fue tratado en una contribucin anterior. Las inflorescencias son del tipo politlico. Las florescencias son en la mayora de los casos espigas, a veces racimos espiciformes, variados en la disposicin, espaciamiento y nmero de flores; las bractolas florales estn presentes slo en las especies de Bouchea y Chascanum Sect. Chascanum. La forma mas frecuente de la inflorescencia compleja en este grupo es el (di)-pleiobotrio homottico disyunto que se presenta en Lantana, Phyla y Xeroaloysia, en la gran mayora de las especies de Aloysia y Lippia y en una especie de Acantholippia. Dos especies de Aloysia poseen pleiobotrios heterotticos paniculiformes. Bouchea, Chascanum y Stachytarpheta son afines en su arquitectura y las inflorescencias son en la mayora de las especies pleiobotrios acrotnicos, no truncados, dicasialmente ramificados. Neosparton, Lampaya, Diostea y Acantholippia son gneros de pocas especies, con adaptaciones xricas; las inflorescencias son en general monobotrios; esta forma de la inflorescencia puede considerarse, en estos casos, un carcter convergente que forma parte del sndrome xeromorfo y se origina por pauperizacin de una inflorescencia ms compleja. 23222531|Ultrastructure of Pleurosigma chilensis var. patagonica nov. var. (Bacillariophyceae). The genus Pleurosigma has a few planktonic species, with straight or almost straight outline and raphe. In this work we study a material with these characteristics from Caleta Valds (Chubut, Argentina), that we consider a new variety of Pleurosigma chilensis Hustedt et Krasske. 90005706|The scientific correspondence of the Argentine botanist Lorenzo Raimundo Parodi (1895-1966) includes 5280 letters interchanged between 1916 and 1966 with 1257 correspondents from 50 countries. Parodis correspondence is comparatively rich in copies of his own letters, and therefore it offers both an insight into his personal views and a record of the ways in which he communicated with an extensive network of relationships. The article first describes the structure and formation dynamics of the documentary corpus, then analyzes in detail the thirty epistolary exchanges in which Parodis participation (as measured by the number of his own letters) was maximal. Also, a full index of the correspondence is added as an electronic supplement. In spite of Parodis various academic interests and of the considerable diversity of his partners, the correspondence unequivocally reflects that research on grasses was the axis that organized Parodis scientific life. The central position he occupied in Argentinas botany during the first two thirds of the past century, along with his international reputation as agrostologist, makes his correspondence a repository of manuscripts by virtually every significant member of these two corporations that were active during Parodis life. This article makes a contribution to the scarce bibliography on epistolary exchanges of Argentine scientists, and is apparently the first edited correspondence of an Argentine botanist.
23225160|The fruit and seed production of I. purpurea were estimated with respect to different pollination treatments (autonomous self-, hand self-, and hand cross-pollination treatments) during two reproductive seasons. Seed mass, fruit mass, and seed number per fruit were measured for each fruit and compared between treatments and seasons to evaluate fruit quality. The results obtained for Argentinean populations confirm that this species is self-compatible and capable of producing fruits by autonomous selfing. Reproductive success of naturally pollinated plants was high (> 50%). A ripened fruit weights 0.1 g and contains 4-6 seeds which represent ca. 60% of the total fruit mass. Fruit and seed traits were not significantly different between pollination treatments and between years. In addition, fruits and seeds produced by natural pollination were compared between different flower color morphs. No significant differences were detected, with the exception of one morph (pink flowers) which produced fruits with a slight lower number of seeds than the fruits of the other morphs (white or purple flowers). The main flower visitors were different species of Hymenoptera, which can be considered as pollinators. Other flower visitors were recorded but they do not seem to make a significant contribution to transfer pollen. Se evalu la produccin de frutos y semillas en Ipomea purpurea en relacin con diferentes tratamientos de polinizacin (autopolinizacin espontnea, autopolinizacin manual y polinizacin cruzada), durante dos temporadas reproductivas. La masa de los frutos, de las semillas y el nmero de semillas por fruto, se compararon entre tratamientos y entre aos, a fin de detectar diferencias en la calidad de los frutos. Los resultados para las poblaciones estudiadas en el centro de Argentina confirman que se trata de una especie autocompatible y con la capacidad de producir frutos por autogamia espontnea. Los valores de xito reproductivo mediados por polinizacin natural fueron altos (> 50%). Un fruto maduro pesa 0,1 g y contiene 4-6 semillas; la masa del total de semillas producidas por un fruto representa alrededor del 60% de la masa total del fruto. Los caracteres de los frutos y las semillas no presentaron diferencias significativas entre aos o tratamientos. Asimismo, se compararon los frutos provenientes de polinizacin natural entre los individuos con distinto color de flor. En general, tampoco se encontraron diferencias significativas. Slo los frutos provenientes de flores rosa presentaron un nmero significativamente menor de semillas que los frutos de los otros morfotipos florales (blanco o prpura). El grupo principal de visitantes florales fue el de los Himenpteros, que pueden ser considerados polinizadores. Se registraron otros grupos de visitantes florales que no tendran un papel preponderante en la transferencia de polen.
23228247|Eight regions of native forests have been recognized in Argentina: Chaco forest, Misiones rain forest, Tucumn-Bolivia forest (Yunga), Andean-Patagonian forest, "Monte", "Espinal", fluvial forests of the Paraguay, Paran and Uruguay rivers, and "Talares" in the Pampean region. We reviewed the available data concerning biodiversity of saprotrophic micro-fungi (anamorphic Ascomycota) in those native forests from Argentina, from the earliest collections, done by Spegazzini, to present. Among the above mentioned regions most studies on saprotrophic micro-fungi concentrates on the Andean-Patagonian forest, the fluvial forests of the Paraguay, Paran and Uruguay rivers and the "Talares", in the Pampean region. There are only a few records of fungal species in other native forests. No record of anamorphic species of Ascomycota was previously available for "Monte" forests. From a comprehensive bibliographic review, a total of 344 species were registered, of which 81 (23,5%) are new species.This work manifests the lack of explorations in important areas of the country, and demonstrates the need to increase those studies. En Argentina se reconocen ocho regiones de bosques nativos: bosque Andino-Patagnico, Talares de la Regin Pampeana, Parque Chaqueo, Selva Misionera, Selva Tucumano-Boliviana, Monte, Espinal y Bosques Pluviales de los ros Paraguay, Paran y Uruguay. El objetivo de este trabajo ha sido reunir y revisar la informacin sobre la biodiversidad de microhongos saprtrofos (Ascomycetes anamrficos) citados en los bosques nativos de Argentina, desde las primeras colecciones de Spegazzini hasta el presente. De las regiones anteriormente mencionadas los bosques Andino-Patagnicos, Bosques Pluviales de los ros Paraguay, Paran y Uruguay y recientemente los Talares de la provincia de Buenos Aires son aquellos donde se han realizado ms exploraciones de microhongos saprtrofos. Por otro lado se obtuvieron muy pocos registros de especies fngicas del resto de los bosques; para la regin de Monte en particular no se han realizado hasta el presente estudios de hongos anamrficos, por lo cual no se cuenta con registros de especies anamrficas de Ascomycetes. Como resultado de una revisin bibliogrfica exhaustiva, se registraron 344 especies, de las cuales 81 (23,5%) son nuevas especies. Este trabajo pone de manifiesto la falta de exploraciones de reas de importancia en nuestro pas, y muestra la necesidad de incrementar estos estudios.

23612312|Nassella is an American genus which, according to its current circumscription, includes about 116 species, distributed from Canada to Argentina and Chile. It is characterized by its florets with the lemma conspicuously convolute, with an apical conspicuous or inconspicuous crown, and the palea shorter than the lemma; furthermore, the lemma presents a distinctive epidermal pattern. The aim of this work is to provide a synopsis of the 99 species of Nassella which grow in southern South America, comprising Argentina, Bolivia, southern Brasil, Chile, Paraguay and Uruguay. A key to identify the species, mainly based on floret characters, is given. For each species, the current synonyms, geographic distribution, phenology, observations, and illustrations are presented. Nassella barbinodis is accepted and, Nassella linearifolia is a new synonym of Nassella caespitosa. Lectotypes are here designated for the following taxa: Danthonia nardoides, Piptochaetium collinum, P. gibbum, P. laevissimum, Stipa arechavaletae, S. barbinodis, S. breviculmis, S. calchaquia, S. carettei, S. clarazii var. bulbosa, S. curicoana, S. debilis var. papillosa, S. duriuscula, S. hispida, S. hyalina, S. julietti, S. longiglumis, S. macrathera, S. manicata var. media, S. mendocina, S. pratensis, S. pseudopampagrandensis, S. rupestris, S. tenuis, S. trachysperma, S. trichocaulos, and S. uspallatensis. A neotype is designated for S. filiculmis. Nassella es un gnero americano que, de acuerdo a su actual circunscripcin, incluye unas 116 especies, distribuidas desde Canad hasta Argentina y Chile. 23223847|A floristic study on 15 physiographic landscapes in the south of the Colombian Amazon was carried out. In 2.8 ha, 593 vascular plants (dbh  10 cm) were found, belonging to 254 genera distributed among 65 families. Nine families represent 52 % of the total number of species and comprise 65 % of the total number of individuals. The richest families are Fabaceae (78 species, 13%), Chrysobalanaceae (42 species, 7%), Euphorbiaceae (29 species, 5%), Myristicaceae (28 species, 5%), Burseraceae (27 species, 4.5%), Sapotaceae (27 species, 4.5%), Lauraceae (26 species, 4.4%), Moraceae (24 species, 4.1%) and Lecythidaceae (23 species, 4%). The richest genera are Licania (20 species), Protium (18 species), Inga (16 species) and Eschweilera (14 species). Myristicaceae, Euphorbiaceae, Moraceae and Lauraceae are dominant and abundant on well drained soils, while Chrysobalanaceae, Sapotaceae and Sterculiaceae are important families in periodically flooded landscapes. Monopteryx uaucu Spruce ex Benth. (Fabaceae) and Eschweilera coriacea (A. DC.) S. A. Mori (Lecythidaceae) are the most widely distributed species in different landscapes. Plant formations on plio-pleistocenic dissected plains of curved surfaces with acute and rounded summits possess the highest floristic richness; while alluvial plains with intermediate flood level by amazonian rivers show the lowest floristic species richness. Disturbance of the mature forests is caused by geomorphological dynamics, high winds, instability of the river courses, and by human action over thousands of years. Se llev a cabo un estudio florstico en 15 paisajes fisiogrficos del sur de la Amazonia colombiana. En 2,8 ha se registraron 593 especies de plantas vasculares (DAP  10 cm), pertenecientes a 254 gneros y 65 familias. Nueve familias representan el 52% del nmero total de especies y, a la vez, constituyen el 65% del total de los individuos. Las familias ms ricas son Fabaceae (78 especies, 13%), Chrysobalanaceae (42 especies, 7%), Euphorbiaceae (29 especies, 5%), Myristicaceae (28 especies, 5%), Burseraceae (27 especies, 4.5%), Sapotaceae (27 especies, 4.5%), Lauraceae (26 especies, 4.4%), Moraceae (24 especies, 4.1%) y Lecythidaceae (23 especies, 4%). Los gneros ms diversos son Licania (20 especies), Protium (18 especies), Inga (16 especies) y Eschweilera (14 especies). Las Myristicaceae, Euphorbiaceae, Moraceae y Lauraceae son dominantes y abundantes en suelos bien drenados, mientras que las Chrysobalanaceae, Sapotaceae y Sterculiaceae son ms importantes en los paisajes con inundacin peridica. Las especies Monopteryx uaucu Spruce ex Benth. (Fabaceae) y Eschweilera coriacea (A. DC.) S. A. Mori (Lecythidaceae) son las ms ampliamente distribuidas en los diferentes paisajes. Las formaciones vegetales ubicadas en las planicies divididas plio-pleistocnicas de superficies onduladas con cimas agudas y redondeadas poseen la mayor riqueza especfica; mientras que las formaciones con menor riqueza florstica se presentan en las llanuras aluviales de ros amazonenses con inundacin de aguas intermedias. La perturbacin de los bosques maduros del rea est dada por la dinmica geomorfolgica, los vientos huracanados, la inestabilidad de los cursos de los ros y por la intervencin antrpica milenaria.
23216544|Se describen en este trabajo los caracteres antomo-sistemticos foliares de las 9 especies sudamericanas de Nothofagus. Las 3 especies perennifolias son anatmicamente similares no slo por sus caracteres epidrmicos sino tambin por el grado de esclerificacin que presentan. Son semejantes asimismo N. glauca y N. obliqua, particularmente por la naturaleza papilosa de las epidermis. Otras especies poseen significativas diferencias interespecficas como N. alpina y N. antarctica, esta ltima con conspicuos surcos en las paredes internas de las clulas vecinas de los estomas. The systematic anatomical leaf characters of the 9 south american species of Nothofagus are described. The 3 evergreen species are anatomically similar due to their distinctive epidermal characters and the scleromorphic features present in them. N. glauca y N. obliqua are also similar on account of the papillose nature of their epidermises. Some of the other species possess significatives interespecific differences, as N. alpina and N. antarctica, the last with conspicuous internal furrowed walls in the neighbouring cells of the stomata.

23223194|Chromosome counts and meiotic chromosome behavior confirmed previous results for both species. One accession of Panicum dichotomiflorum Michaux, from Corrientes, Argentina, had 2n=4x=36 chromosomes with regular meiotic behavior. Three accessions of Paspalum fasciculatum Willd. ex Fluegge, two from Mato Grosso state, Brazil, and one from Chaco province, Argentina, had 2n=2x=20 chromosomes. This is the first report of the method of reproduction for both species. Embryological studies and observations on flowering habits and seed production indicated that Panicum dichotomiflorum, which is an annual species, reproduced sexually. Its floral arrangement, the flowering habit, and the lack of a genetic barrier to prevent self-fertilization suggested that the species reproduced mainly by autogamy. The three accessions of the perennial species Paspalum fasciculatum were sexual and self-incompatible. Since most diploid sexual self-incompatible species of the genus Paspalum usually have an apomictic tetraploid co-specific counterpart, it is possible that apomictic tetraploid races of Paspalum fasciculatum may also exist.
23218123|Pollen morphology of Huarpea and its relationships with Barnadesia (Mutisieae, Compositae). A comparative study between the pollen morphology of Huarpea andina Cabr. and Barnadesia odorata Griseb. has been undertaken, using the photonic, interference contrast and scanning electron microscopes. The results confirm the great similarity in the pollen morphology of both genera, already pointed out by Cabrera. He consideres this similarity to be the clarest proof of the relationships between both taxa. This affinity is evident not only in the general morphological pattern, but also in exine stratification and ultrarelief. The pollen of Huarpea andina is tricolporate, suboblate, of 47  54 m of polar and equatorial diameter respectively; its exine is ornamented with an elaborate system of inerm crests which circumscribe several alveoli or lacunae, typical of lophate grains.

23216536|Karyotypes of 3 Chilean and 2 Argentine species of the genus Tristagma are described. T. bivalve, T. berteri and T. patagonicum are diploids (2 n = 8), T. nivale is tetraploid (4 n = 16) and T. sp., is hexaploid (6 n = 24). The basic chromosome number in this genus is n = 4, a basic karyotype composed by one long metacentric, two medium metacentrics and one medium acrocentric. The genus Tristagma and their close relatives Nothoscordum and Ipheion are easily delimited by the differences in their basic numbers and karyotypes.

41825708|On the basis of an ethnoarchaeological study of post-harvest quinoa processing in the Lpez Altiplano (Potos, Bolivia), some diagnostic traits of each activity and methods of processing dried grains are established. The potential of these observations to investigate the ancient practices of processing and consumption of this pseudocereal is illustrated by analyzing grains recovered from four archaeological sites near Salar de Uyuni. The quinoas examined were at different stages of processing; some showed no traces of saponin extraction, suggesting that they had been stored immediately after harvest, while others exhibited saponification traces comparable to those observed in current contexts, suggesting that they had been prepared for consumption. A partir del estudio etnoarqueolgico del tratamiento post-cosecha de granos de quinoa entre los habitantes del altiplano de Lpez (Potos, Bolivia), se describen algunos rasgos diagnsticos de cada actividad y forma de procesamiento observables en los granos desecados. El potencial de estas observaciones para investigar las antiguas prcticas de procesamiento y consumo de este pseudocereal es ilustrado mediante el anlisis de granos recuperados en cuatro sitios arqueolgicos cercanos al Salar de Uyuni. Las quinoas examinadas se encontraban en distintas etapas de procesamiento; algunas no haban sido an desaponificadas, por lo que inferimos que haban sido almacenadas inmediatamente despus de la cosecha, mientras que otras muestras exhiban rastros de desaponificacin comparables a los observados en contextos actuales, sugiriendo su preparacin para distintos modos de consumo.

23228356|This investigation analyses the vegetable resources used for tecnofactures during the prehistoric past, based on remains of artefacts recovered at the archaeological site "Punta de la Pea 4", layers 0 - 4, dated to ca. 3900  500 years BP. The site is located in the proximity of the village of "Antofagasta de la Sierra", Catamarca, Argentina (26 11' 16" S and 67 20' 51.3" W) at 3650 m altitude. The site locality belongs to the Southern Argentinean Puna and, according to the environmental characteristics, it belongs to the Salty Puna. The particular objectives were to identify plant species used as raw material, their collection area, and possible use of each artefact considering the recovered context at the archaeological site and the ethnobotanical information. Mobility and socio-economic exchanges taking into account the recovered non-local plant species is also discussed. The comparative anatomical and morphological analysis of present day and archaeological plants revealed that the species used for tecnofactures belong to the families Asteraceae, Cactaceae, Cyperaceae, Fabaceae, Juncaceae, Poaceae, Solanaceae and Typhaceae. Possible collection areas for the archaeological species suggest that long distance human migrations decreased during the Late Holocene, being replaced by itineraries of ruled mobility related to pastoralism. El objetivo de esta investigacin fue analizar el uso de los recursos vegetales para confeccionar tecnofacturas en el pasado prehistrico. Se estudiaron los artefactos recuperados en el sitio arqueolgico Punta de la Pea 4, capas 0 - 4, datadas entre ca. 3900  500 aos AP. El sitio est ubicado en las proximidades de la localidad de Antofagasta de la Sierra, Catamarca, Argentina (26 11' 16" S y 67 20' 51.3" O), a una altura de 3650 m s. m. Esta localidad pertenece a la Puna meridional y de acuerdo con las caractersticas ambientales, se integra a la Puna salada. Los objetivos especficos fueron identificar las especies vegetales utilizadas como materia prima y su rea de procedencia, as como tambin evaluar el posible uso de cada uno de los artefactos hallados. Asimismo, se discuti la movilidad y los posibles intercambios socioeconmicos teniendo en cuenta los vegetales no locales utilizados. El anlisis anatmico comparativo entre las especies actuales que crecen en el rea de estudio y aquellas utilizadas en la confeccin de estas tecnofacturas permiti la identificacin de las ltimas, las cuales pertenecen a las familias Asteraceae, Cactaceae, Cyperaceae, Fabaceae, Juncaceae, Poaceae, Solanaceae y Typhaceae. Considerando las posibles reas de procedencia de las especies arqueolgicas se registr un menor grado de movilidad a grandes distancias durante el Holoceno tardo; en su lugar se instalan circuitos de movilidad pautada que obedecen a las actividades de pastoralismo que comienzan a desarrollarse.
23218930|Vegetation of the Santa Cruz River Basin (Santa Cruz Province, Argentina). The Santa Cruz River Basin, of an approximate area of 58,000 km, was studied using photointerpretation and field checking. Vegetation structure and physiognomy were described with the aid of Dansereau's diagrams (1957), lists of species with indication of their dominance and topographic profiles showing the relationships between vegetation types and physiography. LANDSAT images 1:500,000, bands 5 and 7, and aerial photographs 1:50,000 were used to define and delineate the cartographic units, based on Goosen's physiographic approach (1967). Six vegetation types: desert, semi-desert, shrub-steppe, grass-steppe, desciduous forest and meadow were described, divided in 21 subunits on the basis of physiognomic-structural characteristics and of dominant species. Results were expressed at three different perception levels (Long, 1968): exploratory, scale 1:3.000.000; reconaissance, 1:500,000 and semidetailed, 1:20,000 for those areas with good agricultural possibilities as the Rio Chico flood plain (irrigation). This survey includes some hypothesis about probable successional trends of desertification in the Santa Cruz River Basin. Suggestions are made about the research needs and the use and management of different ecological units. Se efectu el estudio de 58.000 km en la regin de los ros Santa Cruz, Chico y Chala (provincia de Santa Cruz) utilizndose la fotointerpretacin y el correspondiente control terrestre. La fisonoma y estructura de la vegetacin fueron descriptas por medio de esquemas o diagramas (modificados de Dansereau, 1957), listas de especies con indicacin de las dominantes y perfiles fitotopogrficos (topoclinas). Sobre estos materiales se definieron y delimitaron las unidades fisiogrficas (Goosen, 1967) y posteriormente las unidades cartogrficas de vegetacin. Los resultados se expresaron en tres niveles de percepcin (Long, 1968), correspondientes a las escalas 1:3.000.000 (exploratoria); 1:500.000 (reconocimiento) y 1:20.000 (semidetallada) en las reas con alto potencial agrcola (posibilidades de riego) como el llano de inundacin del Ro Chico. 23218131|Synopsis of the Argentine species of Arenaria (Caryophyllaceae). Eight species of the genus Arenaria that grow in Argentina were analyzed, using mainly material from the Argentinian herbaria. 23217335|Embryological studies in Buddleja (Buddlejaceae) I: Endosperm and Episperm. This paper deals with the endosperm and episperm development of two species of Buddleja: B. stachyoides Cham. et Schldl. and B. tubiflora Benth. The following are the main conclusions:  The cellular development of the endosperm is according to the EODP system (Di Fulvio, 1983; 1985) of the heteropolar type and longitudinal subtype (EODP 1221) with chalazal and micropylar primary haustoria. The cells near the primary haustoria differentiate, secondarily, as haustorial cells.  In the mature seed the endosperm is ruminate and corresponds to the Verbascum type of Periasamy.  The endothelium is differentiated at the time of the anthesis but its cells divide actively after fertilization only by means of anticlinal divisions; in this way, the number of cells around the endosperm remains constant since the anthesis until the seed development is completed. These cells keep pace with the endosperm expansion becoming considerably enlarged.  The episperm consists of only 2 layers, the endothelium and the outer epidermis. The outer epidermal cells develop U-like secondary lignified thickenings along the radial and inner tangential walls; the outer tangential wall is compressed. Cells with reticulated thickenings develop around the micropyle.  Preliminary phytochemical and morphological studies showed close affinities between Buddleja and some genera of the Scrophulariaceae. The present study emphasizes this relationship and suggests that Buddlejaceae should be considered as an independent family, to included in the order Scrophulariales. Moreover, the absence of embryological similarities with Loganiaceae is at the same time demonstrated.

23230216|The Tucumano-Boliviano forest, on its Bolivian side, has begun to be studied with greater detail in the last decade. However, the studies that have been conducted have had a more qualitative character or have been undertaken in small areas (0.1 ha); on the other hand, the biogeography of its lower zones is not completely understood. Moreover, some ecological aspects, such as tree spatial patterns, have never been addressed. We conducted a study in one hectare of tucumano-boliviano forest at 700-950 m, and mapped all trees and vines with DBH 10 cm in order to characterize quantitatively a representative area of this forest. The purpose was to obtain insight into its floristic composition, species abundance and structure. We carried out the first study on spatial patterns for this type of forest in Bolivia. We recorded 591 individuals belonging to 31 families, 47 genera, and 57 species. Six species were the most abundant and: Urera caracasana, Trichilia clausenii, Piper tucumanum, Diatenopteryx sorbifolia, Chrysophyllum gonocarpum and Cupania vernalis. The forest studied can be classed more as Tucumano-Boliviano forest than as a Pleistocene Arc type forest. Basal area was 29.04 m/ha. There was a relatively scarce presence of lianas, which indicates that this is a relatively slightly disturbed community. This is a diverse forest. Species richness turned out to be comparable to that of Madidi dry forests, and greater than that in Tucumano-Boliviano forest in Argentina, and was estimated at 74 tree species. Diversity (3.5 Shannon-Wiener index) is as high as that in many tropical forests, even in Amazonia. We found a random spatial pattern in the individuals of the community, and most of the species exhibited clustering at some spatial scale. El bosque tucumano-boliviano, en su sector correspondiente a Bolivia, ha comenzado a ser conocido con mayor detalle en los ltimos aos. Sin embargo, los estudios realizados han tenido un carcter ms cualitativo o se han realizado en superficies pequeas (0,1 ha); adems, la biogeografa de sus zonas ms bajas no est del todo clara. Por otro lado, algunos aspectos ecolgicos, como los referidos a patrones espaciales de los rboles, no han sido nunca abordados. Nosotros realizamos el estudio de una hectrea de bosque tucumano-boliviano a 700-950 m, y mapeamos todos los rboles y lianas con DAP 10 cm a fin de caracterizar cuantitativamente un rea representativa de este bosque. El propsito fue conocer su composicin, abundancia y estructura. Realizamos el primer estudio de patrones espaciales para este tipo de bosque en Bolivia. Registramos 591 individuos agrupados en 31 familias, 47 gneros y 57 especies. Seis especies fueron las ms abundantes: Urera caracasana, Trichilia clausenii, Piper tucumanum, Diatenopteryx sorbifolia, Chrysophyllum gonocarpum y Cupania vernalis. El bosque estudiado puede considerarse parte del bosque tucumano-boliviano ms que del Arco Pleistocnico. El rea basal total fue de 29.4 m/ha. La presencia de lianas fue relativamente baja, lo que indica que se trata de un bosque relativamente poco perturbado. Se trata de un lugar diverso. La riqueza especfica result comparable a la de los bosques secos de Madidi (La Paz, Bolivia), y supenor a la del tucumano-boliviano en el lado argentino, y fue estimada en 74 especies de rboles. La diversidad (3,5 ndice Shannon-Wiener) es tan alta como la de muchos bosques ms tropicales, e incluso algunos amaznicos. Encontramos un patrn espacial aleatorio en los individuos de la comunidad, y la mayora de las especies present agregacin a alguna escala espacial.

23222958|With this paper a revision of the leaf anatomy and architecture of the tribe Colletieae is completed. A comparative study of all 5 members of Colletia Comm. ex Juss. (C. spinosissima Gmel., C. paradoxa (Spreng.) Escal., C. hystrix Clos., C. ulicina Gill. et Hook. and C. spartioides Bertero ex Colla) and the sole member of Adolphia Meissn. (A infesta Meissn.) shows the following generic traits: Colletia: dorsiventral or subisolateral, amphi- or hypostomatic leaf structure; stomata paracytic, generally transverse to leaf axis; simple, usually straight hairs; mucilaginous epidermis absent; dark contents (presumably mucilage associated to tannin) usually absent; druses adaxially subepidermal, sometimes of considerable size; basally acrodromous, less frequently eucamptodromous venation. Adolphia: subisolateral, hypostomatic leaf structure; simple, curved to twisted hairs; dark contents from absent to very common, both in epidermis and mesophyll; druses very common; venation eucamptodromous. Colletia and Adolphia are anatomically close to different sections of Discaria within the Colletieae. As a whole this tribe is an anatomically homogenous group in which, although clear intergeneric differences are not perceived, combinations of a limited number of traits help to define most entities of specific rank.

23217333|Cytogenetics of interspecific hybrids and seed protein electrophoresis of four South American species of Elytrigia (Gramineae). Four caespitose self-fertilizing South American tetraploid species of wheatgrasses have been studied concerning their chromosomes and seed proteins. These species are Elytrigia attenuata (Kunth) Covas, E. breviaristata (A. Hitchc.) Covas, E. scabrifolia (Doell) Covas and E. tilcarensis (J. H. Hunz.) Covas. Three completely sterile hybrids were studied cytogenetically: E. attenuata  E. breviaristata, E. tilcarensis  E. scabrifolia and E. tilcarensis  E. attenuata. The mean number of closed bivalents were 9.09  0.31, 2.52  0.22 and 0.29  0.06, respectively. The meiotic behavior of the fertile artificial allopolyploid E. tilcarensis-E. scabrifolia was regular at diakinesis with 28 bivalents. At 1st. metaphase, however, there was precocious chiasma terminalization and univalents were formed (mean = 0.94 per cell). Seed set was variable (0-77%); in plant 717-21 reached 69.6% and most of the decrease in fertility in this plant is believed to be due to irregular distribution of univalents. From the analysis of the chromosome behavior of species, hybrids and allopolyploid and the study of seed proteins, the following conclusions have been reached: 1) E. attenuata and E. breviaristata have largely homologous genomes and are closely related. 2) E. scabrifolia has rather poor genome homology with both E. tilcarensis and E. breviaristata (see also Hunziker et al., 1965). 3) E. attenuata and E. tilcarensis showed the lowest degree of genome homology. 4) The four species differ from one another in at least 1 or 2 reciprocal translocations. 5) The cytogenetic results show congruency with a numerical study of the exomorphology (Ferrari & Hunziker, 1986) but did not entirely agree with a numerical study of the seed proteins separated by electrophoresis.

23226707|The grass family (Poaceae) is unusually well known taxonomically, with over 10,000 described species. These are characterized and classified according to a variety of morphological characters, particular those of the inflorescence and the spikelet but also a wealth of micromorphological and moleculary characters. Much data on the family is accessible electronically. Available phylogenies have identified 12 major lineages that are classified as subfamilies; within these subfamilies, especially for subfamily Panicoideae, the phylogeny is becoming increasingly clear. Developmental studies focus on the activity and fate of meristems throughout the plant, and illustrate how adult morphology arises. Analyses of quantitative trait loci (QTL) verify that some taxonomic characters are controlled by distinct genes, thus supporting their use in taxonomy. Studies of gene expression identify several genes, including LEAFY HULL STERILE1, RAMOSA 1, and TEOSINTE BRANCHED 1 that may have contributed to diversification of the grasses. La familia de las Gramneas (Poaceae) es bien conocida desde el punto de vista taxonmico, con ms de 10.000 especies descriptas, caracterizadas y clasificadas de acuerdo con una variedad de caracteres morfolgicos, en particular de la inflorescencia y de la espiguilla, como tambin por una gran cantidad de caracteres micromorfolgicos y moleculares. Informacin abundante sobre esta familia es accesible electrnicamente. Las filogenias disponibles han identificado 12 linajes principales clasificados como subfamilias, dentro de cada una de ellas, y en particular dentro de la subfamilia Panicoideae, la filogenia se est revelando con creciente claridad. Los estudios de desarrollo se enfocan en la actividad y el destino de los meristemas de toda la planta, e ilustran cmo se origina la morfologa adulta. Los anlisis de loci de caracteres cuantitativos (QTL) verifican que algunos caracteres taxonmicos son controlados por genes diferentes, apoyando el uso de estos caracteres en la taxonoma. Los estudios de expresin gnica identifican varios genes, entre ellos LEAFY HULL STERILE1, RAMOSA1, y TEOSINTE BRANCHED1, que pueden haber contribuido a la diversificacin de las gramneas.
23223219|The spur anatomy and some aspects of the floral biology of the perennial herb Tropaeolum pentaphyllum Lam. were studied. The hermaphrodite protandrous flowers are typically ornitophilous. They have a red spur which produces abundant nectar secreted through modified stomata. Nectar concentration is variable (27-63% sugars), and its production is greater in the staminate phase than in the pistillate one. Tropaeolum pentaphyllum seems to be a principally xenogamous species. Main pollinators are hummingbirds, but bee pollination cannot be discarded. The low rate of fruit production in isolated branches might have arisen through autogamy, but small arthropods carrying pollen grains on their bodies were occasionally observed on those branches, which may indicate that some cross-pollination is also present. The lack of fruit production in isolated and emasculated flowers indicates that there is no apomixis.

23222518|Observations on the floral biology of Prosopis (Leguminosae, Mimosoideae). II. Floral phases and visitors in the chaqueo serrano district. In this paper we present the results of observations on a community of Prosopis chilensis (Molina) Stuntz em. Burkart, P. flexuosa D.C. and P. pugionata Burkart, growing in the Reserva Provincial "Los Pocitos", Dpto. de Pocho, Prov. de Crdoba. The insects that visited the inflorescences were sampled, their behavior observed, and contents of nests and pollen carried were analysed. The temperature and the relative humidity were recorded throughout the day during all field-work. Studies on maturation of flowers and nectar production were made throughout the day, and interesting features of flowers were also recorded. The growth of flowers can be divided into the following phases: 1. closed bud; 2. closed bud with protruding style, no nectar, dry stigmatic surface; 3. gradual opening of flower, no nectar, dry stigmatic surface; 4. flower completely open, anthers dehiscent, nectar, and moist stigmatic surface; 5. fall of the stamens and the corolla if the pollination and fertilization occurred before, if not, falling of the flower. These phases indicate that flowers are not protogynous and thus this feature does not support the hypothesis of several authors that protogyny is responsible for the great intraspecific variability in Prosopis. The insects observed and captured that can be indicated as the pollinators of the species of Prosopis studied, are the following: 1. Caupolicana mendocina Jorgensen, 1909; 2. Xylocopa splendidula Lepeletier, 1841 and 3. Apis mellifera Linn, 1758. The pollen content of the nests of the two first species is the following: 1. in a recently provisioned nest of C. mendocina, was 50% pollen from P. flexuosa and 50% pollen from P. chilensis; 2. in a nest with larvae of C. mendocina, 3-colporate grains (Prosopis?) and pantoporate equinulate grains (Nyctaginaceae?, Chenopodiaceae?) whose determination was difficult because of the state of decomposition; 3. in a nest of X. splendidula sampled near a group of trees of P. flexuosa, 100% pollen from P. flexuosa; 4. a nest of X. splendidula sampled near two groups of trees, one of P. flexuosa and the other of P. pugionata, 50% pollen from each one of these two species. The palynological analysis of a sample taken from Apis mellifera indicated a mixed pollen from P. flexuosa and P. pugionata.
23222562|H. chillensis (H.B.K.) Hieron. has a great morphological variability. It hybridizes in nature with two closely related species: H. megapotamica Cabr. and H. microcephala var. albiflora (O.K.) Cabr. The meiosis of the putative hybrids is regular except for the presence of univalents at a low frequency. Male gametes show low stainability. The hybrids have low seed production. The similar karyotypes, previously described by Saez (1951) and the absence of heteromorphic bivalents in the hybrids suggest the existence of cryptic structural hybridity, i.e. of small cryptic structural differences which are difficult to detect cytologically. It is also suggested that the great morphological variability of H. chillensis could be due to introgression of genes from the other two closely related species.

Fernndez-islands). while 2 of the new species on the eastern side of the Cordillera, in Argentina, have still to be found in Chile.

23223216|This paper deals with the interpretation, description and typological characterization of inflorescences in the genus Lippia L. This genus comprises 160 species, mainly distributed in tropical and temperate America, with only a few species growing in the Old World, of which 60 have been studied. The inflorescences are of compound polytelic type, with bracteate capituliform spikes as florescences. The phyllotaxis, form, size and colour of the bracts have taxonomic value, these characters correspond with the sections of the genus. In section Dipterocalyx, the inflorescences are bracteate or frondose-bracteate heterothetic pleiobotrya; in the remaining sections the inflorescences are homothetic pleiobotrya. Series Corymbosae and Paniculatae, and some species of section Dioicolippia, have bracteate or frondose-bracteate inflorescences, while the remaining sections have frondose ones. Section Goniostachyum and subsection Mexicanae have numerous paraclades per axile, while the other sections have 1-2 paraclades per axile. Section Pseudoaloysia (Lippia lasiocalycina Cham.) is characterized by the production of flowers in two stages: first, on bracteate brachyblasts with proliferation and the second on frondose macroblasts, which are originated by the first brachyblasts. The heterothetic pleiobotra have been mentioned as the primitive form from which other inflorescences were derived. If this hypothesis is correct, the species of section Dipterocalyx may possibly be the ancestral group, from which the homothetic pleiobotrya of other sections derived.

23222523|On the occurrence of a "crystalliferous sheat" in the stem of some species of Dioscorea (Dioscoreaceae). An endodermoid sheath with Casparian lines was recognized in the inner boundary of the stem cortex of ten species of Dioscorea from Argentina. Only in Dioscorea multiflora Griseb. and D. hassleriana Chodat there is a "crystalliferous sheath" this denomination is here proposed by inclusion of prismatic and rhomboedral calcium oxalate crystals. The crystal formation is related to the deposition of new cellulose walls, mostly radials; each original endodermal cell is thus converted in a 24 chambered cell. The presence of calcium oxalate crystals in endodermal position is cited for the first time. The "crystalliferous sheath" is present in lignified stems with a high increase in thickness and in a late state of growth. A brief discussion on the probable function is added.

23222567|A comparative study of all 4 members of this genus (R. ephedra (Vent.) Brongn., R. patagonica (Speg.) Tort., R. trinervia (Gill. & Hook.) Hook. & Arn., and R. stricta Hook. & Arn.) pointed out to the following generic traits: generally dorsiventral, hypostomatic leaf structure; mucilaginous epidermis uniformly present; simple, straight to sinuous hairs; dark contents in several tissues (presumably mucilage associated to tannin), often in mesophyll idioblasts; basally acrodromous venation. 41825695|Zoosporic true fungi and fimgal-like organisms include unrelated groups in the kingdoms Fungi, Straminipila and Protozoa. There is very little information on the diversity of these organisms in many ecosystems of great biodiversity, particularly tropical or neotropical areas. Research assessing their diversity has been mainly conducted in Argentina and Brazil using multiple baiting techniques, resulting in the discovery of many new taxa and new records. To date, 434 species in these groups have been recorded for both countries. Continuing research is necessary to provide a more comprehensive understanding of their diversity in South America. Few specialists are available to study such extensive areas, which are being degraded by deforestation, land/clearing, pollution and other anthropogenic activities that affect the habitat of these organisms, long before surveys can be carried out by mycologists and protistologists. Hence, attempts to gather information about the diversity of zoosporic true fungi, heterotrophic Straminipila and Plasmodiophorids from South America are urgently needed, and should receive high priority. Existe escasa informacin disponible acerca de estos organismos en ecosistemas de gran biodiversidad, particularmente en reas tropicales y neotropicales. En Sudamrica, las investigaciones sobre su diversidad han sido principalmente realizadas en Argentina y en Brasil utilizando tcnicas de cebado mltiple, resultando en el descubrimiento de nuevos taxones y nuevas citas. Hasta el momento, en ambos pases se han registrado 434 especies pertenecientes a estos grupos, lo que demuestra que se necesitan ms investigaciones para ampliar su conocimiento en Sudamrica. Existen pocosespecialistas disponibles para estudiar reas tan extensas, las cuales estn siendo degradadas por la deforestacin, la contaminacin, y otras actividades antrpicas que afectan el habitat de estos organismos, antes de que su diversidad pueda ser estudiada por miclogos y protistlogos. De esta forma, los estudios tendientes a reunir informacin sobre la diversidad de los hongos zoospricos verdaderos, los Straminipilas heterotrfcos y los Plasmodioforidios deben ser considerados altamente prioritarios en Sudamrica.

23223908|Paspalum hydrophilum Henrard is a tetraploid, facultative apomictic, pseudogamous and self-compatible species for which occasional diploid and triploid plants have also been found. Three new plant collections from Mato Grosso, Brasil, were cytologically and embryologically surveyed. All three accessions were diploid (2n = 2 x = 20), sexual, and allogamous due to self-incompatibility. Reciprocal crosses concerning two diploid P. hydrophilum accessions and one plant of diploid P. palustre Mez produced several interspecific hybrids. Crossability, the number of hybrids obtained for every 100 pollinated spikelets, ranged from approximately 8% to 28%. The hybrids showed regular meiotic behaviour with 10 bivalent chromosome associations at meiosis, indicating a high chromosome homology among these species. The F hybrids inherited self-incompatibility from both parents, attributable to pollen-pistil interactions that arrested pollen tube growth at the central axis of the stigma. Low seed fertility was observed under open pollination. Seed performance ranged up to approximately 23% when parental pollen was dusted on hybrids. This performance may allow to transfer genes among these species. Our results showed a close phylogenetic relationship between P. hydrophilum and P. palustre and indicate the feasibility of interspecific genetic exchange. Though the distribution area of P. palustre overlaps the more extensive area of P. hydrophilum, natural hybridization was not observed. Allopatry of the diploid cytotypes of these species may account for lack of natural hydrization. Paspalum hydrophilum Henrard es una especie tetraploide, apomctica facultativa, pseudgama y autocompatible. Tambin se ha mencionado la existencia ocasional de plantas diploides y triploides. Aqu se estudian tres nuevas colecciones de plantas originarias de Mato Grosso, Brasil. Las tres resultaron ser diploides (2n = 2x = 20), sexuales, y algamas debido a autoincompatibilidad. Se lograron varios hbridos interespecficos al realizar cruzamientos recprocos entre una planta diploide de P.palustre Mez y dos de las plantas de P.hydrophilum. La capacidad de producir hbridos vari entre el 8 y el 28% de las espiguillas polinizadas. Los hbridos logrados mostraron meiosis regular con formacin de 10 bivalentes, indicando un alto grado de homologa entre los cromosomas de estas especies. Los hbridos heredaron de los padres la autoincompatibilidad, y en general produjeron muy pocas semillas en polinizacin libre. La polinizacin con polen de los padres aument la produccin de semillas, llegando en algunos casos hasta el 23% de las espiguillas polinizadas. Este nivel de fertilidad en retrocruzas indica que es posible la transferencia de genes entre estas especies. A pesar de que el rea de distribucin de P. palustre abarca parte del rea general de distribucin de P. hydrophilum, no hemos registrado en los herbarios ejemplares con caractersticas semejantes a los hbridos logrados ni hemos observado en el campo plantas que pudiesen ser consideradas hbridas.

23222556|The isoenzymatic patterns of aspartate amine transferase (AAT=GOT) have been studied in individuals belonging to five populations of Bulnesia retama (Gillies ex Hook.) Griseb., three of them from La Rioja, one from Mendoza, Argentina, and one from Per. AAT evidenced dimeric structure in this species and depending on the stage analized, two or three zones of AAT activity were observed. This would imply that at least three loci are controlling the AAT isozymes. The Argentine populations were polymorphic for thee three loci with a mean expected heterozygosity per locus (H) varying from 0.536 (Mendoza) to 0.398 (La Rioja). The Peruvian sample, separated from the Argentine populations by an extensive gap of more than 1600 Km, showed polymorphism in only one locus and its mean expected heterozygosity ([symbol]) was 0.164. This lower variation could be due to strong selection in an extreme environment or more likely a consequence of long distance dispersal by one or very few migrants from Southern latitudes (founder effect). Since there is evidence that B. retama is self-compatible, an entire population could have been originated by a single migrant.

23223243|Three floral phases were distinguished through anthesis, which starts after 1 p.m. Flowers in phase 1 and 3 (pollen donors) had their stigmas up. Flowers in phase 2 (receptors and donors of pollen) had their stigmas recurved near the anthers. Flowers in phase 2 occurred simultaneously with others in phase 1, during the day, and also with others in phase 3 (during the night). Sugar concentration in nectar varied: it was acceptable for Hymenoptera in the afternoon (when Xylocopa spp. and Centris spp. pollinate) and for sphingids after sunset (when Erinnyis ello seems to pollinate). Passiflora mooreana is melitophilous, but also is a resource for moths in the evening. Flowers showed a low degree of autoincompatibility. The low percent of fruits obtained suggests that the great distance between plants does not favor crosspollination. The ovary wall may grow without pollination.

23218907|Stomatal crypts in the leaves of Eupatorium bupleurifolium (Compositae). The leaf anatomy of Eupatorium bupleurifolium De Candolle has been studied, with special reference to the occurrence of stomatal crypts. In these crypts situated on both epidermis, where near all the stomata are confined, 2 different types of glandular hairs are also present: a biseriate one sunken at the bottom of the cavity, flanked commonly by 2 uniseriate ones. No differences were observed in the crypt characters in specimens collected in humid as well as in dry habitats, not accomplishing therefore in this species a protective function of the stomata. Other leaf anatomical characters include: cuticle smooth or striated, anomocytic stomata, isolateral mesophyll with the palisade tissue less developed on the abaxial surface; midrib with simple or compound vascular system whether or not accompanied by sclerenchyma, bundle sheath complete enclosing vascular bundles and adaxial secretory canals accompanying them. As a result of a preliminary literature survey accomplished on the subject the occurrence of stomatal crypts has not been reported previously for this large genus; likewise this character was also absent in several Argentine species studied here, being therefore a diagnostic feature for E. bupleurifolium. A discussion about the influence of ecological factors on the occurrence of foliar crypts in other plants is also given.

23223192|The present treatment deals with different structural variations of the spikelets in the following genera of the tribe Paniceae (Poaceae): Anthaenantiopsis Mez ex Pilg., Axonopus P. Beauv., Digitaria Haller, Lasiacis (Griseb.) Hitchc., Panicum L., Paspalum L., Reimarochloa Hitchc. and Urochloa P. Beauv. This tribe shows a reductive tendency in the development of the spikelets, mainly in morphological and reproductive characters, with regards to the number of flowers and bracts of the spikelets (glumes, lemmas and paleas) and "sexuality" of the flowers. Typical biflowered spikelets is the most common pattern among the studied genera; three-flowered spikelets are always present in Panicum quadriglume (Dll) Hitchc. and Lasiacis anomala Hitchc., being occasional in Anthaenantiopsis fiebrigii Parodi, A. perforata (Nees) Parodi var. perforata, Panicum crateriferum Sohns and P. grumosum Nees. Extension of the rachilla above the upper anthoecium is common in biflowered spikelets of Lasiacis and Urochloa, being exceptional in Panicum and Anthaenantiopsis. This study also concludes that there is variation in the "sexuality" of the flowers in the spikelets: the lower flower may be perfect, staminate or neutral, while the upper one is always perfect in the biflowered ones. In the three-flowered spikelets, the lower flower may be staminate or neutral, the medium one perfect, staminate or neutral, while the upper flower is always perfect. The occurrence of the extension of the rachilla is considered as a possible vestigial character, which represents the transition from many-flowered to few-flowered spikelets.

23228246|Present medicinal plant uses of the Chorote indians of Semiarid Chaco, is identified here. Sixty nine (69) plant species, 2 fungi species and 1 lichen with 194 medicinal uses, are recorded. A low proportion of medicinal uses regarding total ethnobotanical data (15 %), is highlighted. More than a half of such plant uses (52 %) were found identical from those recorded for their Criollo neighbours, concluding that these practices would have been incorporated as a kind of cultural loan. Chorote's pharmacopoeia would have been very reduced in the past owned to the shamanistic nature of their traditional medicine, in which medicinal plants would not have played a significant role. Among Chorote's medicinal plants Achatocarpus praecox, Cleistocactus baumannii, Echinopsis rhodotricha and Funastrum clausum, could be quoted. Ninety Chorote's strictly plant remedies could be counted, mainly as antiemmenagogic; antidiarrheic, for coughs and as cicatrizant. Se identifica la farmacopea vegetal que utilizan actualmente los indgenas Chorote del Chaco semirido argentino. Se registraron 69 especies vegetales, 2 especies de hongos y un liquen con 194 usos medicinales. Se destaca el bajo porcentaje de este tipo de usos respecto al total de datos etnobotnicos recopilados para los Chorote (15 %). De su comparacin con la farmacopea criolla se desprende que el 52 % de los datos resulta idntico, por lo que se concluye que los Chorote habran adquirido estas prcticas a manera de prstamo cultural. La farmacopea de este pueblo, entonces, fue muy reducida debido a que su medicina tradicional de corte chamanstico no involucraba antao el uso de remedios de origen vegetal. Entre las plantas medicinales tpicamente Chorote se pueden citar a Achatocarpus praecox, Cleistocactus baumannii, Echinopsis rhodotricha y Funastrum clausum. Los usos estrictamente Chorote quedaran as reducidos a 90 aplicaciones en total, principalmente como antiemenagogos, antidiarreicos, antitusivos y cicatrizantes.

23218957|Emilia fosbergii (Asteraceae) introduced in Argentina. The widespread annual weed of the American tropics, Emilia fosbergii Nicolson was collected in northern Argentina (Iguaz National Park, Misiones Province), in moistured rocky areas. Its occurrence in the National Park has increased the range of dispersion of this exotic tetraploid species near two degrees South, and ca. six degrees West from the Atlantic coast, at the southern limit, and it is a consequence of the disturbance of the natural vegetation in the area. The tetraploid nature (n = 10) of the Argentine population was determined. Emilia Cass. is also a new adventitious generic record for Argentina.

23218122|Floristic-structural study of a semideciduous forest area from Norwestern Argentina I. Floristic composition, density and diversity. Three types of semideciduous montane forest, situated at 2445' South latitude and at 950 and 1050 m.a.s.l., are described. The climate is strongly stational, rainfalls occur mainly in summer. The most important families are Myrtaceae, Leguminosae, Polygonaceae, Nyctaginaceae and Urticaceae. The density determined was 264 to 337 individuals per hectare, amounting to 40 tree species in the 5 hectares sampled. Basal area was 21 to 30 m per hectare. The classification of the forest and the floristic and structural differences of the three types are discussed. Finally, a table is presented with density and diversity data of similar works in some neotropical forests.
23218073|In this work the author studies the rehabilitation of the genus Maihueniopsis Speg. analysing the generic differences among this genus, Puna and Tephrocactus, the former two segregated from the latter. It also includes a chapter on the organography of Tephrocactus compared with the segregated genera. The following are the principal characters on which the segregation is based: Tephrocactus species are lax shrubs, with crypt-shaped areoles, red glochids; spines of scaly epidermical cells orientated towards the apex (contrary to what is normal in Opuntioideae), dry and dehiscent fruits, seeds with auriculated, soft aerenchymatic aril. These plants grow in Argentine low deserts. Maihueniopsis species are compact cushions with more or less cylindric normally developed areoles, usually yellowish glochids, smooth spines, fleshy indehiscent fruits, soft to very hard nonaerenchymatic aril, these without auricles. These plants grow in very high mountains and in the Patagonian plateu, from Ecuador to Chile and Argentina. In the case of the two species of Puna, the visible parts of these plants consist of only a few segments wich grow at ground-level; their cylindric areoles have no glochids except in the lowest ones in P. subterranea. In the only two species of this genus, the epidermical cells of the spines are grouped into longitudinal lines and though, separated among themselves, they are lengthwise joined to the central body of the spine. Their flowers have reduced areoles. Fruits are dry, indehiscent; the seed arilus cover is soft, hairy-like. These plants grow in highlands between 2.000 and 4.000 m a.s.l. The taxonomical treatment includes: key to the Opuntioideae genera wich grow in Argentina and for the species of Tephrocactus and the Argentine ones of Maihueniopsis, descriptions, data on geographical distribution and ecology, ilustrations and exiccata. The following new combinations are given: Maihueniopsis darwinii var. hickenii (Br. et Rose) Kiesling, M. minuta (Backbg.) Kiesling, M. boliviana (S.-D.) Kiesling, M. nigrispina (K. Schum.) Kiesling y M. pentlandii (S.-D.) Kiesling. Several neotypes are designated.

23216524|The study of the descriptions of Cactus peruvianus Linn and Cereus peruvianus Mill. shows that these two species have to be considered as different; the former still "dubius" and the last one belonging to Stenocereus (S. peruvianus (Mill.) nov. comb.) Based on a wrong name given by A. P. De Candolle in 1800 and 1828, every author since then has used the name Cereus peruvianus for a species of Cereus s. s. from S-Brasil, Uruguay and NE of Argentina. This species had never been correctely described. Here, it is described as Cereus uruguayanus Ritter ex Kiesling, nov. sp. In 1909 Britton and Rose used Cereus peruvianus as typus species for Cereus. Later, in 1920, they correct this, giving Cereus hexagonus as typus; wich gives stability to all the names within Cereus s. s.

23213870|The author reports on chromosome number counts made on 17 species of Chenopodium from Argentina, whose flora has about 30 species of this genus. The counts were made in root-tip cells or with microsporocytes. Only from 7 of the treated species the chromosome number was known from other authors (see Table I). The results are given in Table II. Most of the counts are from species of the section Chenopodia (11 species, from the 3 remaining ones no material could be obtained). As a result the author states that two basic chromosome numbers are found: the sections Roubieva, Orthosporum and Ambrina have x = 8; the sections Botrys, Degenia, Thellungia and Chenopodia have x = 9. These basic chromosome numbers were constant in every section. As to the taxonomy of the genus, the author followed, with some minor changes, the system of Aellen and Just (1943), which proved to be very useful.
23223228|An inventory of the types of Gramineae wich originally came from Berlin herbarium (B) and kept in the Gaspar Xurez herbarium (BAA), has been made. A total of 310 types (fragments of holotypes, isotypes and isosyntypes) which belong to South American taxa, were analyzed. The types have been ordered alphabetically; bibliographical and label data, characteristics of the material, the numbering of samples and up to date identification was included within each entry. This collection belonged to the agrostologist Lorenzo R. Parodi, who in 1936 visited different European herbaria, including Berlin. Parodi obtained isotypes and fragments from (B) through Robert Pilger. When he returned to Argentina the material was ordered and preserved for more than 30 years in his private herbarium. After his death in 1966, his herbarium was donated by his wife to the Gaspar Xuarez herbarium (BAA), where it can be found today.

23222972|The anatomy of young branches of Lessonia nigrescens Bory from central Chile was analyzed using light and transmission electron microscopy. Three regions are recognized: meristoderm, cortex, and medulla. The meristoderm is a few cell layers thick. Cortical cells have several primary pit fields with plasmodesmata 33-60 nm in diameter. Indirect evidence from pit field distribution suggests that symplasmic transport is mainly longitudinal in the inner cortex. The medulla contains hyphae, that originate from the inner cortical cells, and trumpet filaments. These cell systems do not communicate with each other. The hyphae have plasmodesmata in their cross walls, apparently in primary pit fields. The trumpet filaments have sieve areas in the transverse walls, with pores 70-170 nm in diameter. Occasionally, callose accumulates in some of these sieve areas. In general, cell walls are composed of microfibrils which are arranged in lamellae. The cell walls are surrounded by an intercellular matrix, which is more abundant in the medulla than in the meristoderm and the cortex.

23222559|The comparative anatomy and development of fruit and seed in some South American members of three Solaneae genera have been studied -all the species of Aureliana, two of Athenaea and three of Capsicum. Our findings support the point of view of those authors who consider these genera as related but independent.

23228354|The archaeological record of Ambato valley, in northwestern Argentina, has the particularity of preserving the timber used in the construction of the settlings, due to the fires that affected the region by the 11th century. We taxonomically identified 105 sample trunks, used as posts and beams in the construction of the "Iglesia de los Indios" and "Piedras Blancas". The anthracological analysis revealed differences in the choice of timber, as for the Piedras Blancas site the material was from the valley itself, while for the Iglesia de los Indios site the timber came from outside. Based on those results, we discuss similarities and particularities between both sites about the selection, use and meaning of the different forest resources. El registro arqueolgico del Valle de Ambato en el Noroeste argentino presenta la particularidad de preservar las maderas empleadas en la construccin de los asentamientos, debido a incendios ocurridos en la zona hacia el siglo XI d.C. Esta peculiaridad ha permitido recuperar hasta el momento abundante material. Se realiz la identificacin taxonmica de muestras correspondientes a 105 troncos utilizados como postes y vigas en la construccin de los sitios "Iglesia de los Indios" y "Piedras Blancas". Los anlisis antracolgicos presentaron resultados sensiblemente diferentes, habindose empleado para la Iglesia de los Indios materias primas alctonas al valle, contrariamente a lo que ocurre en el sitio Piedras Blancas. Sobre esta base se discuten las correspondencias entre ambos sitios en torno a la seleccin, usos y significados de los distintos recursos forestales.
23213897|The present paper is a synopsis of the 5 species of the genus Ayenia section Ayenia which bear leaf nectaries. These are: A. conciliata (subsection Conciliatae), A. stipularis, A. Cuatrecasae (subsection Stipulares), A. praeclara and a new species which we name A. Klugii (subsection Praeclarae). In addition, the structure of the nectaries of each one of these species is described, and it was found that they are very similar to those described for species of Byttneria (Arbo, 1971 ined.,) and for diverse Malvaceae (Janda, 1937). The only exception is A. praeclara, which has nectaries identical, in their external aspect, to those of some Byttneriae, but which are characterized by roundish lysigenous cavities which open outward through pores. The other species present glandular hairs embedded in a multiseriate epidermis. Besides, A. praeclara is the most closely related especies to A. Klugii nov. sp., so that the anatomical differences found are of great taxonomical interest.

23230215|Flowering in bamboo is an unusual event. Documenting flowering individuals or populations provides valuable information about bamboo life cycles. Bambusa tuldoides is endemic to China but widely cultivated around the world. In Argentina, the first record of its cultivation dates back to 1943. There are no records of caryopses formation of this species in Argentina. We here report the flowering of a cultivated B. tuldoides clump and gather information about previous flowering events for this species in Argentina and neighboring countries occurring in the literature and herbarium collections. With this information, we estimate the flowering cycle of B. tuldoides in southernmost America to be approximately 23 years. Viable seed production is reported for the first time in Argentina. La floracin de un bamb es un evento particular. El registro de la floracin de una mata o una poblacin aporta datos precisos sobre los ciclos biolgicos. Bambusa tuldoides es una especie endmica de China y est ampliamente cultivada en todo el mundo. En la Argentina, la primera referencia sobre su cultivo es de 1943. No se han registrado fructificaciones de esta especie en la Argentina. Registramos la floracin de un ejemplar de B. tuldoides en cultivo y recolectamos datos sobre otros eventos de floracin de esta especie en la Argentina y pases limtrofes. Con esta informacin, estimamos el ciclo de floracin de B. tuldoides en Amrica austral en 23 aos aproximadamente. Registramos la produccin de frutos viables por primera vez en Argentina.

23223015|The karyotypes, number of satellites and maximal nucleoli number are recorded for Ephedra ochreata Miers (10 m + 4 st, 6 SAT, 6 nucleoli), E. rupestris Benth. (10 m + 4 st, 4 SAT, 4 nucleoli) and E. viridis Coville (20 m + 8 st, 8 SAT). Diploid and polyploid taxa of Ephedra are based on a fundamental haplokaryotype composed of 5 m and 2 smaller st, which is presumed to be very old (150 million years ago or more, before the final dismemberment of the Pangea) as it occurs in Asia, Africa and both Americas and in different sections of the genus. Ephedra is an example of extreme karyotype conservation.

23223869|The length and diameter of buds were studied for Nothofagus pumilio and N. dombeyi (Fagaceae) in shoots from different types of axes of young trees growing in natural conditions. Variations in bud length according to bud position on the shoot and on the tree were assessed. In both species, shoots with more than 20 nodes developed buds with wide ranges of length and number of nodes, whereas smaller shoots always developed small buds consisting of a low number of nodes. In shoots with more than 20 nodes, bud length was maximum in buds close to the shoot's distal end. Buds of N. pumilio were almost twice longer and wider than those of N. dombeyi for each shoot size category considered. The number of nodes for buds of a given length was higher for N. dombeyi than N. pumilio. Multiple linear regressions including bud length, bud diameter, bud position on its parent shoot, and number of nodes of the parent shoot as independent variables, explained 81% and 74% of the variation in the number of leaf primordia per bud for N. pumilio and N. dombeyi respectively. Se estudi la longitud y el dimetro de yemas de Nothofagus pumilio y N. dombeyi (Fagaceae) en brotes procedentes de diferentes tipos de ejes de rboles jvenes desarrollados en condiciones naturales. Se evaluaron las variaciones de la longitud de las yemas segn su posicin sobre el brote portador y sobre el rbol. En ambas especies, los brotes con ms de 20 nudos desarrollaron yemas con un amplio rango de longitudes y de nmero de nudos, mientras que los brotes ms cortos desarrollaron siempre yemas pequeas y de bajo nmero de nudos. Para los brotes con ms de 20 nudos, las yemas de mayor tamao fueron aquellas prximas al extremo distal del brote. Las yemas de N. pumilio fueron aproximadamente dos veces ms largas y anchas que las de N. dombeyi en una posicin similar. Para cada longitud de yema considerada, el nmero de nudos de la yema fue mayor para N. dombeyi que para N. pumilio. Regresiones lineares mltiples que incluyeron como variables independientes a la longitud y el dimetro de la yema, la posicin de la yema sobre el brote portador y el nmero de nudos del brote portador, permitieron explicar el 81% y el 74% de la variacin en el nmero de nudos por yema de N. pumilio y de N. dombeyi, respectivamente.

23212149|A detailed study, based upon new materials and cultures, as well as typical specimens, of Poroniopsis Bruchi Speg., led to the conclusion that this genus belongs to the Fungi Imperfecti rather than the Ascomycetes as described, and that it is synonymous with Hypocreodendron sanguineum P. Henn. The sterile stromatic form Rhizomorpha formicarum Speg., is considered also a synonym. It could not be ascertained whether Xylaria is the perfect stage. The fungus develops well in culture  the description of which is added  and forms conidial heads on the stroma, which are phototropic. The conidiophores arise in palisades, and some are naked, whilst others are formed in nests which assume the aspect of "pycnidia" in the specimens collected in nature.

23226689|Alstroemeria (Alstroemeriaceae) is a genus endemic to South America. In Chile, this genus is distributed from the northern end to Patagonia, with a diversification center in central Chile. Precisely in this central zone grows Alstroemeria ligtu with its three subspecies: A. ligtu subsp. incarnata, A. ligtu subsp. simsii and A. ligtu subsp. ligtu. A comparative study of the karyotype with DAPI or acetic orcein of 5 populations of A. ligtu subsp. ligtu from the VIII Region, and one population of A. ligtu subsp. simsii from the V Region was made. The karyotype observed in these six studied populations was asymmetric, with 2n=2x=16 chromosomes. The populations of A. ligtu subsp. ligtu presented a haploid formula conformed by four metacentric chromosomes (pairs 1 and 2 with microsatellites), one submetacentric chromosome with a microsatellite, and three telocentric chromosomes with microsatellites. The haploid formula of A. ligtu subsp. simsii was: five metacentric chromosomes (pair 2 with a microsatellite, and pair 6 with a secondary constriction) and three telocentric chromosomes with satellite. Therefore, the karyotype of A. ligtu is variable, and changes at chromosomal level have probably contributed to the diversification of this species. 23218953|Effect of prolongued floodings in a grassland of the Salado Basin (Province of Buenos Aires - Argentine) - Dynamics of the grassland as a whole and of Ambrosia tenuifolia (Asteraceae). This paper deals with the response of Ambrosia tenuifolia and other species of the Salado Basin grasslands to a long flood period. The following are the main conclusions: 1) Ambrosia tenuifolia and others dictoyledonous species do not tolerate floods of large duration such as the one occured in 1978 in the Salado Basin. 2) Grasses do not stop growing during the flood period and might therefore occupy niches released by the affected dicotyledonous.
23225132|This is a revision of Danaea, the only neotropical genus of the Marattiaceae. Several collections were analized, and both external and internal detailed morphology of the sporophyte was studied. Taxonomy of the species, a key to identify them, comments on their affinities, geographical distribution, altitudinal range, cytology and ecology are also given. Seventeen species of the genus are recognized: D. alata, D. carillensis, D. crispa, D. elliptica, D. humilis, D. imbricata, D. jenmanii, D. mazeana, D. moritziana, D. nodosa, D. oblanceolata, D. plicata, D. simplicifolia, D. tenera, D. trichomanoides, D. ulei and D. wendlandii. Danaea shares several characters with the other four marattiaceous genera (Angiopteris, Archangiopteris, Christensenia and Marattia), as naked, carnose polycyclostelic amylaceous rhizomes with internal collenchymatous tissues, excentric simple starch grains, geminate stipules, pulvinules, types of epidermal patterns of the laminae, marattiaceous stomata, presence of intercellular pectic protuberances in the mesophyll cells (IPP), and mucilage secreting system. However, postrate and erect rhizomes; number of pulvinules in the stipes; simple or 1-pinnate, dimorphic laminae; pinna outline; entire, undulate or crispate pinna margins; glandular indument (both mucilaginiferous trichomes and protoscales); lamina texture; venation patterns; epidermal patterns of the epiphylls and hypophylls which vary at the specific level; both normal and porocyclocytic marattiaceous stomata; mostly filamentose IPP, and the morphology of the exopore in echinate spores are considered good diagnostic characters related to Danaea. Division of the lamina, indument, lamina and pinna outline, number of pinnae, type of pinna margin, lamina texture, venation patterns, presence or absence of terminal pinnae or gemae, and color of veins and the hypophylls are good morphological characteres to identify the species both in fresh and dry specimens, and they were used to prepare the key to identify the species, along with other traits such as rhizome types, which can be additionally useful to complete plant identifications in the field.
