23222525|On the nectary, nectar and floral visitors in Ligaria cuneifolia (Loranthaceae). Nectary structure, nectar-chemical composition, and floral visitors were studied in natural populations of the monotypical genus Ligaria Tieghem. Blooming takes place from autumn to spring. Flowers are perfect, hexamerous, actinomorphic, chasmogamous, and protandrous. The showy red monochlamideous perianth forms a tube in its lower part due to interwoven papilla-like epidermal cells from contiguous tepals. Stamens are adnate to the tube and anthers are dorsifixed and versatile. The ovary is inferior and the style is cylindrical bearing a stylar nectary in its base. Hemiparacytic stomata were found on the apical part of the nectary. This species is hummingbird-pollinated. Chlorostilbon aureoventris was observed cropping nectar. These hummingbirds tend to be intra-specifically territorial. Bumblebees (Xylocopa sp.) are L. cuneifolia (R. et P.) Tieghem nectar-robers piercing the tubular base of the perianth to take the nectar. Considering the nectar chemical composition, no significant variation was detected among the three studied samples of Ligaria growing on three different host plants. The mean sugar nectar composition was found to be of a sucrose-dominant species: 56.5%, 15.9%, and 27.5% for sucrose, fructose, and glucose respectively. Amino acids, lipids, reducing acids, and phenols were detected in all samples, whereas alkaloids and proteins were not. The range of sugar concentration was 28-36% according to the sample.

23218940|Phenetics of Chuquiraga (Compositae-Mutisieae): a numerical analysis. Cluster analysis (UPGMA) and ordination by principal component analysis (PCA) were performed on the data of 52 morphological characters from the 19 species of xerophyllous bushes of the Southamerican (Andean-Patagonian) genus Chuquiraga. The results generally agree in the formation of two large groups which match with sections Chuquiraga and Acanthophylla of the previous classification. Section Chuquiraga seems to be more variable in respect to discriminatory characters than sect. Acanthophylla, and also has a more ample latitudinal distribution. Within this first section two subgroups, which correspond with series Chuquiraga and Parviflora, appeared in the PCA analysis. In most of the numerical treatments section Acanthophylla shows three distinct subgroups which also have distinct distributions, specially in regard to elevation. The characters that discriminate all these groups in the genus are principally the anatomical and exomorphological structures of the leaves, the presence or absence of axillary spines, and the length of the capitulum, all of which coincide with diagnostic characters used to define these sections and series in previous works. These characters not only show some relation with physical factors such as latitude and altitude and associated climatic variations, but also with biotic factors such as type of pollinator (hummingbirds or insects). This suggests that both climatic changes and shift in pollination syndromes may have affected the evolution and diversification of the genus.

Fourteen qualitative and quantitative characters were registered and multivariate analysis was applied to the data obtained. Three well differenciated groups of individuals could be distinguished, constituited by: 1) tetraploid plants of P. distichum, 2) pentaploid, hiperpentaploid and hexaploid plants of P. distichum and 3) P. vaginatum.

B chromosomes were observed in two species. In Aspilia aurantiaca 3 IB were observed. A persistent body was observed in first division up to telophase I in this species. 23224213|A detailed floristic inventory as well as a preliminary phytogeographical analysis was conducted in an Andean secondary wet forest of NW of Colombia, in order to know the vascular species richness and the phytogeographical relationships. The floristic inventory revealed the presence of 712 vascular species distributed among 129 families, of which 17 belong to ferns and allies, with 69 species and 30 genera; 18 monocotyledon families, with 153 species and 87 genera, and 94 dicotyledon families, with 490 species and 290 genera. The best-represented plant families are Melastomataceae (36 species), Rubiaceae (36), Orchidaceae (30), Asteraceae (28), Poaceae (28), Piperaceae (24), Araceae (23), Fabaceae (20), Clusiaceae (18), Moraceae (18), Gesneriaceae (17), Mimosaceae (16), Solanaceae (15), Acanthaceae (14), and Polypodiaceae (13). The richest genera are Piper (17 species), Ficus (11), Psychotria (11), Inga (10), Anthurium (9), Miconia (9), Peperomia (7), Asplenium (6), Blechnum (6), Clidemia (6), Costus (6), Mikania (6), Selaginella (6), and Solanum (6). Regarding life forms, herbs are the best represented with 344 species (48,2%), followed by shrubs and trees (291 species, 41%), lianas (62 species, 8,7%), palms (12 species, 1,7%) and by arborescent herbs (3 species, 0,4%). There are 101 epiphytic or hemiepiphytic species belonging to 23 families. The richest families in epiphytes are Orchidaceae (23 species), Araceae (10), Bromeliaceae (8), Piperaceae (7) and Gesneriaceae (6), while the most common epiphytic genera are Peperomia (7 species), Anthurium (6), Elaphoglossum (5), Huperzia (4) and Trichomanes (4). There are 9 endemic species (1,3%). Some of the species collected are new to science or are new records for the flora of NW of South America. Nine species and 3 genera exhibit a disjunct distribution. The analyzed forest is floristically similar to lowland Neotropical forests. The phytogeographic analysis shows that 62,4% of the genera are neotropical, 25,8% are pantropical, 10% are cosmopolitan, 1,8% are holarctic, and that 15 genera have a tropical amphipacific distribution. Nine genera are confined to South America. Although the area studied was strongly modified, only 8 species are introduced or naturalized. The frequency of disturbances, such as fire, grazing, cutting, selective cutting, abandoned cultivat fields, maintains the area at early successional stages. 23230231|Gomesa bifolia (Orchidaceae, Cymbidieae, Oncidiinae) is an epiphytic orchid that presents showy yellow flowers with brown markings on sepals and petals, fragranceless and with oil as reward. The floral biology of this species was studied in cultivated individuals to describe phenology, flower longevity, reproductive system (using manipulative treatment of cross-pollination vs. self-pollination) and floral pollinators. Moreover, direct observations were made on plants exposed outdoors to identify pollinators, describing their foraging behavior and the duration of visits. The results showed that G. bifolia is a mainly self-incompatible, non-autogamous and pollinator-dependent species. The fruit set in manually cross-pollination flowers (100%) was higher than the manually self-pollinated flowers (30.8%), whereas the control flowers did not set fruits. Females of Centris trigonoides (Apidae, Centridini) were the exclusive pollinators, and the visit rate was low. Several Neotropical orchids of the subtribe Oncidiinae offer floral oils to the pollinators, like the Malpighiaceae familiy. Our results allow inferring that both groups of plants would be part of a guild of species pollinated by oil-collecting bees and that the deceit/pollination syndrome should not be applied to all Oncidiinae flowers. Gomesa bifolia (Orchidaceae, Cymbidieae, Oncidiinae) es una orqudea epfita que presenta vistosas flores amarillas con marcas marrones en los spalos y ptalos, carentes de fragancia y con aceite como recompensa. La biologa floral de esta especie fue estudiada en individuos cultivados para describir la fenologa, longevidad floral, conocer el sistema reproductivo (mediante tratamientos manipulativos de auto-polinizacin vs. polinizacin cruzada) y sus polinizadores. Adems, se realizaron observaciones directas sobre plantas expuestas al aire libre para identificar a los polinizadores, describiendo su comportamiento de forraje y la duracin de las visitas. Los resultados obtenidos revelan que G. bifolia es una especie principalmente auto-incompatible, no autgama y dependiente de sus polinizadores. La formacin de frutos en flores tratadas con polinizacin cruzada manual (100%) fue superior a las flores manualmente auto-polinizadas (30,8%); mientras que las flores no tratadas no formaron frutos. Los nicos polinizadores observados fueron hembras de Centris trigonoides (Apidae, Centridini), y la tasa de visitas fue baja. Numerosas orqudeas Neotropicales de la subtribu Oncidiinae ofrecen aceites florales a sus polinizadores, como lo hacen los representantes de la familia Malpighiaceae. Los resultados obtenidos tambin permiten inferir que ambos grupos de plantas estaran formando parte de un gremio de especies polinizadas por abejas colectoras de aceites y que el sndrome de polinizacin por engao no es verdadero para todas las especies de Oncidiinae.

23223906|The objective was to characterize floral structure and to analyze intraspecific flower variability in G. decorticans (Gillies ex Hok. et Arn.) Burkart, from the view of its reproductive biology. In order to this, three populations of G. decorticans from central Argentina were studied considering the morphology and anatomy of reproductive floral traits. The quantified variables were: size of the complete flower; corolla, anther cycles and gynoecium length; anther-stigma separation; number of pollen grains and ovules per flower; and number and size of nectarial stomata. The protogynous flowers are small (less than 1 cm), yellow, and they are arranged in racemes. The stamens (9 + 1) form two pentamerous cycles of different length. The gynoecium is composed by a hairy ovary with a style variable in length. Thus, the stigma can be observed over or under the position of the anthers. The nectary is persistent. Its upper part is located at the base of the staminal tube whereas its base is fused with the receptacle. Gynoecium and style length were positively correlated, whereas both flower size and filament length were inversely correlated to anther-stigma separation. In a broad sense, flower structure appears to be stable in G. decorticans. However, some characters were variable such as flower size and the number of nectarial estomata. This flower traits variation may affect pollination and/or seed set. Tres poblaciones de Geoffroea decorticans (Gillies ex Hok. et Arn.) Burkart de Argentina central fueron estudiadas con el objetivo de caracterizar la estructura de las flores y analizar la variabilidad floral intraespecfica, desde una perspectiva de la biologa reproductiva. Se consideraron la morfologa y anatoma de las estructuras florales y se cuantificaron los siguientes caracteres: longitud floral, de la corola, de los ciclos de filamentos estaminales y del gineceo, separacin antera-estigma, nmero de granos de polen y de vulos por flor, nmero y tamao de los estomas del nectario. Las flores son protginas, pequeas (menores de 1 cm), amarillas y estn reunidas en racimos. Los estambres (9+1) forman dos ciclos pentmeros de distinta longitud. El gineceo presenta ovario pubescente y estilo de longitud variable. De este modo, el estigma puede observarse por encima o por debajo de la posicin de las anteras. El nectario es persistente. Su parte superior est ubicada en la base del tubo estaminal, mientras que la porcin inferior se fusiona con el receptculo. El largo del gineceo se correlaciona positivamente con el largo del estilo, mientras que el tamao de la flor y el de los filamentos se correlacionan inversamente con la separacin antera-estigma. En lneas generales, la estructura floral es estable en G. decorticans. Sin embargo, algunos caracteres que resultaron variables, como el tamao floral y la cantidad de estomas del nectario, podran afectar la polinizacin y/o la produccin de semillas.
23225125|Based on the caryotype and colour of dry scales in dormant bulbs, Nothoscordum serenense is transferred to Zoellnerallium. Furthermore, the validity of the genus Zoellnerallium is justified on chromosome and morphological grounds. Se propone subordinar Nothoscordum serenense, al gnero Zoellnerallium, basado en observaciones cariolgicas y en la coloracin de los catafilos secos de los bulbos en latencia. Adems, se presenta una justificacin del gnero Zoellnerallium basada en evidencias cromosmicas y morfolgicas.
23222569|This is the first paper of a chemotaxonomic serial studies of the subtribe Phaseolinae in Argentina, wich comprises the generic complex Phaseolus-Vigna-Macroptilium. Chromatographic patterns of 8 species of the genus Macroptilium were determined. Cluster analysis and ordination by principal coordinates analysis were applied to 36 chemical characters ("spots") leading to two distinct groups. These results corroborate the previous taxonomic treatment for this genus based on morphological and palynological studies. Chemical evidence seems to support the sections Macroptilium and Microcochle proposed by Lackey according to Piper, as well as the natural grouping of the species in each of these taxa.
23223887|Synflorescence typology of Neotropical genus Axonopus P. Beauv. was studied using the methodology and the terminology of Troll's school. Fifty two species of ca. 75 species of Axonopus were analized. In all taxa the synflorescence is polytelic and truncate. According to this study, the plesiomorphic flowering unit is found in the series Barbigeri G. A. Black. The synflorescence could be derived from an ancestral form by the following evolutionary steps: 1.- truncation of the main axis; 2.complete homogenization; 3.- reduction of the short paracladia; 4.- decrease of the number of long paracladia; 5.- truncation of the long paracladia. Morphological relationships are discussed and some probable evolutionary trends are outlined. Se estudi la tipologa de la sinflorescencia del gnero neotropical Axonopus P. Beauv. utilizando la metodologa y terminologa de la escuela de Troll. Se analizaron representantes de 52 de las ca. 75 especies del gnero. En todas las especies la sinflorescencia es politlica y truncada. De acuerdo con este estudio, la unidad de floracin plesiomrfica se encuentra en la serie Barbigeri G. A. Black. La sinflorescencia de Axonopus pudo derivarse de una forma ancestral a travs de los siguientes pasos: 1.- truncamiento del eje principal; 2.- homogeneizacin completa; 3.- reduccin de los paracladios cortos; 4.- disminucin del nmero de paracladios largos y 5.- truncamiento de los paracladios largos. Se discuten las relaciones morfolgicas y se comentan algunas posibles tendencias evolutivas.

23223262|The genus Marattia Sw., belonging to the primitive fern family Marattiaceae, was found for the first time in Argentina, in the northeastern part of the Province of Misiones. The specimen, and similar collections from adjacent states in Brazil, were identified as Marattia laevis Sm. However, these specimens exhibit some morphological differences, especially in the synangia, from collections of this species elsewhere in tropical America.

23210031|This work includes a revision of Cyttaria and Cyttariella species of Argentina. The existence of five species of Cyttaria is determined: C. Darwini, C. Harioti, C. Espinosae, C. Hookeri and C. intermedia, and two species of Cyttariella: C. deformans and C. Skottsbergii. C. Espinosae is verified for the first time, and the existence of C. Berteroi is discarded. Of C. Hookeri three new forms are described: C. Hookeri f. typica, C. Hookeri f. moroidea and C. Hookeri f. candida, which live, respectively, on Nothofagus antarctica, N. Dombeyi and N. betuloides. The form cited in the last term has similarity to C. intermedia. A description of all the species and their geographical distribution and pathological manifestations on the parasited hosts, is given.

23222989|The detailed study of the nomenclature types and of abundant collections has revealed that N. linariaefolia R. Graham and N. pulchella Miers have been misunderstood until now. Twenty five names ( 12 at specific level and 13 at varietal level), which we assign to these species, have been considered valid until now. Four varieties can be distinguished in the first species (var. linariaefolia, var. glabriuscula, var. pampeana, and var. pinifolioides) and three in the second one (var. pulchella, var. longistyla, and var. macrocalyx). Their numerous synonyms are critically evaluated, together with an appreciation of their distribution; the article ends with a key to recognize both species and their varieties.

Comparative data on its related species, S. herzogii, are given.
23215058|In this paper the authors treat two vicarious species of Leguminosae and conclude : 1) that Hosackia Dougl. ex Benth. is correctly merged into Lotus L. as a section, according to Ottley, Callen and others; 2) that Lotus subpinnatus Lag., from Chile, and L. wrangelianus Fisch. et Mey. from California, are independent species, whose differences and synonyms are given; 3) The pollen grains of both were studied and found to be very similar; both are tetra-colparate, in marked contrast with other Lotusspecies and Papilionoideae in general, which have tri-colporate pollen grains.
23225164|A new species, Vernonia lanifera, from northeastern Argentina and southern Brazil is described and illustrated. It is a xilopodiferous plant found growing in high stony ground. The leaves show a thick woolly layer on the lower surface; young stems and involucral bracts are also lanate. It resembles V. rubricaulis which is characterized by sericeous indument with short, shining, pressed hairs, numerous lateral thick roots, and grows on low and humid lands. Una nueva especie, Vernonia lanifera, del Nordeste de Argentina y Sur de Brasil es descripta e ilustrada. Es una planta xilopodfera que vive en campos altos, pedregosos. Las hojas poseen una gruesa capa lanosa en el envs, los tallos jvenes y los filarios son tambin lanosos. Se asemeja a V. rubricaulis, la cual se diferencia por el indumento serceo, o sea con pelos cortos, brillantes, acroscpicos, por tener numerosas races laterales engrosadas y por crecer en lugares bajos y hmedos.
23223188|The anatomy of the nomophylls of Mulinum microphyllum (Cav.) Pers., M. hallei Skottsb., M. valentinii Speg., M. echinus D. C. and M. leptacanthum Philippi has been studied. The five species share the following anatomical characters: amphistomatic leaves, one-layered epidermis, hypodermis, homogeneous mesophyll composed of palisade parenchyma, segments of the blade with sclerenchymatous strands in the central vein, vascular bundles accompanied by secretory canals, abaxial collenchyma strands under the main secretory canals, epidermis and mesophyll rich in crystals of calcium oxalate. M. microphyllum and M. hallei differ from the other species by the following features: stomata frequently anisocytic, abaxial hypodermis, a midvein with a sheath interrupted by a sclerenchyma strand wich extends up to the adaxial epidermis. These two species show distinctive epidermal characteristics: papillae and other trichomes are only present in M. microphyllum. The other three species exhibit prevalence of anomocytic stomata, adaxial and abaxial hypodermis, midveins with a distinct sheath and a sclerenchyma strand within the sheath limit. M. echinus and M. valentinii have peristomatal rims, very compact mesophyll, few chloroplasts in hypodermal cells. However, both species differ from one another in epidermal features: papillae are only present in M. echinus; M. valentinii has adaxial epidermal outer cell walls thicker than the abaxial ones. On the other hand, in M. leptacanthum hypodermal cells are full of chloroplasts and epidermis without peristomatal rims. The following xeromorphic characteristics have been detected in the five studied species: thick outer and inner periclinal walls of the epidermal cells, distinct outer stomatal rims, compact mesophyll with high developed palisade chlorenchyma, veins with sclerenchymatic supports. A dichotomic key based on foliar anatomy, to distinguish the studied species, is provided.
23213892|Seven species of Cyttaria are treated here, parasiting Nothofagus sps. in southern South America along the Andes, from 30 S. L. to 56 S. L. A short account on method of study is given and an annotated terminology. Two keys are presented: one for determining species  in situ , attending mainly to their hosts, phenological data and macroscopical features, and another one according to characteristics of mature and spermogonial stromata. The species are described attending to their external and microscopical features, and the development of stromata is described in six species. Phenological data and geographical distribution for each species is given, the last one based only on revised material. The author emphasizes microscopical characters of the stromata and finds inoperculate asci with an amyloid cylinder (or ring) and apical paraphyses in the species studied. Based on these peculiar features she recommends the inclusion of the Cyttareaceae in the Order Cyttariales belonging to the Discomycetes, which is somewhat intermediate between Helotiales and Sphaeriales. A new species is described: Cyttaria exigua on Nothofagus dombeyi.

23223007|The study of pollen grains of Saxegothaea conspicua Lindl. by phase constrast and scanning electron microscopy allowed to observe characteristics not previously pointed out by other authors. Basically the pollen of Saxegothaea conspicua is subisopolar, subspheroidal, 3-4-analept with a relictual trilete mark. The taxonomic position of Saxegothaea is briefly discussed exposing the ideas of different authors, pointing out also the rather isolated position of the genus within the Podocarpaceae. It is concluded that more comparative studies are required, using new techniques that would help defining with more exact data the position of the genus within the conifers.

23222529|Chromosome studies in Barnadesiinae (Mutisieae, Asteraceae). I. Chuquiraga y Doniophyton. All these species are cited for the first time for those localities, thus enlarging their distribution area, as many of them had only been mentioned for the Tierra del Fuego or Islas Malvinas. Ceramium rubrum (Huds.) C. A. Ag. var. barbatum (Ktz.) J. G. Ag. and Ceramium rubrum (Huds.) C. A. Ag. var. pedicellatum J. G. Ag. are cited for the first time for Argentina. Vertical zonation within the Litoral System is indicated for each species. It shows a marked preference for the Mesolitoral floor (middle and inferior horizon), in and outside the tidepools, and the Infralitoral floor (hig horizon). Their form of life is also indicated, which is rupicolous, epizoic of epiphitic. The mayority of species of Ceramium, Callithamnium, Antithamnion and Antithamnionella have been found to be epiphitic, while Griffithsia, Ballia and Dasyptilon are rupicolous. Observations on their presence made during several years, show that these Algae are abundant throughout the year.

41825700|The Andropogon lateralis complex is constituted by 13 taxonomic entities: seven species and six class inter-specific hybrids distributed in Central and South America. Natural hybrids within this group are quite common due to lack of inter-specific barriers. These hybrids have been collected in the last two centuries and, in most cases, have caught the attention of taxonomists, who formally described several as new taxa. Therefore, taxonomic entities based on them have been validly published. In southern South America, among the ten taxonomic entities in the A. lateralis complex, five are natural hybrids and at least three possess legitimate names (A.  coloratus, A.  lindmanii, and A.  subtilior). Based on morphometric analyses and previous studies we propose that other two natural hybrids deserve taxonomic names. These entities are Andropogon  velutinus (A. bicornis  A. glaziovii, = Andropogon sp 1 according to Zanin, 2001) and Andropogon  catarinensis (A. bicornis  A. arenarius). Taxonomic treatments of A.  velutinus and A.  catarinensis are presented. El complejo Andropogon lateralis est constituido por alrededor de 13 entidades taxonmicas: siete especies y seis hbridos inter-especficos distribuidos en Centro y Sudamrica. Los hbridos naturales en este grupo son frecuentes debido a la ausencia de barreras reproductivas entre las especies. Estos hbridos han sido recolectados en los ltimos dos siglos y, en la mayora de los casos, han llamado la atencin de los taxnomos, quienes han descrito a varias de estas combinaciones formalmente como nuevos taxones. Por lo tanto, las entidades taxonmicas basadas en combinaciones hbridas han sido vlidamente publicadas. De las diez entidades taxonmicas que integran el complejo A. lateralis en el Cono Sur de Sudamrica, cinco corresponden a hbridos naturales y tres de estos poseen nombres legtimos (A.  coloratus, A.  lindmanii y A.  subtilior). Sobre la base de anlisis morfomtricos y estudios previos, proponemos que los dos hbridos naturales restantes tambin merecen nombres taxonmicamente vlidos. Estas entidades son Andropogon  velutinus (A. bicornis  A. glaziovii, = Andropogon sp 1 de acuerdo a Zanin, 2001) y Andropogon  catarinensis (A. bicornis  A. arenarius). En este trabajo se presentan los tratamientos taxonmicos de Andropogon  velutinus y Andropogon  catarinensis.

23223907|This study includes an analysis of the species of Poaceae recovered in an archaeological site in the Argentine Southern Puna, province of Catamarca: Quebrada Seca 3. The investigation was carried about the use of Deyeuxia eminens J. Presl by groups of hunter-gatherers during the Archaic period ca. 10000-3000 years BP (8000-1000 years BC). The starting point for the study of the archaeobotanical record was the recording of the present flora and the ethnobotanical information obtained in the area. The comparative taxonomic and anatomic analysis of the actual and the archaeological plants allowed the identification of the latter. The results indicate the abundance of Deyeuxia eminens in the archaeobotanical record of the site. As a result, the areas from which the species comes, its probable use and a certain seasonal occupation of the site were inferred. Se realiz el estudio de las especies de la familia Poaceae recuperadas en un sitio arqueolgico de la Puna Meridional Argentina, provincia de Catamarca: Quebrada Seca 3. El punto de partida para el estudio del registro arqueobotnico fue el relevamiento de la flora actual del rea de estudio y la informacin etnobotnica recogida en la misma. A partir del anlisis taxonmico y anatmico comparativo de los vegetales actuales y arqueolgicos se identificaron los ltimos. Los resultados indican la abundancia de Deyeuxia eminens en el registro arqueobotnico del sitio. Sobre esta base, se infieren las reas de procedencia, el probable uso de esta especie y cierta estacionalidad en la ocupacin del sitio.
23226709|The micromorphological features of the lemma were investigated in Trisetum and related genera in Pooideae (Poaceae) using scanning electron microscopy to evaluate the circumscription of the genus Trisetum and its systematic relationships. Seventy six species were studied including 32 species of Trisetum and selected species of Amphibromus (1 sp.), Avena (2 spp.), Avenula (6 spp.), Deschampsia (6 spp.), Dielsiochloa (1 sp.), Graphephorum (2 spp.), Gymnachne (1 sp.), Helictotrichon (8 spp.), Koeleria (5 spp.), Leptophyllochloa (1 sp.), Peyritschia (4 spp.), Raimundochloa (1 sp.), Relchela (1 sp.), Rhombolytrum (1 sp.), Rostraria (1 sp.) and Sphenopholis (3 spp.). The results showed that the epidermis of the lemma varies very little within the studied genera, thus it is a good character for the generic circumscription and to study the generic relationships in Pooideae. Trisetum is characterized by rectangular long cells, silica cells usually present, stomata absent, and hooks and prickle hairs present. Differences in the presence of silica cells, prickle hairs and various other epidermal features showed that Peyritschia is distinct from Trisetum. Species of Peyritschia generally lack silica cells, macrohairs and prickle hairs. Silica cells and prickle hairs are usually present in Trisetum and some species have macrohairs covering the lemma. Species examined of Sphenopholis have epidermal cells shorter than species of Trisetum and some species of Sphenopholis have stomata in the apical portion of the lemma. The results suggest that Sphenopholis interrupta (= Trisetum interruptum) should be excluded from Trisetum and classified in the genus Sphenopholis. Deschampsia is very distinct from Trisetum in the epidermal characteristics of the lemma. Studied species of Deschampsia have very long epidermal cells, absence of silica cells, prickle hairs and hooks usually absent, and long cells with straight anticlinal walls. The genera Amphibromus, Avena, Avenula, Helictotrichon, Gymnachne, Rhombolytrum, Dielsiochloa, Leptophyllochloa, and Raimundochloa showed various combinations of micromorphological features supporting their generic distinction among them and from Trisetum. On the other hand, Graphephorum, Rostraria and Koeleria are very similar to Trisetum in the epidermal characters of the lemma. Las caractersticas micromorfolgicas de la lemma de Trisetum y gneros relacionados de Pooideae (Poaceae) fueron investigadas utilizando microscopia electrnica de barrido, con el objeto de evaluar la circunscripcin del gnero Trisetum y sus relaciones sistemticas. Se estudiaron 76 especies, incluyendo 32 especies de Trisetum y especies seleccionadas de Amphibromus (1 sp.), Avena (2 spp.), Avenula (6 spp.), Deschampsia (6 spp.), Dielsiochloa (1 sp.), Graphephorum (2 spp.), Gymnachne (1 sp.), Helictotrichon (8 spp.), Koeleria (5 spp.), Leptophyllochloa (1 sp.), Peyritschia (4 spp.), Raimundochloa (1 sp.), Relchela (1 sp.), Rhombolytrum (1 sp.), Rostraria (1 sp.) y Sphenopholis (3 spp.). Los resultados muestran que la epidermis de la lemma vara muy poco en las especies de cada gnero pero es diferente en los distintos gneros estudiados y, por tanto, es un buen carcter para estudiar la circunscripcin de los gneros as como las relaciones sistemticas en Pooideae. Trisetum se caracteriza por poseer clulas largas rectangulares, clulas silceas usualmente presentes, estomas ausentes y ganchos y aguijones presentes. Diferencias en la presencia de clulas silceas, aguijones y varias otras caractersticas demuestran que Peyritschia es distinto de Trisetum. Las especies de Peyritschia generalmente carecen de clulas silceas, macropelos y aguijones. Clulas silceas y aguijones estn usualmente presentes en Trisetum y algunas especies poseen macropelos que cubren la lemma. Las especies examinadas de Sphenopholis tienen clulas epidrmicas ms cortas que las especies de Trisetum y algunas especies de Sphenopholis tienen estomas en la porcin apical de la lemma. Los resultados sugieren que Sphenopholis interrupta (=Trisetum interruptum) debe ser excluido de Trisetum y clasificado en el gnero Sphenopholis. Deschampsia es muy diferente de Trisetum en cuanto a las caractersticas epidrmicas de la lemma. Las especies estudiadas de Deschampsia tienen clulas epidrmicas muy largas, ausencia de clulas silceas y usualmente carecen de aguijones y ganchos y poseen clulas largas con paredes anticlinales rectas. Los gneros Amphibromus, Avena, Avenula, Helictotrichon, Gymnachne, Rhombolytrum, Dielsiochloa, Leptophyllochloa y Raimundochloa muestras diversas combinaciones de caractersticas micromorfolgicas que avalan su delimitacin recproca y de Trisetum. Por otra parte, Graphephorum, Rostraria y Koeleria son muy similares a Trisetum en las caractersticas epidrmicas de la lemma.

23228355|The traditional botanical knowledge (TBK) is defined as a cumulative "corpus" of knowledge, practices and beliefs about the relationships between the human beings and the vegetal components of their environments. This "corpus" of knowledge is modified by selection processes and is transmitted culturally from generation to generation. In this approach it is demonstrated that the temporary variable occupies an outstanding roll in the conformation of the TBK. Nevertheless, considering it as the knowledge shared by a specific human group about local vegetables, it is clear that the knowledge involved in the process of choice, obtaining, processing and consumption, as well as in the local administration, of plant resources, also can be generated by and residing in communities that lack of historical and cultural continuity. From the analysis of two cases (the horticulture in the Puna of Jujuy, NW of Argentina, and suburban areas in Buenos Aires province) where the temporary depth from the experience is different, TBK can be consider a synthesis of wisdom, that is generated so much from the knowledge generated locally by practice and experimentation, as well as by incorporation of information of other sources, including the scientific knowledge. Finally, we extend this analysis to the interpretation of local practices of plant manipulation in archaeology, which reflects CBT in the past. El conocimiento botnico tradicional (CBT) es definido como un cuerpo acumulativo de conocimientos, prcticas y creencias acerca de las relaciones entre los seres humanos y los componentes vegetales de su entorno. Este cuerpo de conocimientos se modifica a partir de procesos de seleccin y es transmitido culturalmente de generacin en generacin. En esta clase de abordaje queda evidenciado que la variable temporal ocupa un rol destacado en la conformacin del CBT. Sin embargo, considerndolo como el saber compartido por un grupo humano especfico acerca de los vegetales locales, se reconoce que ese conocimiento, empleado durante el proceso de eleccin, obtencin, procesamiento y consumo, as como en la administracin local de los recursos, puede ser tambin engendrado por y residir en comunidades que carecen de continuidad histrica y cultural. A partir del anlisis de dos casos (la horticultura en la puna jujefia y en reas suburbanas bonaerenses) donde difiere la profundidad temporal de la experiencia, se concluye que el CBT puede considerarse una sntesis de saberes, que se genera tanto a partir del conocimiento engendrado localmente por prctica y experimentacin, as como por incorporacin de informacin de otras fuentes, incluyendo el conocimiento cientfico. Finalmente se proyecta este anlisis a la identificacin arqueolgica de prcticas locales de manejo de poblaciones vegetales, reflejo del CBT en el pasado.
23216521|This work deals with the inflorescences of the argentine species of Sisyrinchium. All of them are complicated tirsoid inflorescences formed by monopodic and simpodic axes. Each axis of monopodic growth, including the principal one is terminated by a flower preceded by two bracts. The apical bract is always fertile, a lateral axis of simpodial growth which constitutes an helicoidal monocasium is developed in its axil. On the contrary the basal bract is always sterile. According to the different development and complexity of these components, differents types of inflorescence have been established provisionally. These types have been individually analized, the modifications found in the studied material were considered in each case. The possible relationships and derivations between them are also discussed here.
23222519|Karyological studies in South American grasses. Chromosome numbers are reported for 82 accessions of grasses representing 11 genera and 41 specific or underspecific taxa. The results contribute to the general evaluation of native forage grasses, specially of the genus Paspalum, collected through Argentina, Brazil, Paraguay and Uruguay.

23230183|This paper proposes the observation of anatomical features associated with water deficiency in wood as paleoenvironmental indicator. The analysis was applied to charcoal recovered in late archaeological contexts of Aguada in Ambato Valley, Catamarca (Argentina). Based on the correlation between the anatomical structure of wood and the habitat, the observations were done on present-day and archaeological samples of Geoffroea decorticans. Results show arid conditions in the study area at the end of the first millennium. El presente trabajo propone la observacin de rasgos anatmicos ligados a deficiencia hdrica en leosas como indicador paleoambiental. El anlisis fue aplicado a carbn vegetal arqueolgico recuperado en contextos finales de la ocupacin Aguada del Valle de Ambato, Catamarca (Argentina). Sobre la base de la correlacin entre la estructura anatmica de la madera y el tipo de hbitat, se realizaron observaciones en muestras actuales y arqueolgicas de Geoffroea decorticans. Los resultados indican que condiciones ms secas que las actuales debieron operar en el rea de estudio a fines del Primer milenio de la era.

23227136|Cyrtopodium kleinii and C. brandonianum subsp. lageanum (Cyrtopodiinae, Cymbidieae, Orchidaceae) from southern Brazil are described and illustrated. Cyrtopodium kleinii is similar to a group of terrestrial species characterized by their small pseudobulbs, buried underground, and small flowers, but it can be distinguished by the color of its flowers, lip lateral lobes slightly or not falcate and subequal in length and width, lip midlobe base with little or no constriction, and geographical distribution. Cyrtopodium brandonianum subsp. lageanum is similar in general flower color to typical C. brandonianum, but it can be distinguished by its earlier flowering, leaves poorly developed at anthesis and different shape and colour of the lip. Both taxa are rare and only known from southern Brazil. C. brandoniamum subsp. lageanum es similar a la variedad tipo en cuanto al patrn general de coloracin, pero se distingue por florecer ms tempranamente, por las hojas poco desarrolladas en la antesis, y por la forma y coloracin del labelo. 23211734|Esta comunicacin describe las dos comunidades ms importantes del Valle de Santa Mara: el Bosque de Algarrobo (Asociacin de Prosopis alba, P. nigra y Acacia visco) y la Estepa de Jarilla (Asociacin de Larrea cuneifolia, Bulnesia Schickendantzii y Plectrocarpa Rougesii). Se atribuye especial importancia a los puntos siguientes: a) La estratificacin de las races en cada comunidad, vinculada a las exigencias ecolgicas de cada capa. b) Existen grandes diferencias entre los sistemas subterrneos de los arbustos de la Estepa de Jarilla: Zuccagnia punctata y Larrea divaricata que vegetan en las mrgenes de los ros temporarios. c) Los cambios climticos y la actividad humana han favorecido el ulterior desarrollo de la Estepa de Jarilla que actualmente ocupa zonas antes dominadas por el Bosque de Algarrobo. d) El hombre ha cambiado la estructura de los Bosques de Algarrobo, hacindose difcil interpretar las causas de la ausencia de Acacia visco en los Bosques del fondo del valle. This paper describes the two most important communities of the Santa Maria Valley: the Algarrobo Forest (Association of Prosopis alba, P. nigra and Acacia visco) and the Jarilla Steppe (Association of Larrea cuneifolia, Bulnesia Schickendantzii and Plectrocarpa Rougesii). Special importance is assigned to the following facts: a) The subterranean root-layer in each community, related to the ecological demands of each layer. b) There are wide differences between the underground system of shrubs in the Jarilla Steppe, and the Zuccagnia punctata and Larrea divaricata which thrive on the banks of the temporary rivers. c) Both climatic changes and human activites have aided the later development of the Jarilla Steppe which nowadays covers zones that had been formerly dominated by the Algarrobo Forest. d) Man has changed the structure of the Algarrobo Forest making it very difficult to determine the causes of the absency of the Acacia visco in the depth of the valley. Den nachfolgenden Umstnden wird eine besondere Wichtigkeit beigemessen: a) Die Wurzel-Stratifikation jeder einzelnen Pflanzengesellschaft, bedingt durch die kologischen Anforderungen jeder Schicht. b) Es bestehen grosse Unterschiede zwischen den Wurzelsystemen der Bsche der Jarilla-Steppe und denen der Zuccagnia punctata und Larrea divaricata welch letztere Bsche an den Uferrndern der Regenflsse wachsen. c) Wechsel im Klima und menschliche Bettigung haben die Bildung der Jarilla-Steppe begnstigt und diese beherrscht jetzt Gebiete, die vorher von Algarrobo-Wldern bestanden waren. d) Menschliches Einwirken hat die Struktur des Algarrobo-Waldes gendert, wobei es schwierig ist, das Fehlen von Acacia visco in den Wldern des Talbodens zu erklren.

23222558|The floral syndrome of Caesalpinia gilliesii (Wall. ex Hook.) Dietr. (Fabaceae) was studied, including pollinator behaviour, nectary structure, pollen features, nectar-chemical composition and nectar secretion physiology. Members of Caesalpinieae exhibiting other floral syndromes were studied in order to compare the results: melittophily (Caesalpinia angulata (Hook. & Arn.) Baillon, C. coluteifolia Griseb., C. exilifolia Griseb., C. paraguariensis (Parodi) Burkart, Balsamocarpon brevifolium Clos, Cercidium praecox (R. et P.) Harms, Hoffmannseggia glauca (Ort.) Eifert, Parkinsonia aculeata L., Zuccagnia punctata Cav.) and psychophily (C. pulcherrima (L.) SW.). Caesalpinia gilliesii shows floral characters which reflect its adaptation to nocturnal pollination: cream-colored petals, red stamens (apparently invisible at night), nectary development, evening anthesis, pattern of nectar secretion. Three sphingid moths species were observed to be legitimate pollinators. In C. gilliesii nectar removal affects the total sugar amount produced by each flower depending on the time of the removal: it decreases before 21:00 and it increases after that time. The studied species had "hexose rich" or "hexose dominant" nectars. Caesalpinia gilliesii and C. pulcherrima have convergent morphological floral aspects related to pterotriby. Moth and butterfly pollination are considered here to be derived from melittophily, which is the more extensively developed syndrome in the nearest relatives. Sphingophily is cited for the first time in the tribe and could be considered a manifestation of the intrageneric evolutionary radiation that probably took place after the cleavage of Gondwania and also produced psychophily, melittophily and ornithophily. More than one such radiation may have occurred independently within the Caesalpinia group.

23218119|Terminal dilated tracheids in the veinlets of some species of Atriplex (Chenopodiaceae). Specialized terminal veinlet elements are studied in 12 argentine species of Atriplex. These are dilated, bordered pitted tracheids with thick walls and of variable shape; oblong, more or less isodiametric, or irregular with short and acute processes; they occur as conspicuous massive cells of larger size than the other tracheary elements of the leaf. The morphological relationship of these cells with other kind of veinlet endings reported for several genera of dicots as tracheoidal idioblasts, spiral tracheids, sclerenchymatous idioblasts, etc. is discussed. The occurrence of intermediate, confusing "hybrid" types among them as well as the poorly understood role of these elements are also pointed out. The differences between these elements and cells not associated with the vascular system, observed by several authors in other genera of Chenopodiaceae, are also given.

23230233|The species in the Sporobolus indicus complex are analyzed for Argentina. Sporobolus indicus var. indicus and S. indicus var. andinus are recognized for Argentina based on significant value differences in culms height and inflorescence length, and the altitude of collection area. The var. andinus is a new record for the Argentinean flora and it is here illustrated. Sporobolus jacquemontii is excluded from Argentina and S. minor is considered as a synonymy of S. indicus var. indicus. Se analiza el complejo de especies relacionadas a Sporobolus indicus para la Argentina. Se reconocen las variedades S. indicus var. indicus y S. indicus var. andinus para la Argentina, sobre la base de diferencias significativas en la altura de las plantas, el largo de las inflorescencias y la altitud de los sitios de colecta. La variedad andinus representa una nueva cita para la flora argentina y se ilustra por primera vez. Se excluye a S. jacquemontii para la Argentina y se considera a S. minor como sinnimo de S. indicus var. indicus.

23222988|An account is given of the spore germination and young gametophytes of two species of Blechnum L. and one hybrid: B. australe subsp. auriculatum (Cav.) de la Sota; B. laevigatum Cav. and B. australe subsp. auriculatum x B. laevigatum. 23226714|Lichens can affect buildings and monuments inducing a negative aesthetical impact as well as causing deterioration through mechanical and chemical processes. Given that cement mortars and concrete are the primary 20th century building materials worldwide, it is important to study lichens growing on this substrate. In a survey of different localities of Buenos Aires Province, 33 species growing on mortars and concrete were collected and identified utilizing morphological and chemical studies. Results showed that Staurothele frustulenta is a new record for Argentina, and Acarospora subcastanea is a new record for Buenos Aires Province. A high number of foliose lichens (15 species) were registered. Some species were previously only known on tree barks, but in this study they were encountered colonizing cement materials as well. Los lquenes pueden afectar edificios y monumentos causando un impacto esttico negativo, como tambin ocasionar deterioro por procesos mecnicos y qumicos. Puesto que los morteros de cemento y hormigones han sido el material de construccin ms utilizado en el mundo durante el siglo XX, es importante estudiar los lquenes que crecen sobre estos sustratos. En un estudio realizado en diferentes localidades de la Provincia de Buenos Aires, se hallaron 33 especies creciendo sobre morteros y hormigones, identificadas por medio de estudios morfolgicos y qumicos. Staurothele frustulenta es nueva para el pas y Acarospora subcastanea es nueva para la Provincia. Se registr una alta proporcin de lquenes foliosos (15 especies en total). Algunas de estas especies slo se conocidas sobre cortezas de rboles, fueron encontradas colonizando materiales de cemento.

23612321|Munroa is a morphologically heterogeneous American genus of grasses, including five species with disjunct distribution in North and South America. Dasyochloa is a monotypic grass genus, common in western North America, with a controversial taxonomic position, because it has been alternatively included in Erioneuron, Koeleria, Triodia, and Uralepis. We evaluated the relationship of Dasyochloa with Munroa using a phylogenetic analysis of qualitative and quantitative morphological data. Dasyochloa was not supported as an independent genus from Munroa, as Dasyochloa and Munroa species formed a monophyletic group defined by seven synapomorphies. On this basis, we transfer Dasyochloa to Munroa, and propose the new combination M. pulchella together with the emended diagnosis of Munroa. Munroa es un gnero Americano morfolgicamente heterogneo, con cinco especies y distribucin disyunta en Amrica del Norte y del Sur. Dasyochloa es un gnero monotpico, comn en el oeste de Norteamrica, con una historia taxonmica compleja porque ha sido incluido alternativamente en Erioneuron, Koeleria, Triodia y Uralepis. En este trabajo evaluamos las relaciones de Dasyochloa y Munroa con base en un anlisis filogentico con caracteres morfolgicos cualitativos y cuantitativos. Dasyochloa no result independiente de Munroa, ya que ambos gneros formaron un grupo monofiltico definido por siete sinapomorfas. Sobre esta base, transferimos Dasyochloa a Munroa y proponemos la nueva combinacin M. pulchella, junto con una enmienda en la diagnosis de Munroa.

23218075|The seed proteins of Bulnesia chilensis (Chile) and B. retama (Per, Argentina) were studied by polyacrylamide electrophoresis and compared with the other six species of the genus. In total 90 different bands were identified. These were treated numerically by cluster analysis by the unweighted pair - group method (UPGMA). The two main groups that can be distinguished on the basis of the protein patterns, each composed of 4 species (fig. 2) constitute the two subgenera recognized in a new taxonomic revision. (Palacios and Hunziker, 1984). Several species pairs composed of phenetically similar taxa are clearly seen in the phenogram (fig. 2). These are: B. arborea - B. carrapo, B. schickendantzii B. foliosa and B. retama - B. chilensis. The species pair B. foliosa - B. schickendantzii present the most similar protein patterns and thus show the shortest taxonomic distance in the phenogram. On the other hand, the isolated populations of B. retama from Per and Argentina, which show some protein band differences, exhibit greater taxonomic distances than the previously mentioned species pair. Within the subgenus Gonopterodendron, B. bonariensis, which is the only polyploid species and B. sarmientoi, which morphologically shows several reductions (carpel and leaflet numbers, etc.) appear as the most distant species. The electrophoretic results are congruent with a previous numerical analysis of exomorphological characteristics (Crisci et al., 1979) and with the recent taxonomic subdivision of the genus (Palacios and Hunziker, 1984) thus showing once more the reliability of protein electrophoresis as a method for the study of species relationships.
41825711|Sustainable forest management requires appropriate mapping information. In this work we developed a mapping of the current vegetation of Bioko island (Equatorial Guinea) based on supervised classification of a Landsat 7 ETM +, and a mapping of Afromontane forests, including data distribution, surface and forest types where Prunus africana occurs. We propose six new types of transitional vegetation between Guinean-Congolese forest and Afromontane forests and different secondary Afromontane formations. The vegetation map of Bioko had a Kappa coefficient of 0.69. Difficulties were encountered in separating secondary lowland forest classes from transition zones between Guineo-Congolian and Afromontane forests. Accuracy was highly improved when a second classification was restricted to the island's Afromontane vegetation (> 1400 m a.s.l.), yielding a Kappa coefficient of 0.81. Our results have appropiate accuracy for forest management demonstrating that remote sensing is a useful source for mapping development, especially in tropical areas with difficult access. La gestin forestal sostenible requiere de una informacin cartogrfica adecuada. En este trabajo se elabor una cartografa actual de la vegetacin de la isla de Bioko (Guinea Ecuatorial) basada en la clasificacin supervisada de una imagen Landsat 7 ETM+, y una cartografa de la vegetacin del piso afromontano, que incluye datos de la distribucin, la superficie y los tipos forestales con presencia de Prunus africana. Se proponen seis nuevos tipos de vegetacin de transicin entre los bosques Guineo-Congolesa y los bosques afromontanos, y distintas formaciones afromontanas secundarias. El mapa de vegetacin de Bioko tuvo un coeficiente Kappa de 0,69. Los principales errores se asociaron a las clases correspondientes a bosque secundarios de tierras bajas y a las zonas de transicin entre los bosques congoleses y afromontanos. La fiabilidad del anlisis mejor en una segunda clasificacin restringida a la vegetacin afromontana de la isla (> 1400 m s. m.), obtenindose un coeficiente Kappa de 0,81. En este trabajo se muestra la utilidad de la teledeteccin para la elaboracin de cartografa en zonas tropicales de escasa accesibilidad, dado que se obtuvieron resultados con una fiabilidad adecuada para la gestin forestal.

23215738|Se han estudiado los elementos traqueales no perforados de algunas especies de Mirtceas argentinas, plantendose el problema de su clasificacin dada la diversidad de los mismos. Siguiendo el criterio aconsejado por el Comit de Nomenclatura de la Asociacin Internacional de Anatomistas de Maderas, que se basa en la naturaleza de las punteaduras, algunos de los elementos observados en Myrceugenella apiculata, Myrceugenia chrysocarpa, Amomyrtus luma, Blepharocalyx gigantea y B. tweediei deben clasificarse como traqueidas. Estas son semejantes a las citadas para gneros y/o familias poco evolucionadas de las dicotiledneas y para ciertas Coniferales y Gnetales. La presencia de este carcter anatmico primitivo no haba sido citado hasta el presente para las Mirtceas y reviste inters desde el punto de vista filogentico. Existen otros elementos con punteaduras de areola reducida que se clasifican como fibro-traqueidas y finalmente en otros casos el borde est ausente, tratndose por lo tanto de fibras liberiformes, con punteaduras simples. En algunas especies se observa toda la transicin entre estos elementos, siendo necesario un cuidadoso estudio comparativo de la clase de punteaduras visibles para establecer una clasificacin, ya que la presencia o ausencia de borde es el carcter ms seguro para tener en cuenta. La autora analiza en la primer parte del trabajo, los criterios recomendados por los anatomistas de maderas que definieron a los elementos traqueales no perforados de las Gimnospermas y Angiospermas en las sucesivas ediciones del Glosario de trminos como asimismo los problemas originados en su clasificacin. This paper deals with the imperforate tracheary elements of some species of argentine Myrtaceae. On account of these elements exhibit a great diversity, the problem of its classification it was stated. If the definitions and recommendations of the Committee on Nomenclature of the International Association of Wood Anatomists are to be adopted-based largely on the nature of the pitting-some of these elements must be classified as tracheids, as it were observed in Myrceugenella apiculata, Myrceugenia chrysocarpa, Amomyrtus luma, Blepharocalyx gigantea and B. tweediei. These tracheids are very similar to those of various representantives of the Gnetales, Coniferales and many families or genera of dicotyledons, considered as primitive. The presence of tracheids in the Myrtaceae is recorded for the first time here and obviously this character is important from the phylogenetic point of view. Other imperforate tracheary elements with pits of reduced borders were classified as fibretracheids, being libriform fibres when the border is absent. Some species exhibit a graded series of transitional forms among the 3 types of imperforate elements, whereas a careful comparative study of the pitting was carried out in order to classify them properly. The definitions recommended by that Committee of Wood Anatomists and the problems originated about the classification of the imperforate tracheary elements of the dicotyledons were analized by the author in the first part of the paper.

23212991|Tropaeolum majus se halla parasitado en La Plata y otras partes del mundo por un Hifomicete referido hasta hoy a Heterosporium tropaeoli Bond. Los estudios realizados han permitido establecer que el hongo en cuestin pertenece a un gnero nuevo para el cual se propone el nombre de Acroconidiella, fundndose en consecuencia la combinacin Acroconidiella tropaeoli (Bond) nov. comb. Este gnero se caracteriza porque sus esporas se forman en el pice de los conidiforos emergiendo de los mismos a travs de un poro. Estos conidios son cilindrceos o elipsideos con 0-3 tabiques (en su mayora 2). Este gnero es vecino de Alternaria y Curvularia; del primero difiere porque las esporas no son muriformes ni estn encadenadas y del segundo porque sus esporas son rectas y sus clulas de igual dimensin y tonalidad uniforme. Se trata de un hongo patgeno que provoca sntomas necrticos en las hojas, cuya virulencia se ha comprobado experimentalmente. Tropaeolum majus is parasitized in La Plata, as in other parts of the world, by a Hyphomycete heretofore known as Heterosporium tropaeoli Bond. From the results of the studies conducted by the authors it is concluded that this fungus belongs to a new genus, for which the name Acroconidiella and the combination Acroconidiella tropaeoli (Bond) nov. comb., are proposed. This genus is characterized by its spores which are formed on the apex of the conidiophores, emerging through a pore. These conidia are cylindrical or ellipsoideal, with 0-3 septae (mainly 2). This genus is closely related to Alternaria and Curvularia. From the former it differs by its spores not being muriform nor chained; from the latter it differs because its spores are straight and its cells are of uniform size and color. This fungus is a pathogen which produces necrotic symptoms on the leaves. Its virulence has been demonstrated by experimental research work.
23222535|A disjunct species in Eleocharis (Cyperaceae). The study of the type specimens of Eleocharis cylindrica Buckley, described from Texas, Estados Unidos and E. spegazzinii Barros from Argentina and Paraguay, together with the peculiar characteristic that both possess an intermediate anatomy between non Kranz and Kranz-Fimbristyloid types, let us to establish that they belong to the same species with a disjunct area. The valid name by priority is E. cylindrica; it belongs to series Palustriformis, subseries Truncatae. A key to distinguish it from E. tricostata Torrey, E. parishii Britton and E. dombeyana Kunth, closely related species, is given.

23218918|Ruellia sanguinea (Acanthaceae) and allied species in Argentina, Uruguay and southern Brazil. In this area, species allied to Ruellia sanguinea Griseb. are characterized by their narrow red corollas with small semierect lobes which suggest hummingbird pollination, their few-seeded clavate capsules, and their glabrous seeds with hairy margins. Ruellia longipedunculata Lindau, known for Bolivia, is now reported for Argentina. The area of Ruellia angustiflora (Nees) Lindau ex Rambo is expanded to southern Brazil, SE Paraguay, NE Argentina and northern Uruguay, and R. sanguinea, having been erroneously confused with that species, is excluded from that area, thriving instead in southern Bolivia and NW Argentina.

23227936|The South American flora includes 65 genera of Caesalpinioideae (Leguminosae) with wide morphological variation. The four tribes of that subafmily are represented: 31 genera belong to the Caesalpinieae (3 of them introduced); 9 to the Cassieae; 2 to Cercideae (1 introduced), and 23 to Detarieae (2 introduced). Among the South American Caesalpinoideae, 30 genera are endemic (mainly to Brazil), the remaining ones inhabit in tropical and subtropical areas from both hemispheres. All of them grow in diverse habitats: from rainforests, evergreen or deciduous forests, to savannas, semi-deserts and high mountains. Tribes and genera are arranged according to Polhill & Raven (1981), only Poepiggia has been transferred from Caesalpinieae to Cassieae, and Ceratonia from Cassieae to Caesalpinieae. Both Detarieae and Caesalpinia are treated here sensu lato. Cercidium and Parkinsonia are treated as separate taxa until new biosystematic studies and combinations are made. Sclerolobium is included under the synonymy of Tachigali, and Phyllocarpus under Barnebydendron. The genus Thylacanthus is considered of doubtful introduction. Geographic range area in Argentina is expanded for of Zuccagnia punctata and Parkinsonia aculeata. Barnebydendron, Brodriguesia, Ecuadendron, Orphanodendron and Pomaria are treated jointly for the first time for South America. In addition, keys to tribes and genera, generic descriptions, updated bibliography, iconography, remarks, distribution, nomenclatural types, representative specimens, utilization and illustrations for some species are included. darwiniana.2.1.96|The carpological records of edible plant resources exploited within the last 4000 years were recovered from various archaeological sites located in different environmental zones, in southern Mendoza, Argentina. This analysis was performed considering the local environmental heterogeneity and the Optimal Foraging Theory, to determine whether the records are consistent with a model of resource intensification proposed for southern Mendoza from the study of lithic matherials and archaeofauna. This study allowed to contextualize the archaeobotanical information, to discuss previous ideas regarding the intensification processes in the region, and to explore new lines of evidence in central and western Argentina.

23223888|The aim of this work was to study the growth form of Leptochloa chloridiformis (Hack.) Parodi. In this perennial species branching occurs mainly from the axillar buds of the innovation zone. This branching system generates a caespitose plant, in which the connections between structural units are short rhizomes. According to their positions, these connections present different tendencies in relation to the structural disarticulation. In some plants branching in the long internodes zone may occur due to environmental changes. El objetivo de este trabajo fue analizar la forma de crecimiento de Leptochloa chloridiformis (Hack.) Parodi. En esta especie perenne la ramificacin ocurre principalmente a travs de yemas axilares presentes en la zona de innovacin. Este sistema de ramificacin genera una planta cespitosa, en la cual las conexiones entre unidades estructurales son rizomas cortos. Dependiendo de su posicin estas conexiones muestran diferentes tendencias en relacin a la desarticulacin estructural. En algunas plantas se observ ramificacin en la zona de entrenudos largos posiblemente debido a cambios ambientales relacionados con las distintas estaciones.

23216484|This contribution reports the results of a 16 months study of a burned grassland. Changes in species composition and in the dynamics of various aboveground compartments, net aerial primary productivity, plant mortality, rates of litter fall, and dissapearance of dead material are given. The study site was located in Sierra de la Ventana (38 6 Lat. S, 61 56 Long. WG) which is elevated several hundred meters above the Pampas of Argentina. The environmental setting of the grassland as well as the meteorological conditions before and after the fire are also discussed. In the first year after the fire plant diversity increased, the biomass of certain successional and exotic dicots also increased and the pathways of dead organic flux to the ground changed from a sequence of live  standing dead  litter to live  litter. However, with the reestablishment of climax species plant diversity decreased, successional and exotic dicots decreased in importance, dead organic matter accumulate and the pathway organic flux returned to the pattern that was characteristic before the fire.

23612306|Schinopsis lorentzii and S. marginata are closely related species that have been mainly differentiated by the shape, apex and color of the folioles, and also by their physiographical and altitudinal distribution. Nevertheless, these characters are intermediate and confusing between both species. In order to evaluate whether S. lorentzii and S. marginata can be differentiated on a morphological basis, the relationships among 89 specimens of both species were studied. A matrix of 29 morphological characters was analyzed by clustering and ordination methods. Both the dendrogram and the distribution of specimens in the Principal Components Analysis suggest that the limit between both species is not clear and none of the morphological characters are useful to differentiate them. We conclude that the morphological variations are related to altitudinal gradients and, consequently, S. marginata is placed under the synonymy of S. lorentzii (syn. nov.). The species is described and illustrated. A lectotype for Loxopterigium lorentzii is designated. Sin embargo, estos caracteres resultan intermedios y confusos entre ambas especies. Con el objetivo de evaluar si ambos taxones pueden ser diferenciados a partir de caracteres morfolgicos, se estudiaron las relaciones entre 89 ejemplares de ambas especies. Se analiz una matriz de 29 caracteres morfolgicos por mtodos de agrupamiento y ordenacin. Tanto el dendrograma como la distribucin de los ejemplares en el anlisis de componentes principales sugieren que no existe un lmite preciso entre ambos taxones y ninguno de los caracteres morfolgicos son tiles para diferenciarlos. Concluimos que las variaciones morfolgicas estn vinculadas al gradiente altitudinal, por lo que se incluye a S. marginata bajo la sinonimia de S. lorentzii (syn. nov.). 23222515|Observations on the caulinar histology in Dioscorea multiflora (Dioscoreaceae). Dioscorea multiflora Griseb. is a shrubby dioecious vine with vigorous multiannual monopodial shoots. A SEM and optic microscopic study on certain aspects of the caulinar histology and the cellular composition of the xylem is presented. Epidermal glandular trichomes, actinocytic stomata and endodermis in the form of a cristalliferous sheath, are the most important anatomical characters in the cortex. Note-worthy cellular elements in the vascular system are: long and wide metaxylematic vessels, with simple circular pits, scalariform-reticulate perforation plates with 24-64 bars and lignified tertiary helical wall sculpture - cited for the first time in Dioscorea - vasicentric tracheids in axial series around the vessels, with thickening bands interconnected by strands or second order framework; fiber-tracheids in the intervessel tissue and libriform fibers, commonly septate, in the nodal sourroundings. At the nodes, xylem glomeruli consist of tracheary tortuous elements: the vessels are composed of whether simple or irregular, dichotomized branched and anastomosed elements, with terminal or intercalary simple perforation plates; also multiperforated, foraminate plates occur. Nevertheless the bulk of the tissue is formed by irregularly interwoven tracheids with circular bordered pits located in the tracheid walls outside an inner reticulate layer, with the inner circular pit aperture between the bars of this reticulum. Also are present immature tracheid elements in cellular series, with the characteristically lignified walls of biphasic deposition. The present data on the structure of certain xylem elements might suggest a phylogenetical relation with ferns. A functional interpretation of several sylem features could be performed: starch rich parenchyma of the medullary rays, parenchyma distribution in the sourroundings of tracheid-sheathed vessels (mechanical flexibility), unusually wide vessels (efficiency), vascular and vasicentric tracheids (safety), helical sculpture in vessels (mechanic support) and phloem disposition in separated strands (tissue regeneration); all of them suggest similar functional features already reviewed in woody dicotyledoneous vines and lianas. The caulinar histology of Dioscorea, clasically referred as unique in monocotyledons, could be interpreted as an adaptative shift related to the biological form.

23213858|The author presents a synopsis of the large Leguminous genus Adesmia and discusses its systematic position, accepting for it the tribe Adesmieae (Benth.) Hutchinson. The number of accepted species is about 228. A taxonomic history of the genus is presented with particular emphasis on the former attempts to subdivide it. Then the geographic distribution of Aaesmia as a Southamerican extratropical, very natural, group, is considered as a whole (distribution map, Fig. 1). The center of polymorphism is the Chilean-Argentine Cordillera, but the whole area ranges from Peru and South Brazil to Tierra del Fuego. In the following chapter phylogenetic ideas are exposed with the aim of explaining the development of the numerous species groups. After a brief characterization of the genus, its species are grouped into two subgenera and fortyfive series with a key for their identification. This key intends to give a clue for the understanding of the whole genus. Then follow the diagnoses of each series, the fixation of their types and a critical list of the species (with their synonvms in parentheses) pertaining to every series. The number of species per series varies between one and thirty eight ( 42, Microphyllae), this last series comprises spiny shrubs and has not yet been monographed. A list of dubious or excluded species, a bibliography, some illustrations and an alphabetical index conplete the paper. In most series references to earlier works are given, particularly to the contributions I-VI of the author (Lilloa and Darwiniana, 1949-1966), in which detailed descriptions and illustrations on 74 species of this genus are to be seen. Further papers of this kind are announced. The novelties described in the present synopsis are: A. ciliata Vog. var. graminetorum nov. var. (pbg. 507, fig. 3). A. calycicomosa n. sp. (pg. 533). A. boelckeana n. sp. (pg. 542. fig. 6). A. microcalyx Phil. var. calvescens nov. var. (pg. 539). A. littoralis n. sp. (pg. 548).
23218066|The development of the pericarp, in particular the exocarp of two species of Rhynchospora, R. corymbosa (L.) Britton and R. scutellata Gris, was studied, in order to investigate the origin of the silica bodies and its relation with the interposed wall between them and the outer periclinal epidermal wall. The silica body, made up of a platform and a cone arises as a thickening on the inner periclinal wall growing centripetally into the cell. Later on, it is isolated from the protoplast by an intracellular, transverse septum, which is not originated by mitosis and could be confused with the inner periclinal cell wall. The septum contains cellulose, lignin, cutin and silica. In this way the exocarp becomes secondarily bistratified and therefore results in an outer layer with tannin compounds (which is not the true epidermis) and an inner layer with silica bodies. Atypical silica deposits form dendriform bodies and prismatic rods, filling the lumen of sclereids of mesocarp and cellulosic fusiform cells of endocarp, respectively. Scanning electron micrographs of achenes are given. Different stages of development of the pericarp studied with the light microscope are illustrated.
23224223|A taxonomic revision of the genus Hypseocharis in Argentina is presented. Two species are considered: Hypseocharis tridentata and H. pimpinellifolia. H. corydalifolia is considered a synonym of H. pimpinellifolia. Flowers and fruits of H. tridentata are described for the first time. This species has a whorl of 5 alternate stamens and a schizocarpic fruit breaking away as five dehiscent mericarps with 1-few seeds per locule. These characters differ substantially from the original description of the genus, which indicated 15 stamens in two whorls and a capsule with loculicidal dehiscence containing many seeds. H. pimpinellifolia has a wide distribution in cloud grasslands, high Andean grasslands and Puna environments between 2000 and 4200 m in Jujuy, Salta, Tucumn, Catamarca and La Rioja provinces. H. tridentata is a relatively rare species, restricted to a narrow belt of cloud grasslands above the Andean alder forest between 2500 and 3200 m in Jujuy, Salta and Tucumn provinces. La flor y el fruto de H. tridentata son descriptos por primera vez. Esta especie posee un ciclo de 5 estambres alternos y un fruto esquizocrpico que se separa en 5 mericarpos dehiscentes con 1 a pocas semillas por lculo. Estos caracteres difieren sustancialmente de la descripcin original del gnero, que indicaba 15 estambres en dos ciclos y una cpsula loculicida conteniendo numerosas semillas. 23213798|Las bases foliares en varias especies del gnero Adesmia se desarrollan en filopodios persistentes y a veces endurecidos. En la Serie Capitellatae estos filopodios se prolongan a considerable distancia del nudo y estn vascularizados por 3 haces fundamentales, caractersticos de muchos gneros de Papilionoideas. El lmite de estas bases de la hoja est marcado externamente por una articulacin donde se produce la fusin vascular y aparicin de 5 haces, punto que indica el comienzo del pecoloraquis. De este modo se puede distinguir un filopodio, un pseudopecolo o prolongacin del filopodio y un pecolo. En algunas especies arbustivas de hojas caducas de la Serie Microphyllae, se observ la presencia, en la base de los pecolos, de pulvinos que en estos casos estn poco desarrollados. La zona de absicin de la hoja se produce por debajo de estos pulvinos, de modo que los pecolos caen junto con ellos. In some species of Adesmia there is a development of the leafbases into persistent and sometimes hard structures called "hypopodium". In species of the series Capitellatae this hypopodium is prolongued to a considerable distance from the node and it is vascularized by 3 main bundles, as in many genera of the Papilionoideae. An articulation delimits externally the leafbase-petiole zone, where the vascular anastomosis occurs. Above this point 5 bundles appear instead of 3, indicating the beginning of the petiolerachis of the plant. In this way it is possible to distinguish a hypopodium, its prolongation in a pseudopetiole and a petiole. Some shrubby species with non-persistent leaves of the series Microphyllae present, at the petiole base, a zone resembling a pulvinus, which is not well developed in these species of Adesmia. The abscission zone of the leaf occurs below the pulvinus and the petiole falls with it.
23217329|Propagation and dispersion of Tripogandra diuretica (Commelinaceae) in the Paran Delta - River Plate region. Tripogandra diuretica (C. Martius) Handlos, is a penennial herb with rooting decumbent stems. It is known from Central and Southern Brazil, Paraguay, Bolivia, Argentina and Uruguay, thriving generally in wet or swampy soils near rivers and streams. In Argentina it reaches the Marginal Forest of Punta Lara near La Plata city. In the region under study its propagation is only vegetative, through pieces of stem that root easily at the nodes. The species is autogamous, but the developing fruits never reach maturity, falling precociously from the plant. Near the tropics it begins to flower in Summer (December), but the flowering period near Buenos Aires is in Autumn (end of March to June). The shorter photoperiod and lower temperature of this season, may be the cause of the premature abscission of the fruits. Its dispersion to this southern area was perhaps possible by cuttings carried by the periodic swelling of the Paran and Uruguay Rivers.

23223857|Extranuptial nectaries are found in almost all flowers of the studied species, and always on the calyx. Their shape varies from patelliform to cupuliform. Considering their anatomy, three groups of cells are distinguished: (i) a secretory stratum of cylindrical, elongated cells, resting upon (ii) a layer or a single basal cell, and (iii) a reduced group of subepidermic cells. Based upon these characteristics, the terms simple and complex are proposed to describe extranuptial nectaries with one or with many basal cells respectively. This anatomic nectary feature is maintained within the level of species, thus becoming a significant specific character. The two types of extranuptial nectaries can be found within a genus, constituting an important character to differentiate similar species. Se hallaron nectarios extranupciales en casi todas las flores de las especies estudiadas y siempre en el cliz. Sus formas variaron de pateliformes a cupuliformes. Teniendo en cuenta su anatoma se distinguen tres grupos de clulas: (i) un estrato secretor de clulas cilndricas y alargadas que se disponen sobre (ii) una capa de clulas basales o una nica clula basal y (iii) un grupo reducido de clulas subepidrmicas. Basndose en estas caractersticas se propone la denominacin simple y complejo para describir los nectarios extranupciales con una o muchas clulas basales respectivamente. Esta caracterstica anatmica se mantiene a nivel especfico, constituyendo un carcter descriptivo importante. Los dos tipos de nectario extranupcial pueden encontrarse en un mismo gnero, resultando un carcter que permite diferenciar especies similares.

23215714|En este trabajo se presenta el anlisis palinolgico de casi la totalidad de especies de Malvastrum y Acaulimalva (Malvaceae). En Acaulimalva el dimetro de los granos de polen, el nmero de aberturas y su posicin en la superficie del grano es bastante uniforme en todas las especies, de modo que no es posible identificarlas en base a la morfologa del polen. En este gnero hay especies con granos de 4 a 10 aberturas, que son semejantes a los de Acaulimalva. In this paper we present the pollen analysis of almost the whole of Malvastrum and Acaulimalva species (Malvaceae). Acaulimalva, a genus proposed by Krapovickas (Darwiniana, 19:10. 1974), comprises the acaulescent species included up to now in the genus Malvastrum. The study of the pollen morphology allowed to establish schemes of variation which are different for both genera. In Acaulimalva the diameter of the pollen grains, the number of apertures and their position on the surface of the grain is rather uniform in all species, thus it is not possible to identify them based on the pollen morphology. On the contrary, in Malvastrum these polynological characters show such variation that it is possible to separate the species in groups quite distinctible. In this genus there are species with grains of 4 to 10 apertures, which are similar to those of Acaulimalva. Nevertheless it is possible to distinguish them because in Malvastrum the bacules are always much thicker and the base of the spines is always of larger diameter than in those of Acaulimalva grains.

23218070|The systematic anatomical leaf characters of the Argentine species of the tribe Sophoreae (excluding Adesmia) have been studied.
