23227930|The breeding system, fruit set, seed set, floral visitors and pollination of Cologania broussonetii were studied. Four pollination treatments were applied: autogamy, geitonogamy, xenogamy, and natural pollination (flowers exposed to pollinators). The frequency of visits was recorded, and pollen grains deposited per stigma on bagged (self pollen deposition) and exposed flowers were counted. The results indicate that this species is self-compatible and autogamus. A small number of low quality fruits and seeds (lowest mass and germination capability) were obtained by spontaneous self-pollination. When fruits obtained by natural pollination were analyzed, a specific pattern of seed formation was detected: ovules were successively fertilized from the apical to the basal portion of the ovary. However, no pattern was observed for seed abortion. The frequency of visits of possible pollinators (species of Bombus) was very low. The number of pollen grains per stigma was similar on bagged and exposed flowers. Nevertheless, the comparison of quantity and quality of fruits and seeds obtained by natural and autonomous self-pollination suggests that the visits of pollinators contribute to increase the quality of seeds (higher mass and germination capability). Se estudi el sistema reproductivo, la produccin natural de frutos y semillas, y el papel de los polinizadores en Cologania broussonetii. Se realizaron cuatro cruzamientos controlados: autopolinizacin espontnea, autopolinizacin manual, polinizacin cruzada y polinizacin natural (flores expuestas a los polinizadores). Se registr la frecuencia de visitas de los polinizadores y se cuantific el nmero de granos de polen depositados en el estigma de flores expuestas a los polinizadores y en flores aisladas (autodepsito de polen). Los resultados obtenidos indican que esta especie es autocompatible y autgama. Los frutos y semillas obtenidos por autopolinizacin espontnea fueron pocos y los de menor calidad (menor masa y germinabilidad). Al analizar los frutos producidos por polinizacin abierta se infiere que las semillas se forman siguiendo un patrn determinado: primero son fertilizados los vulos prximos al estigma y por ltimo los ms alejados. Sin embargo, no se encontr un patrn en el aborto de semillas dentro del fruto. La frecuencia de visita de los posibles polinizadores (especies de Bombus) fue muy baja. El nmero de granos de polen depositados en el estigma fue muy similar entre flores expuestas a los visitantes y aqullas aisladas. Sin embargo, al comparar la calidad y cantidad de frutos y semillas obtenidos por polinizacin abierta y por autopolinizacin se infiere que la visita de los polinizadores es importante para la produccin de semillas de mejor calidad (mayor masa y germinabilidad).
23226690|Lake Planetario is an urban recreational lake that suffered a Microcystis aeruginosa bloom in March 1999. At the same time the birds and fishes that inhabited the lake died, probably affected by microcystin, hepatotoxin that some strains of Miycrocyistis produce. The City of Buenos Aires requested Aguas Argentinas to restore the lake. Restoration tasks included treatment of sediments and pumping of water from a brackish aquifer. For one year, monthly samples were taken with a phytoplankton net, the qualitative and quantitative composition of the phytoplankton were studied, and physicochemical data were collected. The structure and composition of the phytoplankton were studied and revealed that due to the turbulence caused by the pumping of water, the Cyanophyta were controlled and phytoplankton diversity increased significantly. Chlorophyta dominated during spring, Cyanophyta during fall and Bacillariophyta during summer and winter. The change in conductivity provided a favourable environment for new taxa to colonize the lake, with representatives of taxa typical for brackish water. El lago del Planetario es un lago recreativo urbano localizado en la ciudad de Buenos Aires, Argentina. En marzo de 1999 se produjo una floracin de Microcystis aeruginosa. Al mismo tiempo los peces y aves que habitaban el lago murieron, probablemente afectados por microcystina, una hepatotoxina que producen algunas cepas de Microcystis. El Gobierno de la Ciudad de Buenos Aires encomend la restauracin del lago a Aguas Argentinas. Las tareas de restauracin incluyeron el tratamiento de los sedimentos y el bombeo de agua de una napa salobre. Durante un ao se tomaron muestras mensuaes con una red de fitoplancton, se estudi su composicin cuantitativa y cualitativa, y se tomaron medidas de factores fsicoqumicos. Debido a la turbulencia causada por el bombeo de agua, el crecimiento de las Cyanophyta fue controlado y la diversidad fitoplanctnica aument significativamente. Las Chlorophyta dominaron durante la primavera, las Cyanophyta durante el otoo y las Bacillariophyta en verano e invierno. El cambio en la conductividad provey condiciones favorables para que nuevos taxones, tpicos de ambientes salobres, colonizaran el lago.
23227992|Thirty-seven South American species representing seven sections of Solanum subgen. Leptostemonum were analyzed. Andromonoecious as well as hermaphrodite species were considered. The length and width of their fruits was measured, and the number of seeds per fruit was counted. Medial cross sections of fresh, ripe fruits were observed with a stereoscopic microscope and illustrated. Six placentation patterns and three types of seeds were described. A relationship among seed number, fruit size, fruit color and sexual system was detected by means of statistical analysis. These results suggest that andromonoecy affects fruit size and placentation patterns, in order to contain a higher number of seeds per fruit. Se analizaron 37 especies sudamericanas pertenecientes a siete secciones de Solanum subgen. Leptostemonum. Fueron consideradas tanto especies andromonoicas como hermafroditas. Se midi el ancho y el largo de sus frutos y se cont el nmero de semillas por fruto. Se estudiaron bajo lupa y se ilustraron cortes por la zona media de frutos frescos maduros. Se describieron seis patrones de placentacin y tres tipos de semillas. Mediante anlisis estadstico, se detect una relacin entre el nmero de semillas, el tamao del fruto, el color del fruto y el sistema sexual. Estos resultados sugieren que la andromonoecia afecta al tamao del fruto y su patrn de placentacin, para contener un mayor nmero de semillas.
23218935|Karyotypes and chromosomes meiotic behavior of Festuca pallescens (Poaceae). Chromosome counts were carried out in samples from 24 populations of Festuca pallescens (St.-Yves) L. Parodi and F. pallescens var. scabra (St.-Yves) L. Parodi. It was found 2n = 42 chromosomes. The karyotypes of both varieties are very similar, uniform and composed by metacentric chromosomes. Also secondary constrictions were observed in 6 out of 21 homomorphic pairs. The number of secondary constrictions almost coincided with that of nucleoli found in resting nuclei, where a maximum of 14 nucleoli was counted. Meiosis was regular and 21 bivalents were found in 97% of the pollen mother cells examined. Pairing at metaphase I and the chromosome arrangement in homomorphic pairs suggests that this species is an allohexaploid.
23213873|Two new species of Lycopodium are described for the NW of Argentina: L. sanctaebarbarae and L. sotae. Data on the geographic and altitudinal distribution and on affinities are given. Finally the author adds a key for the determination of all species of that genus which grow in the NW area of that country.
23218952|Embryological studies in Buddleja (Buddlejaceae). II: Embryogeny. The development of the embryo is studied in two species of Buddleja: B. stachyoides Cham, et Schldl. and B. tubiflora Benth. The main conclusions are: Embryogeny follows the Veronica Variation of the Onagrad type. According with the Souges System, the mode of development may be designated as belonging to the First Grand Division, Serie A, Megarchtype IV. This pattern is present in most of the Scrophulariaceae representatives. The hypothesis suggesting close affinities between Buddleja and some genera of Scrophulariaceae seems to be strengthened once more by the peculiarities of their embryogeny.
23217332|Karyological studies in Compositae III. Meiotic or mitotic chromosome numbers and observations were made in 14 taxa belonging to 6 different genera of Eupatorieae, Heliantheae and Senecioneae. The numbers include counts in 10 taxa that so far had never been investigated cytologically or had a previous count which is different from the one reported here. These are as follows: Eupatorium angustifolium (H.B.K.) Spr. (n = ca. 90), E. arbutifolium Benth. (n = 42), E. arnottianum Griseb. (n = 10 + ca. 7 IB), E. baccharoides H.B.K. (n = ca. 42), E. candolleanum Hook. et Arn. (n = 10), E. elegans H.B.K. (n = 43), E. tweedianum Hook. et Arn. (n = 10), Bidens exigua Sherff (2n = 24), Flourensia macroligulata Seeligmann (n = 18), Wedelia kerri N. E. Brown (n = 23) and Werneria pygmaea Gillies ex Hook. et Arn. (n = 50). B chromosomes were observed in two species of Eupatorium. E. arnottianum had up to 7 Bs, which were heteropycnotic at first metaphase (Fig. 1a) and showed difficulties in separating at first anaphase. Subsequently bridges and their remains were seen at the end of this stage (Fig. 1b). In E. hecatanthum (DC.) Baker there were 0-2 Bs in different cells of a single plant; these would form a bivalent in diakinesis (Fig. 2b) or be in single dose as univalents (Fig. 2a, c) or absent (Fig. 2d). These results indicate that the Bs are somatically unstable. The Colombian species Eupatorium arbutifolium (Fig. 3c) (n = 42), E. baccharoides (Fig. 1f) (n = ca. 42) and E. elegans (Fig. 1c) (n = 43) would have hyperoctoploid level if one assumes x = 10. The presence of B chromosomes in diploid species of Eupatorium (with n = 10) could have facilitated the process of increase of the chromosome number to hyperploid levels after translocation to the Bs of genetic material from A chromosomes. The number n = ca. 90 established for Eupatorium angustifolium (Fig. 3a) is by far the highest polyploid in the genus and one of the highest for the Compositae.
23612305|This work confirms the presence of Imperata tenuis in Argentina, and includes an illustration, reference material, a map showing its geographic distribution in southern South America, and a key to identify the species of Imperata that inhabit Argentina. En este trabajo se confirma la presencia de Imperata tenuis en Argentina. Se presenta una ilustracin, material de referencia y un mapa de su distribucin geogrfica en el sur de Sudamrica. Se incluye una clave para identificar las especies del gnero Imperata presentes en la Argentina.
23225109|The neotropical genus Liabum is reincorporated to Argentina (province of Salta) with the first record of L. acuminatum. This new record extends the distribution of the genus Liabum to 23 S. L. acuminatum is described and illustrated. In addition, a map of distribution of Liabum and L. acuminatum, and a key to differentiate the members of the tribe Liabeae of Argentina are provided. Se reincorpora el gnero neotropical Liabum a la flora argentina (provincia de Salta) con el primer registro de L. acuminatum para este pas. El nuevo registro extiende el lmite meridional de distribucin del gnero Liabum hasta los 23 S. L. acuminatum se describe e ilustra. Adems se provee un mapa de distribucin de Liabum y L. acuminatum, y una clave para diferenciar los miembros de la tribu Liabeae de Argentina.
23223258|Elymus hitchcocki Davidse and E. scabrifolius (Dll) J.H. Hunz. are regarded as species distantly related and not as conspecific as considered recently by several authors. A number of morphological, ecological, distributional and chromosomal differences, which were pointed out more than 30 years ago, are stressed. A new status and combination is proposed for the latter taxon.

23223205|The Argentine species of Alstroemeria L. are studied and a brief nomenclatural history of the genera is given. The taxonomic treatment includes keys to species, descriptions, synonyms, illustrations, ecological observations and distribution maps. At present, 10 taxa are recognized and treated for Argentina: Alstroemeria andina Phil. subsp. venustula Ehr. Bayer, A. apertiflora Baker, A. aurea Graham, A. bakeri Pax, A. isabellana Herb., A. patagonica Phil., A. presliana Herb., A. pseudospathulata Ehr. Bayer, A. psittacina Lehm. and A. pygmaea Herb. The probable occurrence in our country of A. spathulata C. Presl and A. pallida Graham is pointed out. A. inodora Herb. is a new synonym of A. psittacina Lehm. A. bakeri and the name A. hassleriana are here lectotypified. Morphological data of taxonomical value are discussed. The most important interespecific differences are found in the floral characters. The presence or absence of resupination in the leaf, the plant height and the characteristics of the inflorescence are also of importance.
23227933|A Microcystis aeruginosa bloom occurred in the Planetario Lake (Parque Tres de Febrero, Ciudad Autnoma de Buenos Aires, Argentina) that led to the restoration of the lake. Before and after the restoration (since October 1999 to September 2000), samples were collected to assess changes in the phytoplankton structure. The genus Interfilum (Chlorococcales, Chlorophyta) was recorded in the samples for February and May 2000 for the first time in America. Furthermore, it is a new variety for science: I. paradoxum var regulare var. nov. El Lago del Planetario (Parque Tres de Febrero, Ciudad Autnoma de Buenos Aires, Argentina) sufri una floracin de Microcystis aeruginosa que condujo a un proceso de recuperacin. Se realiz el estudio del fitoplancton antes y despus del proceso de recuperacin, a lo largo de un ao (octubre 1999 a septiembre 2000). En las muestras de los meses de febrero y mayo de 2000 se registr por primera vez para Amrica la presencia de Interfilum (Chlorococcales, Chlorophyta). El taxn descripto es adems una nueva variedad para la ciencia: I. paradoxum var regulare var. nov.
